Liṅgapurāṇa, 
namo rudrāya haraye brahmaṇe paramātmane 
pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityantakāriṇe ।। 

nārado abhyarcya śaileśe śaṅkaraṃ saṅgameśvare 
hiraṇyagarbhe svarlīne hy avimukte mahālaye ।। 

raudre goprekṣake caiva śreṣṭhe pāśupate tathā 
vighneśvare ca kedāre tathā gomāyukeśvare ।। 

hiraṇyagarbhe candreśe īśānye ca triviṣṭape 
śukreśvare yathānyāyaṃ naimiṣaṃ prayayau muniḥ ।। 

naimiṣeyāstadā dṛṣṭvā nāradaṃ hṛṣṭamānasāḥ 
samabhyarcyāsanaṃ tasmai tadyogyaṃ samakalpayan ।। 

so api hṛṣṭo munivarair dattaṃ bheje tadāsanam 
sampūjyamāno munibhiḥ sukhāsīno varāsane ।। 

cakre kathāṃ vicitrārthāṃ liṅgamāhātmyamāśritām 
etasminnevakāle tu sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ svayam ।। 

jagāma naimiṣaṃ dhīmān praṇāmārthaṃ tapasvinām 
tasmai sāma ca pūjāṃ ca yathāvaccakrire tadā ।। 

naimiṣeyāstu śiṣyāya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya tu 
atha teṣāṃ purāṇasya śuśrūṣā samapadyata ।। 

dṛṣṭvā tam ativiśvastaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ romaharṣaṇam 
apṛcchaṃśca tataḥ sūtam ṛṣiṃ sarve tapodhanāḥ ।। 

purāṇasaṃhitāṃ puṇyāṃ liṅgamāhātmyasaṃyutām 
tvayā sūta mahābuddhe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ ।। 

upāsitaḥ purāṇārthaṃ labdhā tasmācca saṃhitā 
tasmādbhavantaṃ pṛcchāmaḥ sūta paurāṇikottamam ।। 

purāṇasaṃhitāṃ divyāṃ liṅgamāhātmyasaṃyutām 
nārado apyasya devasya rudrasya paramātmanaḥ ।। 

kṣetrāṇyāsādya cābhyarcya liṅgāni munipuṅgavaḥ 
iha saṃnihitaḥ śrīmān nārado brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। 

bhavabhakto bhavāṃścaiva vayaṃ vai nāradastathā 
asyāgrato muneḥ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। 

saphalaṃ sādhitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavatā viditaṃ bhavet 
evamuktaḥ sa hṛṣṭātmā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।। 

abhivādyāgrato dhīmān nāradaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutam 
naimiṣeyāṃśca puṇyātmā purāṇaṃ vyājahāra saḥ ।। 

namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca janārdanam 
munīśvaraṃ tathā vyāsaṃ vaktuṃ liṅgaṃ smarāmyaham ।। 

śabdaṃ brahmatanuṃ sākṣāc chabdabrahmaprakāśakam 
varṇāvayavam avyaktalakṣaṇaṃ bahudhā sthitam ।। 

akārokāramakāraṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ parātparam 
oṅkārarūpam ṛgvaktraṃ samajihvāsamanvitam ।। 

yajurvedamahāgrīvam atharvahṛdayaṃ vibhum 
pradhānapuruṣātītaṃ pralayotpattivarjitam ।। 

tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam 
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram ।। 

pradhānāvayavaṃ vyāpya saptadhādhiṣṭhitaṃ kramāt 
punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva ṣaḍviṃśakam ajodbhavam ।। 

sargapratiṣṭhāsaṃhāralīlārthaṃ liṅgarūpiṇam 
praṇamya ca yathānyāyaṃ vakṣye liṅgodbhavaṃ śubham ।। 

iti śrīlaiṅge mahāpurāṇe prathamo adhyāyaḥ

īśānakalpavṛttāntam adhikṛtya mahātmanā 
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgam uttamam ।। 

granthakoṭipramāṇaṃ tu śatakoṭipravistare 
caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte vyāsaiḥ sarvāntareṣu vai ।। 

vyasteṣṭā daśadhā caiva brahmādau dvāparādiṣu 
liṅgamekādaśaṃ proktaṃ mayā vyāsācchrutaṃ ca tat ।। 

asyaikādaśasāhasre granthamānamiha dvijāḥ 
tasmātsaṃkṣepato vakṣye na śrutaṃ vistareṇa yat ।। 

caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte kṛṣṇadvaipāyanena tu 
atraikādaśasāhasraiḥ kathito liṅgasambhavaḥ ।। 

sargaḥ prādhānikaḥ paścāt prākṛto vaikṛtāni ca 
aṇḍasyāsya ca sambhūtir aṇḍasyāvaraṇāṣṭakam ।। 

aṇḍodbhavatvaṃ śarvasya rajoguṇasamāśrayāt 
viṣṇutvaṃ kālarudratvaṃ śayanaṃ cāpsu tasya ca ।। 

prajāpatīnāṃ sargaś ca pṛthivyuddharaṇaṃ tathā 
brahmaṇaś ca divārātram āyuṣo gaṇanaṃ punaḥ ।। 

savanaṃ brahmaṇaścaiva yugakalpaś ca tasya tu 
divyaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ varṣam ārṣaṃ vai dhrauvyameva ca ।। 

pitryaṃ pitṝṇāṃ sambhūtir dharmaścāśramiṇāṃ tathā 
avṛddhirjagato bhūyo devyāḥ śaktyudbhavastathā ।। 

strīpumbhāvo viriñcasya sargo mithunasambhavaḥ 
ākhyāṣṭakaṃ hi rudrasya kathitaṃ rodanāntare ।। 

brahmaviṣṇuvivādaś ca punarliṅgasya sambhavaḥ 
śilādasya tapaścaiva vṛtrārerdarśanaṃ tathā ।। 

prārthanā yonijasyātha durlabhatvaṃ sutasya tu 
śilādaśakrasaṃvādaḥ padmayonitvameva ca ।। 

bhavasya darśanaṃ caiva tiṣyeṣvācāryaśiṣyayoḥ 
vyāsāvatārāś ca tathā kalpamanvantarāṇi ca ।। 

kalpatvaṃ caiva kalpānām ākhyābhedeṣvanukramāt 
kalpeṣu kalpe vārāhe vārāhatvaṃ hares tathā ।। 

meghavāhanakalpasya vṛttāntaṃ rudragauravam 
punarliṅgodbhavaścaiva ṛṣimadhye pinākinaḥ ।। 

liṅgasyārādhanaṃ snānavidhānaṃ śaucalakṣaṇam 
vārāṇasyāś ca māhātmyaṃ kṣetramāhātmyavarṇanam ।। 

bhuvi rudrālayānāṃ tu saṃkhyā viṣṇorgṛhasya ca 
antarikṣe tathāṇḍe asmin devāyatanavarṇanam ।। 

dakṣasya patanaṃ bhūmau punaḥ svārociṣe antare 
dakṣaśāpaś ca dakṣasya śāpamokṣastathaiva ca ।। 

kailāsavarṇanaṃ caiva yogaḥ pāśupatas tathā 
caturyugapramāṇaṃ ca yugadharmaḥ suvistaraḥ ।। 

saṃdhyāṃśakapramāṇaṃ ca saṃdhyāvṛttaṃ bhavasya ca 
śmaśānanilayaścaiva candrarekhāsamudbhavaḥ ।। 

udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasyātha putrotpādanameva ca 
maithunātiprasaṅgena vināśo jagatāṃ bhayam ।। 

śāpaḥ satyā kṛto devānpurā viṣṇuṃ ca pālitam 
śukrotsargastu rudrasya gāṅgeyodbhava eva ca ।। 

grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu snāpya liṅgaṃ phalaṃ tathā 
kṣubdhadhī ca vivādaś ca dadhīcopendrayos tathā ।। 

utpattirnandināmnā tu devadevasya śūlinaḥ 
pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ paśupāśavicāraṇā ।। 

pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ nivṛttyadhikṛtā tathā 
vasiṣṭhatanayotpattir vāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 

munīnāṃ vaṃśavistāro rājñāṃ śaktervināśanam 
daurātmyaṃ kauśikasyātha surabherbandhanaṃ tathā ।। 

sutaśoko vasiṣṭhasya arundhatyāḥ pralāpanam 
snuṣāyāḥ preṣaṇaṃ caiva garbhasthasya vacas tathā ।। 

parāśarasyāvatāro vyāsasya ca śukasya ca 
vināśo rākṣasānāṃ ca kṛto vai śaktisūnunā ।। 

devatāparamārthaṃ tu vijñānaṃ ca prasādataḥ 
purāṇakaraṇaṃ caiva pulastyasyājñayā guroḥ ।। 

bhuvanānāṃ pramāṇaṃ ca grahāṇāṃ jyotiṣāṃ gatiḥ 
jīvacchrāddhavidhānaṃ ca śrāddhārhāḥ śrāddhameva ca ।। 

nāndīśrāddhavidhānaṃ ca tathādhyayanalakṣaṇam 
pañcayajñaprabhāvaś ca pañcayajñavidhis tathā ।। 

rajasvalānāṃ vṛttiś ca vṛttyā putraviśiṣṭatā 
maithunasya vidhiścaiva prativarṇamanukramāt ।। 

bhojyābhojyavidhānaṃ ca sarveṣāmeva varṇinām 
prāyaścittam aśeṣasya pratyekaṃ caiva vistarāt ।। 

narakāṇāṃ svarūpaṃ ca daṇḍaḥ karmānurūpataḥ 
svarginārakiṇāṃ puṃsāṃ cihnaṃ janmāntareṣu ca ।। 

nānāvidhāni dānāni pretarājapuraṃ tathā 
kalpaṃ pañcākṣarasyātha rudramāhātmyameva ca ।। 

vṛtrendrayormahāyuddhaṃ viśvarūpavimardanam 
śvetasya mṛtyoḥ saṃvādaḥ śvetārthe kālanāśanam ।। 

devadāruvane śambhoḥ praveśaḥ śaṃkarasya tu 
sudarśanasya cākhyānaṃ kramasaṃnyāsalakṣaṇam ।। 

śraddhāsādhyo atha rudrastu kathitaṃ brahmaṇā tadā 
madhunā kaiṭabhenaiva purā hṛtagatervibhoḥ ।। 

brahmaṇaḥ paramaṃ jñānam ādātuṃ mīnatā hareḥ 
sarvāvasthāsu viṣṇoś ca jananaṃ līlayaiva tu ।। 

rudraprasādādviṣṇoś ca jiṣṇoścaiva tu sambhavaḥ 
manthānadhāraṇārthāya hareḥ kūrmatvamevaca ।। 

saṃkarṣaṇasya cotpattiḥ kauśikyāś ca punarbhavaḥ 
yadūnāṃ caiva sambhūtir yādavatvaṃ hareḥ svayam ।। 

bhojarājasya daurātmyaṃ mātulasya harervibhoḥ 
bālabhāve hareḥ krīḍā putrārthaṃ śaṃkarārcanam ।। 

nārasya ca tathotpattiḥ kapāle vaiṣṇavāddharāt 
bhūbhāranigrahārthe tu rudrasyārādhanaṃ hareḥ ।। 

vainyena pṛthunā bhūmeḥ purā dohapravartanam 
devāsure purā labdho bhṛguśāpaś ca viṣṇunā ।। 

kṛṣṇatve dvārakāyāṃ tu nilayo mādhavasya tu 
labdho hitāya śāpastu durvāsasyānanāddhareḥ ।। 

vṛṣṇyandhakavināśāya śāpaḥ piṇḍāravāsinām 
erakasya tathotpattis tomarasyodbhavas tathā ।। 

erakālābhato anyonyaṃ vivāde vṛṣṇivigrahaḥ 
līlayā caiva kṛṣṇena svakulasya ca saṃhṛtiḥ ।। 

erakāstrabalenaiva gamanaṃ svecchayaiva tu 
brahmaṇaścaiva mokṣasya vijñānaṃ tu suvistaram ।। 

purāndhakāgnidakṣāṇāṃ śakrebhamṛgarūpiṇām 
madanasyādidevasya brahmaṇaś cāmarāriṇām ।। 

halāhalasya daityasya kṛtāvajñā pinākinā 
jālaṃdharavadhaścaiva sudarśanasamudbhavaḥ ।। 

viṣṇorvarāyudhāvāptis tathā rudrasya ceṣṭitam 
tathānyāni ca rudrasya caritāni sahasraśaḥ ।। 

hareḥ pitāmahasyātha śakrasya ca mahātmanaḥ 
prabhāvānubhavaścaiva śivalokasya varṇanam ।। 

bhūmau rudrasya lokaṃ ca pātāle hāṭakeśvaram 
tapasāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva dvijānāṃ vaibhavaṃ tathā ।। 

ādhikyaṃ sarvamūrtīnāṃ liṅgamūrterviśeṣataḥ 
liṅge asminnānupūrvyeṇa vistareṇānukīrtyate ।। 

etajjñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepaṃ kīrtayettu yaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

aliṅgo liṅgamūlaṃ tu avyaktaṃ liṅgamucyate 
aliṅgaḥ śiva ityukto liṅgaṃ śaivamiti smṛtam ।। 

pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhurliṅgamuttamam 
gandhavarṇarasairhīnaṃ śabdasparśādivarjitam ।। 

aguṇaṃ dhruvamakṣayyam aliṅgaṃ śivalakṣaṇam 
gandhavarṇarasairyuktaṃ śabdasparśādilakṣaṇam ।। 

jagadyoniṃ mahābhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vigraho jagatāṃ liṅgam aliṅgād abhavatsvayam ।। 

saptadhācāṣṭadhā caiva tathaikādaśadhā punaḥ 
liṅgānyaliṅgasya tathā māyayā vitatāni tu ।। 

tebhyaḥ pradhānadevānāṃ trayamāsīcchivātmakam 
ekasmāttriṣvabhūdviśvam ekena parirakṣitam ।। 

ekenaiva hṛtaṃ viśvaṃ vyāptaṃ tvevaṃ śivena tu 
aliṅgaṃ caiva liṅgaṃ ca liṅgāliṅgāni mūrtayaḥ ।। 

yathāvatkathitāścaiva tasmādbrahma svayaṃ jagat 
aliṅgī bhagavān bījī sa eva parameśvaraḥ ।। 

bījaṃ yoniś ca nirbījaṃ nirbījo bījamucyate 
bījayonipradhānānām ātmākhyā vartate tviha ।। 

paramātmā munirbrahma nityabuddhasvabhāvataḥ 
viśuddho ayaṃ tathā rudraḥ purāṇe śiva ucyate ।। 

śivena dṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ śaivī samabhavaddvijāḥ 
sargādau sā guṇairyuktā purāvyaktā svabhāvataḥ ।। 

avyaktādiviśeṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ tasyāḥ samucchritam 
viśvadhātrī tvajākhyā ca śaivī sā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā ।। 

tāmajāṃ lohitāṃ śuklāṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ bahuprajām 
janitrīmanuśete sma juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm ।। 

tāmevājāmajo anyastu bhuktabhogāṃ jahāti ca 
ajā janitrī jagatāṃ sājena samadhiṣṭhitā ।। 

prādurbabhūva sa mahān puruṣādhiṣṭhitasya ca 
ajājñayā pradhānasya sargakāle guṇais tribhiḥ ।। 

sisṛkṣayā codyamānaḥ praviśyāvyaktamavyayam 
vyaktasṛṣṭiṃ vikurute cātmanādhiṣṭhito mahān ।। 

mahatastu tathā vṛttiḥ saṃkalpādhyavasāyikā 
mahatas triguṇas tasmād ahaṃkāro rajo adhikaḥ ।। 

tenaiva cāvṛtaḥ samyag ahaṃkāras tamo adhikaḥ 
mahato bhūtatanmātraṃ sargakṛdvai babhūva ca ।। 

ahaṃkārācchabdamātraṃ tasmādākāśamavyayam 
saśabdamāvṛṇotpaścād ākāśaṃ śabdakāraṇam ।। 

tanmātrādbhūtasargaś ca dvijāstvevaṃ prakīrtitaḥ 
sparśamātraṃ tathākāśāt tasmādvāyur mahānmune ।। 

tasmācca rūpamātraṃ tu tato agniśca rasastataḥ 
rasādāpaḥ śubhāstābhyo gandhamātraṃ dharā tataḥ ।। 

āvṛṇoddhi tathākāśaṃ sparśamātraṃ dvijottamāḥ 
āvṛṇodrūpamātraṃ tu vāyurvāti kriyātmakaḥ ।। 

āvṛṇodrasamātraṃ vai devaḥ sākṣādvibhāvasuḥ 
āvṛṇvānā gandhamātram āpaḥ sarvarasātmikāḥ ।। 

kṣmā sā pañcaguṇā tasmād ekonā rasasambhavāḥ 
triguṇo bhagavānvahnir dviguṇaḥ sparśasambhavaḥ ।। 

avakāśastato deva ekamātrastu niṣkalaḥ 
tanmātrādbhūtasargaś ca vijñeyaś ca parasparam ।। 

vaikārikaḥ sāttviko vai yugapatsampravartate 
sargas tathāpyahaṃkārād evamatra prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

pañca buddhīndriyāṇyasya pañca karmendriyāṇi tu 
śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ manaścaivobhayātmakam ।। 

mahadādiviśeṣāntā hy aṇḍamutpādayanti ca 
jalabudbudavattasmād avatīrṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। 

sa eva bhagavān rudro viṣṇurviśvagataḥ prabhuḥ 
tasminnaṇḍe tvime lokā antarviśvamidaṃ jagat ।। 

aṇḍaṃ daśaguṇenaiva vāriṇā prāvṛtaṃ bahiḥ 
āpo daśaguṇenaiva tadbāhyastejasā vṛtāḥ ।। 

tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunā vṛtam 
vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ ।। 

ākāśenāvṛto vāyur ahaṃkāreṇa śabdajaḥ 
mahatā śabdaheturvai pradhānenāvṛtaḥ svayam ।। 

saptāṇḍāvaraṇānyāhus tasyātmā kamalāsanaḥ 
koṭikoṭiyutānyatra cāṇḍāni kathitāni tu ।। 

tatratatra caturvaktrā brahmāṇo harayo bhavāḥ 
sṛṣṭāḥ pradhānena tadā labdhvā śambhostu saṃnidhim ।। 

layaścaiva tathānyonyam āndyantam iti kīrtitam 
sargasya pratisargasya sthiteḥ kartā maheśvaraḥ ।। 

sarge ca rajasā yuktaḥ sattvasthaḥ pratipālane 
pratisarge tamodriktaḥ sa eva trividhaḥ kramāt ।। 

ādikartā ca bhūtānāṃ saṃhartā paripālakaḥ 
tasmānmaheśvaro devo brahmaṇo adhipatiḥ śivaḥ ।। 

sadāśivo bhavo viṣṇur brahmā sarvātmako yataḥ 
ekadaṇḍe tathā lokā ime kartā pitāmahaḥ ।। 

prākṛtaḥ kathitastveṣa puruṣādhiṣṭhito mayā 
sargaś cābuddhipūrvastu dvijāḥ prāthamikaḥ śubhaḥ ।। 

atha prāthamikasyeha yaḥ kālastadahaḥ smṛtam 
sargasya tādṛśī rātriḥ prākṛtasya samāsataḥ ।। 

divā sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute rajanyāṃ pralayaṃ vibhuḥ 
aupacārikamasyaitad ahorātraṃ na vidyate ।। 

divā vikṛtayaḥ sarve vikārā viśvadevatāḥ 
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve tiṣṭhantyanye maharṣayaḥ ।। 

rātrau sarve pralīyante niśānte sambhavanti ca 
ahastu tasya vaikalpo rātristādṛgvidhā smṛtā ।। 

caturyugasahasrānte manavastu caturdaśa 
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vatsarāṇāṃ kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

tāvacchatī ca vai saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca kṛtasya tu 
triśatī dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā caikaśatī kramāt ।। 

aṃśakaḥ ṣaṭśataṃ tasmāt kṛtasaṃdhyāṃśakaṃ vinā 
tridvyekasāhasramito vinā saṃdhyāṃśakena tu ।। 

tretādvāparatiṣyāṇāṃ kṛtasya kathayāmi vaḥ 
nimeṣapañcadaśakā kāṣṭhā svasthasya suvratāḥ ।। 

martyasya cākṣṇostasyāś ca tatas triṃśatikā kalā 
kalātriṃśatiko viprā muhūrta iti kalpitaḥ ।। 

muhūrtapañcadaśikā rajanī tādṛśaṃ tvahaḥ 
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। 

kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī 
triṃśadye mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। 

śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭyā cāpyadhikāni vai 
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ।। 

mānuṣeṇaiva mānena varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet 
pitṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātānīha tāni vai ।। 

daśa vai dvyadhikā māsāḥ pitṛsaṃkhyeha saṃsmṛtā 
laukikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

etaddivyamahorātram iti laiṅge atra paṭhyate 
divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। 

ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam 
ete rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte viśeṣataḥ ।। 

triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi divyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ 
mānuṣaṃ tu śataṃ viprā divyamāsāstrayastu te ।। 

daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
trīṇi varṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni tu ।। 

divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ 
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇataḥ ।। 

triṃśadanyāni varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ 
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। 

anyāni navatīścaiva dhrauvaḥ saṃvatsarastu saḥ 
ṣaṭtriṃśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। 

varṣāṇāṃ tacchataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
trīṇyeva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। 

ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṃkhyātāni tu saṃkhyayā 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ ।। 

divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṃkhyāprakalpanam 
pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate ।। 

dvāparaśca kaliścaiva yugānyetāni suvratāḥ 
atha saṃvatsarā dṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ ।। 

kṛtasyādyasya viprendrā divyamānena kīrtitam 
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāsaṃś caturdaśa ca saṃkhyayā ।। 

catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi tathānyāni kṛtaṃ yugam 
tathā daśasahasrāṇāṃ varṣāṇāṃ śatasaṃkhyayā ।। 

aśītiś ca sahasrāṇi kālastretāyugasya ca 
saptaiva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। 

viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālastu dvāparasya ca 
tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ trīṇi saṃkhyayā ।। 

ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi kālaḥ kaliyugasya tu 
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kāla ṛte saṃdhyāṃśakātsmṛtaḥ ।। 

niyutānyeva ṣaṭtriṃśan niraṃśāni tu tāni vai 
catvāriṃśattathā trīṇi niyutānīha saṃkhyayā ।। 

viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi saṃdhyāṃśaś ca caturyugaḥ 
evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ ।। 

kṛtatretādiyuktānāṃ manorantaramucyate 
manvantarasya saṃkhyā ca varṣāgreṇa prakīrtitā ।। 

triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ 
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu ।। 

viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālo ayam adhikaṃ vinā 
manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā laiṅge asminkīrtitā dvijāḥ ।। 

caturyugasya ca tathā varṣasaṃkhyā prakīrtitā 
caturyugasahasraṃ vai kalpaścaiko dvijottamāḥ ।। 

niśānte sṛjate lokān naśyante niśi jantavaḥ 
tatra vaimānikānāṃ tu aṣṭāviṃśatikoṭayaḥ ।। 

manvantareṣu vai saṃkhyā sāntareṣu yathātathā 
trīṇi koṭiśatānyāsan koṭyo dvinavatis tathā ।। 

kalpe atīte tu vai viprāḥ sahasrāṇāṃ tu saptatiḥ 
punastathāṣṭasāhasraṃ sarvatraiva samāsataḥ ।। 

kalpāvasānikāṃstyaktvā pralaye samupasthite 
maharlokāt prayāntyete janalokaṃ janāstataḥ ।। 

koṭīnāṃ dve sahasre tu aṣṭau koṭiśatāni tu 
dviṣaṣṭiś ca tathā koṭyo niyutāni ca saptatiḥ ।। 

kalpārdhasaṃkhyā divyā vai kalpamevaṃ tu kalpayet 
kalpānāṃ vai sahasraṃ tu varṣamekamajasya tu ।। 

varṣāṇāmaṣṭasāhasraṃ brāhmaṃ vai brahmaṇo yugam 
savanaṃ yugasāhasraṃ sarvadevodbhavasya tu ।। 

savanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu trividhaṃ triguṇaṃ tathā 
brahmaṇastu tathā proktaḥ kālaḥ kālātmanaḥ prabho ।। 

bhavodbhavastapaścaiva bhavyo rambhaḥ kratuḥ punaḥ 
ṛturvahnirhavyavāhaḥ sāvitraḥ śuddha eva ca ।। 

uśikaḥ kuśikaścaiva gāndhāro munisattamāḥ 
ṛṣabhaś ca tathā ṣaḍjo majjālīyaś ca madhyamaḥ ।। 

vairājo vai niṣādaś ca mukhyo vai meghavāhanaḥ 
pañcamaścitrakaścaiva ākūtir jñāna eva ca ।। 

manaḥ sudarśo bṛṃhaś ca tathā vai śvetalohitaḥ 
raktaś ca pītavāsāś ca asitaḥ sarvarūpakaḥ ।। 

evaṃ kalpāstu saṃkhyātā brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ 
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi kalpānāṃ munisattamāḥ ।। 

gatāni tāvaccheṣāṇi aharniśyāni vai punaḥ 
parānte vai vikārāṇi vikāraṃ yānti viśvataḥ ।। 

vikārasya śivasyājñāvaśenaiva tu saṃhṛtiḥ 
saṃhṛte tu vikāre ca pradhāne cātmani sthite ।। 

sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau 
guṇānāṃ caiva vaiṣamye viprāḥ sṛṣṭiriti smṛtā ।। 

sāmye layo guṇānāṃ tu tayorheturmaheśvaraḥ 
līlayā devadevena sargāstvīdṛgvidhāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। 

asaṃkhyātāś ca saṃkṣepāt pradhānād anvadhiṣṭhitāt 
asaṃkhyātāś ca kalpākhyā hy asaṃkhyātāḥ pitāmahāḥ ।। 

harayaścāpyasaṃkhyātās tv eka eva maheśvaraḥ 
pradhānādipravṛttāni līlayā prākṛtāni tu ।। 

guṇātmikā ca tadvṛttis tasya devasya vai tridhā 
aprākṛtasya tasyādir madhyāntaṃ nāsti cātmanaḥ ।। 

pitāmahasyātha paraḥ parārdhadvayasaṃmitaḥ 
divā sṛṣṭaṃ tu yatsarvaṃ niśi naśyati cāsya tat ।। 

bhūrbhuvaḥsvarmahastatra naśyate cordhvato na ca 
rātrau caikārṇave brahmā naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। 

suṣvāpāmbhasi yastasmān nārāyaṇa iti smṛtaḥ 
śarvaryante prabuddho vai dṛṣṭvā śūnyaṃ carācaram ।। 

sraṣṭuṃ tadā matiṃ cakre brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ 
udakairāplutāṃ kṣmāṃ tāṃ samādāya sanātanaḥ ।। 

pūrvavatsthāpayāmāsa vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ 
nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca pūrvavaccākarotprabhuḥ ।। 

kṛtvā dharāṃ prayatnena nimnonnativivarjitām 
dharāyāṃ so acinotsarvān girīn dagdhān purāgninā ।। 

bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat 
sraṣṭuṃ ca bhagavāṃścakre tadā sraṣṭā punarmatim ।। 

yadā sraṣṭuṃ matiṃ cakre mohaścāsīnmahātmanaḥ 
dvijāś ca buddhipūrvaṃ tu brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। 

tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ 
avidyā pañcadhā hyeṣā prādurbhūtā svayambhuvaḥ ।। 

avidyayā munergrastaḥ sargo mukhya iti smṛtaḥ 
asādhaka iti smṛtvā sargo mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। 

abhyamanyata so anyaṃ vai nagā mukhyodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tridhā kaṇṭho munestasya dhyāyato vai hyavartata ।। 

prathamaṃ tasya vai jajñe tiryaksroto mahātmanaḥ 
ūrdhvasrotaḥ parastasya sāttvikaḥ sa iti smṛtaḥ ।। 

arvāksroto anugrahaś ca tathā bhūtādikaḥ punaḥ 
brahmaṇo mahatastvādyo dvitīyo bhautikas tathā ।। 

sargastṛtīyaścaindriyas turīyo mukhya ucyate 
tiryagyonyaḥ pañcamastu ṣaṣṭho daivika ucyate ।। 

saptamo mānuṣo viprā aṣṭamo anugrahaḥ smṛtaḥ 
navamaścaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvime ।। 

purastādasṛjaddevaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā 
sanātanaṃ muniśreṣṭhā naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param ।। 

marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum 
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so asṛjadyogavidyayā ।। 

navaite brahmaṇaḥ putrā brahmajñā brāhmaṇottamāḥ 
brahmavādina evaite brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

saṃkalpaścaiva dharmaś ca hy adharmo dharmasaṃnidhiḥ 
dvādaśaiva prajāstvetā brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। 

ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca sasarjādau sanātanaḥ 
tāvūrdhvaretasau divyau cāgrajau brahmavādinau ।। 

kumārau brahmaṇas tulyau sarvajñau sarvabhāvinau 
vakṣye bhāryākulaṃ teṣāṃ munīnāmagrajanmanām ।। 

samāsato muniśreṣṭhāḥ prajāsambhūtimeva ca 
śatarūpāṃ tu vai rājñīṃ virājamasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। 

svāyambhuvāttu vai rājñī śatarūpā tvayonijā 
lebhe putradvayaṃ puṇyā tathā kanyādvayaṃ ca sā ।। 

uttānapādo hyavaro dhīmāñjyeṣṭhaḥ priyavrataḥ 
jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā tvākūtiḥ prasūtiścānujā smṛtā ।। 

upayeme tadākūtiṃ rucirnāma prajāpatiḥ 
prasūtiṃ bhagavāndakṣo lokadhātrīṃ ca yoginīm ।। 

dakṣiṇāsahitaṃ yajñam ākūtiḥ suṣuve tathā 
dakṣiṇā janayāmāsa divyā dvādaśa putrikāḥ ।। 

prasūtiḥ suṣuve dakṣāc caturviṃśatikanyakāḥ 
śraddhāṃ lakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ puṣṭiṃ tuṣṭiṃ medhāṃ kriyāṃ tathā ।। 

buddhiṃ lajjāṃ vapuḥśāntiṃ siddhiṃ kīrtiṃ mahātapāḥ 
khyātiṃ śāntiṃ ca sambhūtiṃ smṛtiṃ prītiṃ kṣamāṃ tathā ।। 

saṃnatiṃ cānasūyāṃ ca ūrjāṃ svāhāṃ surāraṇim 
svadhāṃ caiva mahābhāgāṃ pradadau ca yathākramam ।। 

śraddhādyāścaiva kīrtyantās trayodaśa sudārikāḥ 
dharmaṃ prajāpatiṃ jagmuḥ patiṃ paramadurlabhāḥ ।। 

upayeme bhṛgurdhīmān khyātiṃ tāṃ bhārgavāraṇim 
sambhūtiṃ ca marīcistu smṛtiṃ caivāṅgirā muniḥ ।। 

prītiṃ pulastyaḥ puṇyātmā kṣamāṃ tāṃ pulaho muniḥ 
kratuś ca saṃnatiṃ dhīmān atristāṃ cānasūyakām ।। 

ūrjāṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavān variṣṭho vārijekṣaṇām 
vibhāvasus tathā svāhāṃ svadhāṃ vai pitaras tathā ।। 

putrīkṛtā satī yā sā mānasī śivasambhavā 
dakṣeṇa jagatāṃ dhātrī rudramevāsthitā patim ।। 

ardhanārīśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sargādau kanakāṇḍajaḥ 
vibhajasveti cāhādau yadā jātā tadābhavat ।। 

tasyāścaivāṃśajāḥ sarvāḥ striyastribhuvane tathā 
ekādaśāvidhā rudrās tasya cāṃśodbhavās tathā ।। 

strīliṅgamakhilaṃ sā vai puṃliṅgaṃ nīlalohitaḥ 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān brahmā dakṣamālokya suvratām ।। 

bhajasva dhātrīṃ jagatāṃ mamāpi ca tavāpi ca 
punnāmno narakāttrāti iti putrītvihoktitaḥ ।। 

praśastā tava kānteyaṃ syāt putrī viśvamātṛkā 
tasmāt putrī satī nāmnā tavaiṣā ca bhaviṣyati ।। 

evamuktastadā dakṣo niyogādbrahmaṇo muniḥ 
labdhvā putrīṃ dadau sākṣāt satīṃ rudrāya sādaram ।। 

dharmasya patnyaḥ śraddhādyāḥ kīrtitā vai trayodaśa 
tāsu dharmaprajāṃ vakṣye yathākramamanuttamam ।। 

kāmo darpo atha niyamaḥ saṃtoṣo lobha eva ca 
śrutastu daṇḍaḥ samayo bodhaścaiva mahādyutiḥ ।। 

apramādaś ca vinayo vyavasāyo dvijottamāḥ 
kṣemaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaścaiva dharmaputrāś ca tāsu vai ।। 

dharmasya vai kriyāyāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ samaya eva ca 
apramādas tathā bodho buddherdharmasya tau sutau ।। 

tasmātpañcadaśaivaite tāsu dharmātmajāstviha 
bhṛgupatnī ca suṣuve khyātirviṣṇoḥ priyāṃ śriyam ।। 

dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ merorjāmātarau sutau 
prabhūtirnāma yā patnī marīceḥ suṣuve sutau ।। 

pūrṇamāsaṃ tu mārīcaṃ tataḥ kanyācatuṣṭayam 
tuṣṭirjyeṣṭhā ca vai dṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣiścāpacitis tathā ।। 

kṣamā ca suṣuve putrān putrīṃ ca pulahācchubhām 
kardamaṃ ca varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ munisattamāḥ ।। 

tathā kanakapītāṃ sa pīvarīṃ pṛthivīsamām 
prītyāṃ pulastyaś ca tathā janayāmāsa vai sutān ।। 

dattorṇaṃ vedabāhuṃ ca putrīṃ cānyāṃ dṛṣadvatīm 
putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ saṃnatiḥ suṣuve śubhā ।। 

kratostu bhāryā sarve te vālakhilyā iti śrutāḥ 
sinīvālīṃ kuhūṃ caiva rākāṃ cānumatiṃ tathā ।। 

smṛtiś ca suṣuve patnī muneścāṅgirasas tathā 
labdhānubhāvamagniṃ ca kīrtimantaṃ ca suvratā ।। 

atrerbhāryānasūyā vai suṣuve ṣaṭprajāstu yāḥ 
tāsvekā kanyakā nāmnā śrutiḥ sā sūnupañcakam ।। 

satyanetro munirbhavyo mūrtirāpaḥ śanaiścaraḥ 
somaś ca vai śrutiḥ ṣaṣṭhī pañcātreyāstu sūnavaḥ ।। 

ūrjā vasiṣṭhādvai lebhe sutāṃś ca sutavatsalā 
jyāyasī puṇḍarīkākṣān vāsiṣṭhān varalocanā ।। 

rajaḥ suhotro bāhuś ca savanaścānaghas tathā 
sutapāḥ śukra ityete munervai sapta sūnavaḥ ।। 

yaścābhimānī bhagavān bhavātmā paitāmaho vahnirasuḥ prajānām 
svāhā ca tasmātsuṣuve sutānāṃ trayaṃ trayāṇāṃ jagatāṃ hitāya ।। 

pavamānaḥ pāvakaś ca śuciragniś ca te smṛtāḥ 
nirmathyaḥ pavamānastu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

śuciḥ saurastu vijñeyaḥ svāhāputrāstrayastu te 
putraiḥ pautraistvihaiteṣāṃ saṃkhyā saṃkṣepataḥ smṛtā ।। 

visṛjya saptakaṃ cādau catvāriṃśannavaiva ca 
ityete vahnayaḥ proktāḥ praṇīyante adhvareṣu ca ।। 

sarve tapasvinastvete sarve vratabhṛtaḥ smṛtāḥ 
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve sarve rudrātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

ayajvānaś ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ prītimānasāḥ 
agniṣvāttāś ca yajvānaḥ śeṣā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

menāṃ tu mānasīṃ teṣāṃ janayāmāsa vai svadhā 
agniṣvāttātmajā menā mānasī lokaviśrutā ।। 

asūta menā mainākaṃ krauñcaṃ tasyānujāmumām 
gaṅgāṃ haimavatīṃ jajñe bhavāṅgāśleṣapāvanīm ।। 

dharaṇīṃ janayāmāsa mānasīṃ yajñayājinīm 
svadhā sā merurājasya patnī padmasamānanā ।। 

pitaro amṛtapāḥ proktās teṣāṃ caiveha vistaraḥ 
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca kulaṃ sarvaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ tatsuvistaram ।। 

vadāmi pṛthagadhyāyasaṃsthitaṃ vastadūrdhvataḥ 
dākṣāyaṇī satī yātā pārśvaṃ rudrasya pārvatī ।। 

paścāddakṣaṃ vinindyaiṣā patiṃ lebhe bhavaṃ tathā 
tāṃ dhyātvā vyasṛjadrudrān anekānnīlalohitaḥ ।। 

ātmanastu samānsarvān sarvalokanamaskṛtān 
yācito muniśārdūlā brahmaṇā prahasan kṣaṇāt ।। 

taistu saṃchāditaṃ sarvaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ jagat 
tāndṛṣṭvā vividhān rudrān nirmalānnīlalohitān ।। 

jarāmaraṇanirmuktān prāha rudrānpitāmahaḥ 
namo astu vo mahādevās trinetrā nīlalohitāḥ ।। 

sarvajñāḥ sarvagā dīrghā hrasvā vāmanakāḥ śubhāḥ 
hiraṇyakeśā dṛṣṭighnā nityā buddhāś ca nirmalāḥ ।। 

nirdvaṃdvā vītarāgāś ca viśvātmāno bhavātmajāḥ 
evaṃ stutvā tadā rudrān rudraṃ cāha bhavaṃ śivam 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tadā bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ ।। 

namo astu te mahādeva prajā nārhasi śaṃkara 
mṛtyuhīnā vibho sraṣṭuṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ sṛja prabho ।। 

tatastamāha bhagavān na hi me tādṛśī sthitiḥ 
sa tvaṃ sṛja yathākāmaṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ prajāḥ prabho ।। 

labdhvā sasarja sakalaṃ śaṃkarāccaturānanaḥ 
jarāmaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ jagadetaccarācaram ।। 

śaṃkaro api tadā rudrair nivṛttātmā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ 
sthāṇutvaṃ tasya vai viprāḥ śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 

niṣkalasyātmanaḥ śambhoḥ svecchādhṛtaśarīriṇaḥ 
śaṃ rudraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ karoti ghṛṇayā yataḥ ।। 

śaṃkaraścāprayatnena tadātmā yogavidyayā 
vairāgyasthaṃ viraktasya vimuktiryacchamucyate ।। 

aṇostu viṣayatyāgaḥ saṃsārabhayataḥ kramāt 
vairāgyājjāyate puṃso virāgo darśanāntare ।। 

vimukhyo viguṇatyāgo vijñānasyāvicārataḥ 
tasya cāsya ca saṃdhānaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ śaṃkarādiha 
sa eva śaṃkaraḥ sākṣāt pinākī nīlalohitaḥ ।। 

ye śaṃkarāśritāḥ sarve mucyante te na saṃśayaḥ 
na gacchantyeva narakaṃ pāpiṣṭhā api dāruṇam ।। 

āśritāḥ śaṃkaraṃ tasmāt prāpnuvanti ca śāśvatam 
māyāntāścaiva ghorādyā hy aṣṭaviṃśatireva ca ।। 

koṭayo narakāṇāṃ tu pacyante tāsu pāpinaḥ 
anāśritāḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śaṃkaraṃ nīlalohitam ।। 

āśrayaṃ sarvabhūtānām avyayaṃ jagatāṃ patim 
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam ।। 

tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam 
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram ।। 

kena gacchanti narakaṃ narāḥ kena mahāmate 
karmaṇākarmaṇā vāpi śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। 

rahasyaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi bhavasyāmitatejasaḥ 
prabhāvaṃ śaṃkarasyādyaṃ saṃkṣepātsarvadarśinaḥ ।। 

yoginaḥ sarvatattvajñāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ ।। 

prāṇāyāmādibhiścāṣṭasādhanaiḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ।। 

karuṇādiguṇopetāḥ kṛtvāpi vividhāni te 
karmāṇi narakaṃ svargaṃ gacchantyeva svakarmaṇā ।। 

prasādājjāyate jñānaṃ jñānādyogaḥ pravartate 
yogena jāyate muktiḥ prasādādakhilaṃ tataḥ ।। 

prasādād yadi vijñānaṃ svarūpaṃ vaktumarhasi 
divyaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva yogaṃ yogavidāṃ vara ।। 

kathaṃ karoti bhagavān cintayā rahitaḥ śivaḥ 
prasādaṃ yogamārgeṇa kasminkāle nṛṇāṃ vibhuḥ ।। 

devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ saṃnidhau purā 
śailādinā tu kathitaṃ śṛṇvantu brahmasūnave ।। 

vyāsāvatārāṇi tathā dvāparānte ca suvratāḥ 
yogācāryāvatārāṇi tathā tiṣye tu śūlinaḥ ।। 

tatratatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāś catvāraḥ śamabhājanāḥ 
praśiṣyā bahavasteṣāṃ prasīdatyevamīśvaraḥ ।। 

evaṃ kramāgataṃ jñānaṃ mukhādeva nṛṇāṃ vibhoḥ 
vaiśyāntaṃ brāhmaṇādyaṃ hi ghṛṇayā cānurūpataḥ ।। 

dvāpare dvāpare vyāsāḥ ke vai kutrāntareṣu vai 
kalpeṣu kasminkalpe no vaktumarhasi cātra tān ।। 

śṛṇvantu kalpe vārāhe dvijā vaivasvatāntare 
vyāsāṃś ca sāmprataṃ rudrāṃs tathā sarvāntareṣu vai ।। 

vedānāṃ ca purāṇānāṃ tathā jñānapradarśakān 
yathākramaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāvarteṣu sāmpratam ।। 

kratuḥ satyo bhārgavaś ca aṅgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ 
mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmān vasiṣṭho munipuṃgavaḥ ।। 

sārasvatastridhāmā ca trivṛto munipuṃgavaḥ 
śatatejāḥ svayaṃdharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ ।। 

tarakṣuścāruṇirdhīmāṃs tathā devaḥ kṛtaṃjayaḥ 
ṛtaṃjayo bharadvājo gautamaḥ kavisattamaḥ ।। 

vācaśravā muniḥ sākṣāt tathā śuṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ 
tṛṇabindur munī rūkṣaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ ।। 

jātūkarṇyo hariḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ 
vyāsāstvete ca śṛṇvantu kalau yogeśvarān kramāt ।। 

asaṃkhyātā hi kalpeṣu vibhoḥ sarvāntareṣu ca 
kalau rudrāvatārāṇāṃ vyāsānāṃ kila gauravāt ।। 

vaivasvatāntare kalpe vārāhe ye ca tān punaḥ 
avatārān pravakṣyāmi tathā sarvāntareṣu vai ।। 

manvantarāṇi vārāhe vaktumarhasi sāmpratam 
tathaiva cordhvakalpeṣu siddhānvaivasvatāntare ।। 

manuḥ svāyambhuvastvādyas tataḥ svārociṣo dvijāḥ 
uttamastāmasaścaiva raivatāścākṣuṣas tathā ।। 

vaivasvataś ca sāvarṇir dharmaḥ sāvarṇikaḥ punaḥ 
piśaṅgaścāpiśaṅgābhaḥ śabalo varṇakas tathā ।। 

aukārāntā akārādyā manavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
śvetaḥ pāṇḍus tathā raktas tāmraḥ pītaśca kāpilaḥ ।। 

kṛṣṇaḥ śyāmas tathā dhūmraḥ sudhūmraś ca dvijottamāḥ 
apiśaṅgaḥ piśaṅgaś ca trivarṇaḥ śabalas tathā ।। 

kālaṃdhurastu kathitā varṇato manavaḥ śubhāḥ 
nāmato varṇataścaiva varṇataḥ punareva ca ।। 

svarātmānaḥ samākhyātāś cāntareśāḥ samāsataḥ 
vaivasvata ṛkārastu manuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sureśvaraḥ ।। 

saptamastasya vakṣyāmi yugāvarteṣu yoginaḥ 
samatīteṣu kalpeṣu tathā cānāgateṣu vai ।। 

vārāhaḥ sāmprataṃ jñeyaḥ saptamāntarataḥ kramāt 
yogāvatārāṃś ca vibhoḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃtatis tathā ।। 

samprekṣya sarvakāleṣu tathāvarteṣu yoginām 
ādye śvetaḥ kalau rudraḥ sutāro madanas tathā ।। 

suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇaścaiva lokākṣir munisattamāḥ 
jaigīṣavyo mahātejā bhagavān dadhivāhanaḥ ।। 

ṛṣabhaś ca munirdhīmān ugraścātriḥ subālakaḥ 
gautamaścātha bhagavān sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।। 

vedaśīrṣaś ca gokarṇo guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍabhṛt 
jaṭāmālyaṭṭahāsaś ca dāruko lāṅgalī tathā ।। 

mahākāyamuniḥ śūlī daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ svayam 
sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśo jagadguruḥ ।। 

vaivasvate antare samyak proktā hi paramātmanaḥ 
yogācāryāvatārā ye sarvāvarteṣu suvratāḥ ।। 

vyāsāścaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā dvāpare dvāpare tvime 
yogeśvarāṇāṃ catvāraḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyekamavyayāḥ ।। 

śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaṇḍī ca śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ 
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃs tathā ।। 

viśokaśca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ 
sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdamo duratikramaḥ ।। 

sanakaś ca sanandaś ca prabhuryaś ca sanātanaḥ 
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā ।। 

śaṅkhapād vairajaścaiva meghaḥ sārasvatas tathā 
suvāhano muniśreṣṭho meghavāho mahādyutiḥ ।। 

kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcaśikho muniḥ 
vālkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ ।। 

parāśaraś ca gargaś ca bhārgavaścāṅgirās tathā 
balabandhur nirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ ।। 

lambodaraś ca lambaśca lambākṣo lambakeśakaḥ 
sarvajñaḥ samabuddhiś ca sādhyaḥ sarvastathaiva ca ।। 

sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajās tathā 
atrir devasadaścaiva śravaṇo atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ 
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ ।। 

kaśyapo apyuśanāścaiva cyavano atha bṛhaspatiḥ 
utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ ।। 

vācaśravāḥ sudhīkaśca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ 
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo logākṣiḥ kuthumis tathā ।। 

sumanturbarbarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikaṃdharaḥ 
plakṣo dālbhyāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gopanas tathā ।। 

bhallāvī madhupiṅgaśca śvetaketustaponidhiḥ 
uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca ।। 

śālihotro agniveśaśca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ 
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kumbhaścaiva pravāhakaḥ ।। 

ulūko vidyutaścaiva maṇḍūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ 
akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca ।। 

kuśikaścaiva garbhaś ca mitraḥ kauruṣya eva ca 
śiṣyāstvete mahātmānaḥ sarvāvarteṣu yoginām ।। 

vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ 
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।। 

śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāścaiteṣāṃ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ 
prāpya pāśupataṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ ।। 

devādayaḥ piśācāntāḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
teṣāṃ patitvātsarveśo bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

tena praṇīto rudreṇa paśūnāṃ patinā dvijāḥ 
yogaḥ pāśupato jñeyaḥ parāvaravibhūtaye ।। 

saṃkṣepataḥ pravakṣyāmi yogasthānāni sāmpratam 
kalpitāni śivenaiva hitāya jagatāṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

galādadho vitastyā yan nābherupari cottamam 
yogasthānamadho nābher āvartaṃ madhyamaṃ bhruvoḥ ।। 

sarvārthajñānaniṣpattir ātmano yoga ucyate 
ekāgratā bhaveccaiva sarvadā tatprasādataḥ ।। 

prasādasya svarūpaṃ yat svasaṃvedyaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ brahmādyaiḥ kramaśo jāyate nṛṇām ।। 

yogaśabdena nirvāṇaṃ māheśaṃ padamucyate 
tasya heturṛṣerjñānaṃ jñānaṃ tasya prasādataḥ ।। 

jñānena nirdahetpāpaṃ nirudhya viṣayān sadā 
niruddhendriyavṛttestu yogasiddhirbhaviṣyati ।। 

yogo nirodho vṛtteṣu cittasya dvijasattamāḥ 
sādhanānyaṣṭadhā cāsya kathitānīha siddhaye ।। 

yamastu prathamaḥ prokto dvitīyo niyamas tathā 
tṛtīyamāsanaṃ proktaṃ prāṇāyāmastataḥ param ।। 

pratyāhāraṃ pañcamo vai dhāraṇā ca tataḥ parā 
dhyānaṃ saptamamityuktaṃ samādhistvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

tapasyuparamaścaiva yama ityabhidhīyate 
ahiṃsā prathamo hetur yamasya yamināṃ varāḥ ।। 

satyamasteyamaparaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahau 
niyamasyāpi vai mūlaṃ yama eva na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ātmavat sarvabhūtānāṃ hitāyaiva pravartanam 
ahiṃsaiṣā samākhyātā yā cātmajñānasiddhidā ।। 

dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ cānumitaṃ svānubhūtaṃ yathārthataḥ 
kathanaṃ satyamityuktaṃ parapīḍāvivarjitam ।। 

nāślīlaṃ kīrtayedevaṃ brāhmaṇānāmiti śrutiḥ 
paradoṣān parijñāya na vadediti cāparam ।। 

anādānaṃ parasvānām āpadyapi vicārataḥ 
manasā karmaṇā vācā tadasteyaṃ samāsataḥ ।। 

maithunasyāpravṛttirhi manovākkāyakarmaṇā 
brahmacaryamiti proktaṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।। 

iha vaikhānasānāṃ ca vidārāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
sadārāṇāṃ gṛhasthānaṃ tathaiva ca vadāmi vaḥ ।। 

svadāre vidhivatkṛtvā nivṛttiścānyataḥ sadā 
manasā karmaṇā vācā brahmacaryamiti smṛtam ।। 

medhyā svanārī sambhogaṃ kṛtvā snānaṃ samācaret 
evaṃ gṛhastho yuktātmā brahmacārī na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ahiṃsāpyevamevaiṣā dvijagurvagnipūjane 
vidhinā yādṛśī hiṃsā sā tvahiṃsā iti smṛtā ।। 

striyaḥ sadā parityājyāḥ saṅgaṃ naiva ca kārayet 
kuṇapeṣu yathā cittaṃ tathā kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

viṇmūtrotsargakāleṣu bahirbhūmau yathā matiḥ 
tathā kāryā ratau cāpi svadāre cānyataḥ kutaḥ ।। 

aṅgārasadṛśī nārī ghṛtakumbhasamaḥ pumān 
tasmānnārīṣu saṃsargaṃ dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।। 

bhogena tṛptirnaivāsti viṣayāṇāṃ vicārataḥ 
tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manasā karmaṇā girā ।। 

na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati 
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।। 

tasmāttyāgaḥ sadā kāryas tv amṛtatvāya yoginā 
avirakto yato martyo nānāyoniṣu vartate ।। 

tyāgenaivāmṛtatvaṃ hi śrutismṛtividāṃ varāḥ 
karmaṇā prajayā nāsti dravyeṇa dvijasattamāḥ ।। 

tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manovākkāyakarmaṇā 
ṛtau ṛtau nivṛttistu brahmacaryamiti smṛtam ।। 

yamāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktā niyamāṃś ca vadāmi vaḥ 
śaucamijyā tapo dānaṃ svādhyāyopasthanigrahaḥ ।। 

vratopavāsamaunaṃ ca snānaṃ ca niyamā daśa 
niyamaḥ syādanīhā ca śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapas tathā ।। 

japaḥ śivapraṇīdhānaṃ padmakādyaṃ tathāsanam 
bāhyamābhyantaraṃ proktaṃ śaucamābhyantaraṃ varam ।। 

bāhyaśaucena yuktaḥ saṃs tathā cābhyantaraṃ caret 
āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ brāhmaṃ kartavyaṃ śivapūjakaiḥ ।। 

snānaṃ vidhānataḥ samyak paścād ābhyantaraṃ caret 
ā dehāntaṃ mṛdālipya tīrthatoyeṣu sarvadā ।। 

avagāhyāpi malino hy antaḥ śaucavivarjitaḥ 
śaivalā jhaṣakā matsyāḥ sattvā matsyopajīvinaḥ ।। 

sadāvagāhya salile viśuddhāḥ kiṃ dvijottamāḥ 
tasmādābhyantaraṃ śaucaṃ sadā kāryaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। 

ātmajñānāmbhasi snātvā sakṛdālipya bhāvataḥ 
suvairāgyamṛdā śuddhaḥ śaucamevaṃ prakīrtitam ।। 

śuddhasya siddhayo dṛṣṭā naivāśuddhasya siddhayaḥ 
nyāyenāgatayā vṛttyā saṃtuṣṭo yastu suvrataḥ ।। 

saṃtoṣastasya satatam atītārthasya cāsmṛtiḥ 
cāndrāyaṇādinipuṇas tapāṃsi suśubhāni ca ।। 

svādhyāyastu japaḥ proktaḥ praṇavasya tridhā smṛtaḥ 
vācikaścādhamo mukhya upāṃśuścottamottamaḥ ।। 

mānaso vistareṇaiva kalpe pañcākṣare smṛtaḥ 
tathā śivapraṇīdhānaṃ manovākkāyakarmaṇā ।। 

śivajñānaṃ gurorbhaktir acalā supratiṣṭhitā 
nigraho hyapahṛtyāśu prasaktānīndriyāṇi ca ।। 

viṣayeṣu samāsena pratyāhāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
cittasya dhāraṇā proktā sthānabandhaḥ samāsataḥ ।। 

tasyāḥ svāsthyena dhyānaṃ ca samādhiś ca vicārataḥ 
tatraikacittatā dhyānaṃ pratyayāntaravarjitam ।। 

cidbhāsamarthamātrasya dehaśūnyamiva sthitam 
samādhiḥ sarvahetuś ca prāṇāyāma iti smṛtaḥ ।। 

prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyur yamastasya nirodhanam 
tridhā dvijairyamaḥ prokto mando madhyottamas tathā ।। 

prāṇāpānanirodhastu prāṇāyāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
prāṇāyāmasya mānaṃ tu mātrādvādaśakaṃ smṛtam ।। 

nīco dvādaśamātrastu uddhāto dvādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ 
madhyamas tu dviruddhātaś caturviṃśatimātrakaḥ ।। 

mukhyastu yastriruddhātaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśanmātra ucyate 
prasvedakampanotthānajanakaśca yathākramam ।। 

ānandodbhavayogārthaṃ nidrāghūrṇistathaiva ca 
romāñcadhvanisaṃviddhasvāṅgamoṭanakampanam ।। 

bhramaṇaṃ svedajanyā sā saṃvinmūrchā bhavedyadā 
tadottamottamaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ suśobhanaḥ ।। 

sagarbho agarbha ityuktaḥ sajapo vijapaḥ kramāt 
ibho vā śarabho vāpi durādharṣo atha kesarī ।। 

gṛhīto damyamānastu yathāsvasthastu jāyate 
tathā samīraṇo asvastho durādharṣaś ca yoginām ।। 

nyāyataḥ sevyamānastu sa evaṃ svasthatāṃ vrajet 
yathaiva mṛgarāṅnāgaḥ śarabho vāpi durmadaḥ ।। 

kālāntaravaśādyogād damyate paramādarāt 
tathā paricayātsvāsthyaṃ samatvaṃ cādhigacchati ।। 

yogādabhyasate yastu vyasanaṃ naiva jāyate 
evamabhyasyamānastu muneḥ prāṇo vinirdahet ।। 

manovākkāyajān doṣān karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati 
saṃyuktasya tathā samyak prāṇāyāmena dhīmataḥ ।। 

doṣāttasmācca naśyanti niśvāsastena jīryate 
prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti divyāḥ śāntyādayaḥ kramāt ।। 

śāntiḥ praśāntirdīptiś ca prasādaś ca tathā kramāt 
ādau catuṣṭayasyeha proktā śāntiriha dvijāḥ ।। 

sahajāgantukānāṃ ca pāpānāṃ śāntir ucyate 
praśāntiḥ saṃyamaḥ samyag vacasāmiti saṃsmṛtā ।। 

prakāśo dīptirityuktaḥ sarvataḥ sarvadā dvijāḥ 
sarvendriyaprasādastu buddhervai marutāmapi ।। 

prasāda iti samproktaḥ svānte tviha catuṣṭaye 
prāṇo apānaḥ samānaś ca udāno vyāna eva ca ।। 

nāgaḥ kūrmastu kṛkalo devadatto dhanaṃjayaḥ 
eteṣāṃ yaḥ prasādastu marutāmiti saṃsmṛtaḥ ।। 

prayāṇaṃ kurute tasmād vāyuḥ prāṇa iti smṛtaḥ 
apānayatyapānastu āhārādīn krameṇa ca ।। 

vyāno vyānāmayatyaṅgaṃ vyādhyādīnāṃ prakopakaḥ 
udvejayati marmāṇi udāno ayaṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

samaṃ nayati gātrāṇi samānaḥ pañca vāyavaḥ 
udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane tu saḥ ।। 

kṛkalaḥ kṣutakāyaiva devadatto vijṛmbhaṇe 
dhanaṃjayo mahāghoṣaḥ sarvagaḥ sa mṛte api hi ।। 

iti yo daśavāyūnāṃ prāṇāyāmena sidhyati 
prasādo asya turīyā tu saṃjñā viprāścatuṣṭaye ।। 

visvarastu mahān prajño mano brahmā citiḥ smṛtiḥ 
khyātiḥ saṃvittataḥ paścād īśvaro matireva ca ।। 

buddheretāḥ dvijāḥ saṃjñā mahataḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena sidhyati ।। 

visvaro visvarībhāvo dvaṃdvānāṃ munisattamāḥ 
agrajaḥ sarvatattvānāṃ mahānyaḥ parimāṇataḥ ।। 

yatpramāṇaguhā prajñā manastu manute yataḥ 
bṛhattvād bṛṃhaṇatvācca brahmā brahmavidāṃvarāḥ ।। 

sarvakarmāṇi bhogārthaṃ yaccinoti citiḥ smṛtā 
smarate yatsmṛtiḥ sarvaṃ saṃvidvai vindate yataḥ ।। 

khyāyate yattviti khyātir jñānādibhir anekaśaḥ 
sarvatattvādhipaḥ sarvaṃ vijānāti yadīśvaraḥ ।। 

manute manyate yasmān matirmatimatāṃvarāḥ 
arthaṃ bodhayate yacca budhyate buddhirucyate ।। 

asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena sidhyati 
doṣānvinirdahetsarvān prāṇāyāmādasau yamī ।। 

pātakaṃ dhāraṇābhistu pratyāhāreṇa nirdahet 
viṣayānviṣavaddhyātvā dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān ।। 

samādhinā yatiśreṣṭhāḥ prajñāvṛddhiṃ vivardhayet 
sthānaṃ labdhvaiva kurvīta yogāṣṭāṅgāni vai kramāt ।। 

labdhvāsanāni vidhivad yogasiddhyartham ātmavit 
ādeśakāle yogasya darśanaṃ hi na vidyate ।। 

agnyabhyāse jale vāpi śuṣkaparṇacaye tathā 
jantuvyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇagoṣṭhe catuṣpathe ।। 

saśabde sabhaye vāpi caityavalmīkasaṃcaye 
aśubhe durjanākrānte maśakādisamanvite ।। 

nācareddehabādhāyāṃ daurmanasyādisambhave 
sugupte tu śubhe ramye guhāyāṃ parvatasya tu ।। 

bhavakṣetre sugupte vā bhavārāme vane api vā 
gṛhe tu suśubhe deśe vijane jantuvarjite ।। 

atyantanirmale samyak supralipte vicitrite 
darpaṇodarasaṃkāśe kṛṣṇāgarusudhūpite ।। 

nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānopari śobhite 
phalapallavamūlāḍhye kuśapuṣpasamanvite ।। 

samāsanastho yogāṅgāny abhyaseddhṛṣitaḥ svayam 
praṇipatya guruṃ paścād bhavaṃ devīṃ vināyakam ।। 

yogīśvarān saśiṣyāṃś ca yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit 
āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmamardhāsanaṃ tu vā ।। 

samajānus tathā dhīmān ekajānurathāpivā 
samaṃ dṛḍhāsano bhūtvā saṃhṛtya caraṇāvubhau ।। 

saṃvṛtāsyopabaddhākṣa uro viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ 
pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃs tathā prajananaṃ punaḥ ।। 

kiṃcidunnāmitaśira dantairdantānna saṃspṛśet 
samprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan ।। 

tamaḥ pracchādya rajasā rajaḥ sattvena chādayet 
tataḥ sattvasthito bhūtvā śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। 

oṃkāravācyaṃ paramaṃ śuddhaṃ dīpaśikhākṛtim 
dhyāyedvai puṇḍarīkasya karṇikāyāṃ samāhitaḥ ।। 

nābheradhastādvā vidvān dhyātvā kamalamuttamam 
tryaṅgule cāṣṭakoṇaṃ vā pañcakoṇamathāpi vā ।। 

trikoṇaṃ ca tathāgneyaṃ saumyaṃ sauraṃ svaśaktibhiḥ 
sauraṃ saumya tathāgneyam atha vānukrameṇa tu ।। 

āgneyaṃ ca tataḥ sauraṃ saumyamevaṃ vidhānataḥ 
agneradhaḥ prakalpyaivaṃ dharmādīnāṃ catuṣṭayam ।। 

guṇatrayaṃ krameṇaiva maṇḍalopari bhāvayet 
sattvasthaṃ cintayedrudraṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam ।। 

nābhau vātha gale vāpi bhrūmadhye vā yathāvidhi 
lalāṭaphalikāyāṃ vā mūrdhni dhyānaṃ samācaret ।। 

dvidale ṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre krameṇa tu 
daśāre vā ṣaḍasre vā caturasre smarecchivam ।। 

kanakābhe tathāgārasaṃnibhe susite api vā 
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśe candrabimbasame api vā ।। 

vidyutkoṭinibhe sthāne cintayetparameśvaram 
agnivarṇe athavā vidyud valayābhe samāhitaḥ ।। 

vajrakoṭiprabhe sthāne padmarāganibhe api vā 
nīlalohitabimbe vā yogī dhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। 

maheśvaraṃ hṛdi dhyāyen nābhipadme sadāśivam 
candracūḍaṃ lalāṭe tu bhrūmadhye śaṃkaraṃ svayam ।। 

divye ca śāśvatasthāne śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset 
nirmalaṃ niṣkalaṃ brahma suśāntaṃ jñānarūpiṇam ।। 

alakṣaṇamanirdeśyam aṇoralpataraṃ śubham 
nirālambam atarkyaṃ ca vināśotpattivarjitam ।। 

kaivalyaṃ caiva nirvāṇaṃ niḥśreyasam anuttamam 
amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma hy apunarbhavam adbhutam ।। 

mahānandaṃ parānandaṃ yogānandamanāmayam 
heyopādeyarahitaṃ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraṃ śivam ।। 

svayaṃvedyamavedyaṃ tac chivaṃ jñānamayaṃ param 
atīndriyam anābhāsaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ parātparam ।। 

sarvopādhivinirmuktaṃ dhyānagamyaṃ vicārataḥ 
advayaṃ tamasaścaiva parastātsaṃsthitaṃ param ।। 

manasyevaṃ mahādevaṃ hṛtpadme vāpi cintayet 
nābhau sadāśivaṃ cāpi sarvadevātmakaṃ vibhum ।। 

dehamadhye śivaṃ devaṃ śuddhajñānamayaṃ vibhum 
kanyasenaiva mārgeṇa codghātenāpi śaṃkaram ।। 

kramaśaḥ kanyasenaiva madhyamenāpi suvrataḥ 
uttamenāpi vai vidvān kumbhakena samabhyaset ।। 

dvātriṃśad recayeddhīmān hṛdi nābhau samāhitaḥ 
recakaṃ pūrakaṃ tyaktvā kumbhakaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। 

sākṣātsamarasenaiva dehamadhye smarecchivam 
ekībhāvaṃ sametyaivaṃ tatra yadrasasambhavam ।। 

ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān sākṣātsamarase sthitaḥ 
dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśa dhāraṇam ।। 

dhyānaṃ dvādaśakaṃ yāvat samādhir abhidhīyate 
athavā jñānināṃ viprāḥ samparkādeva jāyate ।। 

prayatnādvā tayostulyaṃ cirādvā hyacirāddvijāḥ 
yogāntarāyās tasyātha jāyante yuñjataḥ punaḥ ।। 

naśyanty abhyāsatas te api praṇidhānena vai guroḥ ।। 

ālasyaṃ prathamaṃ paścād vyādhipīḍā prajāyate 
pramādaḥ saṃśayasthāne cittasyehānavasthitiḥ ।। 

aśraddhādarśanaṃ bhrāntir duḥkhaṃ ca trividhaṃ tataḥ 
daurmanasyamayogyeṣu viṣayeṣu ca yogyatā ।। 

daśadhābhiprajāyante muneryogāntarāyakāḥ 
ālasyaṃ cāpravṛttiś ca gurutvātkāyacittayoḥ ।। 

vyādhayo dhātuvaiṣamyāt karmajā doṣajās tathā 
pramādastu samādhestu sādhanānām abhāvanam ।। 

idaṃ vetyubhayaspṛktaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ 
anavasthitacittatvam apratiṣṭhā hi yoginaḥ ।। 

labdhāyāmapi bhūmau ca cittasya bhavabandhanāt 
aśraddhābhāvarahitā vṛttirvai sādhaneṣu ca ।। 

sādhye cittasya hi gurau jñānācāraśivādiṣu 
viparyayajñānamiti bhrāntidarśanam ucyate ।। 

anātmanyātmavijñānam ajñānāttasya saṃnidhau 
duḥkhamādhyātmikaṃ proktaṃ tathā caivādhibhautikam ।। 

ādhidaivikamityuktaṃ trividhaṃ sahajaṃ punaḥ 
icchāvighātātsaṃkṣobhaś cetasastadudāhṛtam ।। 

daurmanasyaṃ niroddhavyaṃ vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu 
tamasā rajasā caiva saṃspṛṣṭaṃ durmanaḥ smṛtam ।। 

tadā manasi saṃjātaṃ daurmanasyamiti smṛtam 
haṭhātsvīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yogyāyogyavivekataḥ ।। 

viṣayeṣu vicitreṣu jantorviṣayalolatā 
antarāyā iti khyātā yogasyaite hi yoginām ।। 

atyantotsāhayuktasya naśyanti na ca saṃśayaḥ 
pranaṣṭeṣvantarāyeṣu dvijāḥ paścāddhi yoginaḥ ।। 

upasargāḥ pravartante sarve te asiddhisūcakāḥ 
pratibhā prathamā siddhir dvitīyā śravaṇā smṛtā ।। 

vārttā tṛtīyā viprendrās turīyā ceha darśanā 
āsvādā pañcamī proktā vedanā ṣaṣṭhikā smṛtā ।। 

svalpaṣaṭsiddhisaṃtyāgāt siddhidāḥ siddhayo muneḥ 
pratibhā pratibhāvṛtiḥ pratibhāva iti sthitiḥ ।। 

buddhirvivecanā vedyaṃ budhyate buddhirucyate 
sūkṣme vyavahite atīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate ।। 

sarvatra sarvadā jñānaṃ pratibhānukrameṇa tu 
śravaṇātsarvaśabdānām aprayatnena yoginaḥ ।। 

hrasvadīrghaplutādīnāṃ guhyānāṃ śravaṇādapi 
sparśasyādhigamo yas tu vedanā tūpapāditā ।। 

darśanāddivyarūpāṇāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ 
saṃviddivyarase tasminn āsvādo hyaprayatnataḥ ।। 

vārttā ca divyagandhānāṃ tanmātrā buddhisaṃvidā 
vindante yoginastasmād ābrahmabhuvanaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

jagatyasmin hi dehasthaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ samam 
aupasargikam eteṣu guṇeṣu guṇitaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

saṃtyājyaṃ sarvathā sarvam aupasargikamātmanaḥ 
paiśāce pārthivaṃ cāpyaṃ rākṣasānāṃ pure dvijāḥ ।। 

yākṣe tu taijasaṃ proktaṃ gāndharve śvasanātmakam 
aindre vyomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saumye caiva tu mānasam ।। 

prājāpatye tvahaṅkāraṃ brāhme bodhamanuttamam 
ādye cāṣṭau dvitīye ca tathā ṣoḍaśarūpakam ।। 

caturviṃśattṛtīye tu dvātriṃśacca caturthake 
catvāriṃśat pañcame tu bhūtamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam ।। 

gandho rasas tathā rūpaṃ śabdaḥ sparśastathaiva ca 
pratyekamaṣṭadhā siddhaṃ pañcame tacchatakratoḥ ।। 

tathāṣṭacatvāriṃśac ca ṣaṭpañcāśattathaiva ca 
catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ brāhmaṃ labhate dvijasattamāḥ ।। 

aupasargikam ā brahma bhuvaneṣu parityajet 
lokeṣvālokya yogena yogavitparamaṃ sukham ।। 

sthūlatā hrasvatā bālyaṃ vārdhakyaṃ yauvanaṃ tathā 
nānājātisvarūpaṃ ca caturbhir dehadhāraṇam ।। 

pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhir gandhasaṃyutaḥ 
etadaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktam aiśvaryaṃ pārthivaṃ mahat ।। 

jale nivasanaṃ yadvad bhūmyāmiva vinirgamaḥ 
icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ ।। 

yatrecchati jagatyasmiṃs tatrāsya jaladarśanam 
yadyadvastu samādāya bhoktumicchati kāmataḥ ।। 

tattadrasānvitaṃ tasya trayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam 
bhāṇḍaṃ vinātha hastena jalapiṇḍasya dhāraṇam ।। 

avraṇatvaṃ śarīrasya pārthivena samanvitam 
etat ṣoḍaśakaṃ proktam āpyamaiśvaryamuttamam ।। 

dehādagnivinirmāṇaṃ tattāpabhayavarjitam 
lokaṃ dagdhamapīhānyad adagdhaṃ svavidhānataḥ ।। 

jalamadhye hutavahaṃ cādhāya parirakṣaṇam 
agninigrahaṇaṃ haste smṛtimātreṇa cāgamaḥ ।। 

bhasmībhūtavinirmāṇaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ sakāmataḥ 
dvābhyāṃ rūpaviniṣpattir vinā taistribhir ātmanaḥ ।। 

caturviṃśātmakaṃ hyetat taijasaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
manogatitvaṃ bhūtānām antarnivasanaṃ tathā ।। 

parvatādimahābhāraskandhenodvahanaṃ punaḥ 
laghutvaṃ ca gurutvaṃ ca pāṇibhyāṃ vāyudhāraṇam ।। 

aṅgulyagranighātena bhūmeḥ sarvatra kaṃpanam 
ekena dehaniṣpattir vātaiśvaryaṃ smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ ।। 

chāyāvihīnaniṣpattir indriyāṇāṃ ca darśanam 
ākāśagamanaṃ nityam indriyārthaiḥ samanvitam ।। 

dūre ca śabdagrahaṇaṃ sarvaśabdāvagāhanam 
tanmātraliṅgagrahaṇaṃ sarvaprāṇinidarśanam ।। 

aindram aiśvaryam ityuktam etairuktaḥ purātanaḥ 
yathākāmopalabdhiś ca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ ।। 

sarvatrābhibhavaścaiva sarvaguhyanidarśanam 
kāmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam ।। 

saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva mānasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam 
chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ bandhaṃ saṃsāraparivartanam ।। 

sarvabhūtaprasādaś ca mṛtyukālajayas tathā 
prājāpatyamidaṃ proktam āhaṅkārikamuttamam ।। 

akāraṇajagatsṛṣṭis tathānugraha eva ca 
pralayaścādhikāraś ca lokavṛttapravartanam ।। 

asādṛśyamidaṃ vyaktaṃ nirmāṇaṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak 
saṃsārasya ca kartṛtvaṃ brāhmam etad anuttamam ।। 

etāvattattvamityuktaṃ prādhānyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam 
brahmaṇā tadguṇaṃ śakyaṃ vettumanyairna śakyate ।। 

vidyate tatparaṃ śaivaṃ viṣṇunā nāvagamyate 
asaṃkhyeyaguṇaṃ śuddhaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam ।। 

vyutthāne siddhayaścaitā hy upasargāś ca kīrtitāḥ 
niroddhavyāḥ prayatnena vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu ।। 

nāśātiśayatāṃ jñātvā viṣayeṣu bhayeṣu ca 
aśraddhayā tyajetsarvaṃ virakta iti kīrtitaḥ ।। 

vaitṛṣṇyaṃ puruṣe khyātaṃ guṇavaitṛṣṇyamucyate 
vairāgyeṇaiva saṃtyājyāḥ siddhayaścaupasargikāḥ ।। 

aupasargikam ā brahmabhuvaneṣu parityajet 
nirudhyaiva tyajetsarvaṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ ।। 

prasanne vimalā muktir vairāgyeṇa pareṇa vai 
athavānugrahārthaṃ ca līlārthaṃ vā tadā muniḥ ।। 

anirudhya viceṣṭedyaḥ so apyevaṃ hi sukhī bhavet 
kvacidbhūmiṃ parityajya hy ākāśe krīḍate śriyā ।। 

udgirecca kvacidvedān sūkṣmānarthān samāsataḥ 
kvacicchrute tadarthena ślokabandhaṃ karoti saḥ ।। 

kvaciddaṇḍakabandhaṃ tu kuryādbandhaṃ sahasraśaḥ 
mṛgapakṣisamūhasya rutajñānaṃ ca vindati ।। 

brahmādyaṃ sthāvarāntaṃ ca hastāmalakavadbhavet 
bahunātra kimuktena vijñānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। 

utpadyante muniśreṣṭhā munestasya mahātmanaḥ 
abhyāsenaiva vijñānaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthiraṃ bhavet ।। 

tejorūpāṇi sarvāṇi sarvaṃ paśyati yogavit 
devabimbānyanekāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। 

paśyati brahmaviṣṇvindrayamāgnivaruṇādikān 
grahanakṣatratārāś ca bhuvanāni sahasraśaḥ ।। 

pātālatalasaṃsthāś ca samādhisthaḥ sa paśyati 
ātmavidyāpradīpena svasthenācalanena tu ।। 

prasādāmṛtapūrṇena sattvapātrasthitena tu 
tamo nihatya puruṣaḥ paśyati hyātmanīśvaram ।। 

tasya prasādāddharmaś ca aiśvaryaṃ jñānameva ca 
vairāgyamapavargaś ca nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

na śakyo vistaro vaktuṃ varṣāṇāmayutairapi 
yoge pāśupate niṣṭhā sthātavyaṃ ca munīśvarāḥ ।। 

satāṃ jitātmanāṃ sākṣād dvijātīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ 
dharmajñānāṃ ca sādhūnām ācāryāṇāṃ śivātmanām ।। 

dayāvatāṃ dvijaśreṣṭhās tathā caiva tapasvinām 
saṃnyāsināṃ viraktānāṃ jñānināṃ vaśagātmanām ।। 

dānināṃ caiva dāntānāṃ trayāṇāṃ satyavādinām 
alubdhānāṃ sayogānāṃ śrutismṛtividāṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

śrautasmārtāviruddhānāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ 
saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdas tadante ye labhantyuta ।। 

sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇo yāti tena santaḥ pracakṣate 
daśātmake ye viṣaye sādhane cāṣṭalakṣaṇe ।। 

na krudhyanti na hṛṣyanti jitātmānastu te smṛtāḥ 
sāmānyeṣu ca dravyeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca ।। 

brahmakṣatraviśo yasmād yuktāstasmāddvijātayaḥ 
varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargādisukhakāriṇaḥ ।। 

śrautasmārtasya dharmasya jñānāddharmajña ucyate 
vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhubrahmacārī gurorhitaḥ ।। 

kriyāṇāṃ sādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate 
sādhanāttapaso araṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt 
evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatis tathā 
dharmādharmāviha proktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau ।। 

kuśalākuśalaṃ karma dharmādharmāviti smṛtau 
dhāraṇārthe mahān hy eṣa dharmaśabdaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। 

adhāraṇe mahattve ca adharma iti cocyate 
atreṣṭaprāpako dharma ācāryairupadiśyate ।। 

adharmaścāniṣṭaphalo hy ācāryairupadiśyate 
vṛddhāścālolupāścaiva ātmavanto hyadāmbhikāḥ ।। 

samyagvinītā ṛjavas tānācāryān pracakṣate 
svayamācarate yasmād ācāre sthāpayatyapi ।। 

ācinoti ca śāstrārthān ācāryastena cocyate 
vijñeyaṃ śravaṇācchrautaṃ smaraṇātsmārtamucyate ।। 

ijyā vedātmakaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ varṇāśramātmakam 
dṛṣṭvānurūpamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo naivāpi gūhati ।। 

yathādṛṣṭapravādastu satyaṃ laiṅge atra paṭhyate 
brahmacaryaṃ tathā maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca ।। 

ahiṃsā sarvataḥ śāntis tapa ityabhidhīyate 
ātmavat sarvabhūteṣu yo hitāyāhitāya ca ।। 

vartate tvasakṛdvṛttiḥ kṛtsnā hyeṣā dayā smṛtā 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ kramāt ।। 

tattadguṇavate deyaṃ dātustaddānalakṣaṇam 
dānaṃ trividhamityetat kaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhyamam ।। 

kāruṇyātsarvabhūtebhyaḥ saṃvibhāgastu madhyamaḥ 
śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varṇāśramātmakaḥ ।। 

śiṣṭācārāviruddhaś ca sa dharmaḥ sādhurucyate 
māyākarmaphalatyāgī śivātmā parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

nivṛttaḥ sarvasaṅgebhyo yukto yogī prakīrtitaḥ 
asakto bhayato yastu viṣayeṣu vicārya ca ।। 

alubdhaḥ saṃyamī proktaḥ prārthito api samantataḥ 
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā indriyāṇīha yasya vai ।। 

na mithyā sampravartante śamasyaiva tu lakṣaṇam 
anudvigno hyaniṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭānnābhinandati ।। 

prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā 
saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha ।। 

kuśalākuśalānāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate 
avyaktādyaviśeṣānte vikāre asminnacetane ।। 

cetanācetanānyatvavijñānaṃ jñānamucyate 
evaṃ tu jñānayuktasya śraddhāyuktasya śaṅkaraḥ ।। 

prasīdati na saṃdeho dharmaścāyaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
kiṃ tu guhyatamaṃ vakṣye sarvatra parameśvare ।। 

bhave bhaktirna saṃdehas tayā yukto vimucyate 
ayogyasyāpi bhagavān bhaktasya parameśvaraḥ ।। 

prasīdati na saṃdeho nigṛhya vividhaṃ tamaḥ 
jñānamadhyāpanaṃ homo dhyānaṃ yajñastapaḥ śrutam ।। 

dānamadhyayanaṃ sarvaṃ bhavabhaktyai na saṃśayaḥ 
cāndrāyaṇasahasraiś ca prājāpatyaśatais tathā ।। 

māsopavāsaiścānyairvā bhaktirmunivarottamāḥ 
abhaktā bhagavatyasmiṃl loke giriguhāśaye ।। 

patanti cātmabhogārthaṃ bhakto bhāvena mucyate 
bhaktānāṃ darśanādeva nṛṇāṃ svargādayo dvijāḥ ।। 

na durlabhā na sandeho bhaktānāṃ kiṃ punas tathā 
brahmaviṣṇusurendrāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāmapi sthitiḥ ।। 

bhaktyā eva munīnāṃ ca balasaubhāgyameva ca 
bhavena ca tathā proktaṃ samprekṣyomāṃ pinākinā ।। 

devyai devena madhuraṃ vārāṇasyāṃ purā dvijāḥ 
avimukte samāsīnā rudreṇa paramātmanā ।। 

rudrāṇī rudramāhedaṃ labdhvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm 
kena vaśyo mahādeva pūjyo dṛśyastvamīśvaraḥ ।। 

tapasā vidyayā vāpi yogeneha vada prabho 
niśamya vacanaṃ tasyās tathā hyālokya pārvatīm ।। 

āha bālendutilakaḥ pūrṇenduvadanāṃ hasan 
smṛtvātha menayā patnyā girergāṃ kathitāṃ purā ।। 

cirakālasthitiṃ prekṣya girau devyā mahātmanaḥ 
devi labdhā purī ramyā tvayā yatpraṣṭumarhasi ।। 

sthānārthaṃ kathitaṃ mātrā vismṛteha vilāsini 
purā pitāmahenāpi pṛṣṭaḥ praśnavatāṃ vare ।। 

yathā tvayādya vai pṛṣṭo draṣṭuṃ brahmātmakaṃ tvaham 
śvete śvetena varṇena dṛṣṭvā kalpe tu māṃ śubhe ।। 

sadyojātaṃ tathā rakte raktaṃ vāmaṃ pitāmahaḥ 
pīte tatpuruṣaṃ pītam aghore kṛṣṇamīśvaram ।। 

īśānaṃ viśvarūpākhyo viśvarūpaṃ tadāha mām ।। 

vāma tatpuruṣāghora sadyojāta maheśvara 
dṛṣṭo mayā tvaṃ gāyatryā devadeva maheśvara 
kena vaśyo mahādeva dhyeyaḥ kutra ghṛṇānidhe ।। 

dṛśyaḥ pūjyas tathā devyā vaktumarhasi śaṅkara 
avocaṃ śraddhayaiveti vaśyo vārijasaṃbhava ।। 

dhyeyo liṅge tvayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā payasāṃ nidhau 
pūjyaḥ pañcāsyarūpeṇa pavitraiḥ pañcabhirdvijaiḥ ।। 

bhava bhaktyādya dṛṣṭo ahaṃ tvayāṇḍaja jagadguro 
so api māmāha bhāvārthaṃ dattaṃ tasmai mayā purā ।। 

bhāvaṃ bhāvena deveśi dṛṣṭavānmāṃ hṛdīśvaram 
tasmāttu śraddhayā vaśyo dṛśyaḥ śreṣṭhagireḥ sute ।। 

pūjyo liṅge na saṃdehaḥ sarvadā śraddhayā dvijaiḥ 
śraddhā dharmaḥ paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ śraddhā jñānaṃ hutaṃ tapaḥ ।। 

śraddhā svargaś ca mokṣaś ca dṛśyo ahaṃ śraddhayā sadā ।। 

kathaṃ vai dṛṣṭavānbrahmā sadyojātaṃ maheśvaram 
vāmadevaṃ mahātmānaṃ purāṇapuruṣottamam ।। 

aghoraṃ ca tatheśānaṃ yathāvadvaktumarhasi 
ekonatriṃśakaḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।। 

tasmiṃstatparamaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyāyato brahmaṇastadā 
utpannastu śikhāyuktaḥ kumāraḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ śrīmān brahmā vai viśvatomukhaḥ 
hṛdi kṛtvā mahātmānaṃ brahmarūpiṇamīśvaram ।। 

sadyojātaṃ tato brahmā dhyānayogaparo abhavat 
dhyānayogātparaṃ jñātvā vavande devamīśvaram ।। 

sadyojātaṃ tato brahma brahma vai samacintayat 
tato asya pārśvataḥ śvetāḥ prādurbhūtā mahāyaśāḥ ।। 

sunando nandanaścaiva viśvanandopanandanau 
śiṣyāste vai mahātmāno yaistadbrahma sadāvṛtam ।। 

tasyāgre śvetavarṇābhaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ 
vijajñe atha mahātejās tasmājjajñe harastvasau ।। 

tatra te munayaḥ sarve sadyojātaṃ maheśvaram 
prapannāḥ parayā bhaktyā gṛṇanto brahma śāśvatam ।। 

tasmādviśveśvaraṃ devaṃ ye prapadyanti vai dvijāḥ 
prāṇāyāmaparā bhūtvā brahmatatparamānasāḥ ।। 

te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimalā brahmavarcasaḥ 
viṣṇulokamatikramya rudralokaṃ vrajanti te ।। 

tatastriṃśattamaḥ kalpo rakto nāma prakīrtitaḥ 
brahmā yatra mahātejā raktavarṇamadhārayat ।। 

dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāro raktabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

raktamālyāmbaradharo raktanetraḥ pratāpavān 
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ kumāraṃ raktavāsasam ।। 

paraṃ dhyānaṃ samāśritya bubudhe devamīśvaram 
sa taṃ praṇamya bhagavān brahmā paramayantritaḥ ।। 

vāmadevaṃ tato brahmā brahma vai samacintayat 
tathā stuto mahādevo brahmaṇā parameśvaraḥ ।। 

pratītahṛdayaḥ sarva idamāha pitāmaham 
dhyāyatā putrakāmena yasmātte ahaṃ pitāmaha ।। 

dṛṣṭaḥ paramayā bhaktyā stutaś ca brahmapūrvakam 
tasmāddhyānabalaṃ prāpya kalpe kalpe prayatnataḥ ।। 

vetsyase māṃ prasaṃkhyātaṃ lokadhātāramīśvaram 
tatastasya mahātmānaś catvāraste kumārakāḥ ।। 

saṃbabhūvurmahātmāno viśuddhā brahmavarcasaḥ 
virajāś ca vibāhuś ca viśoko viśvabhāvanaḥ ।। 

brahmaṇyā brahmaṇastulyā vīrā adhyavasāyinaḥ 
raktāṃbaradharāḥ sarve raktamālyānulepanāḥ ।। 

raktakuṅkumaliptāṅgā raktabhasmānulepanāḥ 
tato varṣasahasrānte brahmatve adhyavasāyinaḥ ।। 

gṛṇantaś ca mahātmāno brahma tadvāmadaivikam 
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 

dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā te brahmaṇaḥ priyāḥ 
punareva mahādevaṃ praviṣṭā rudramavyayam ।। 

ye api cānye dvijaśreṣṭhā yuñjānā vāmamīśvaram 
prapaśyanti mahādevaṃ tadbhaktās tatparāyaṇāḥ ।। 

te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ 
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। 

ekatriṃśattamaḥ kalpaḥ pītavāsā iti smṛtaḥ 
brahmā yatra mahābhāgaḥ pītavāsā babhūva ha ।। 

dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāraḥ pītavastradhṛk ।। 

pītagandhānuliptāṅgaḥ pītamālyāṃbaro yuvā 
hemayajñopavītaś ca pītoṣṇīṣo mahābhujaḥ ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmā lokamaheśvaram 
manasā lokadhātāraṃ prapede śaraṇaṃ vibhum ।। 

tato dhyānagatastatra brahmā māheśvarīṃ varām 
gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ dadṛśe maheśvaramukhāccyutām ।। 

catuṣpadāṃ caturvaktrāṃ caturhastāṃ catuḥstanīm 
caturnetrāṃ catuḥśṛṅgīṃ caturdaṃṣṭrāṃ caturmukhīm ।। 

dvātriṃśadguṇasaṃyuktām īśvarīṃ sarvatomukhīm 
sa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātejā mahādevīṃ maheśvarīm ।। 

punarāha mahādevaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ 
matiḥ smṛtirbuddhiriti gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

ehyehīti mahādevi sātiṣṭhatprāñjalirvibhum 
viśvamāvṛtya yogena jagatsarvaṃ vaśīkuru ।। 

atha tāmāha deveśo rudrāṇī tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi 
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya paramārthā bhaviṣyasi ।। 

tathaināṃ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
pradadau devadeveśaḥ catuṣpādāṃ jagadguruḥ ।। 

tatastāṃ dhyānayogena viditvā parameśvarīm 
brahmā lokaguroḥ so atha pratipede maheśvarīm ।। 

gāyatrīṃ tu tato raudrīṃ dhyātvā brahmānuyantritaḥ 
ityetāṃ vaidikīṃ vidyāṃ raudrīṃ gāyatrīmīritām ।। 

japitvā tu mahādevīṃ brahmā lokanamaskṛtām 
prapannastu mahādevaṃ dhyānayuktena cetasā ।। 

tatastasya mahādevo divyayogaṃ bahuśrutam 
aiśvaryaṃ jñānasaṃpattiṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau prabhuḥ ।। 

tato asya pārśvato divyāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ kumārakāḥ 
pītamālyāṃbaradharāḥ pītasraganulepanāḥ ।। 

pītābhoṣṇīṣaśirasaḥ pītāsyāḥ pītamūrdhajāḥ 
tato varṣasahasrānta uṣitvā vimalaujasaḥ ।। 

yogātmānastapohlādāḥ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitaiṣiṇaḥ 
dharmayogabalopetā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām ।। 

upadiśya mahāyogaṃ praviṣṭāste maheśvaram 
evametena vidhinā ye prapannā maheśvaram ।। 

anye api niyatātmāno dhyānayuktā jitendriyāḥ 
te sarve pāpamutsṛjya vimalā brahmavarcasaḥ ।। 

praviśanti mahādevaṃ rudraṃ te tvapunarbhavāḥ ।। 

tatastasmingate kalpe pītavarṇe svayaṃbhuvaḥ 
punaranyaḥ pravṛttastu kalpo nāmnāsitastu saḥ ।। 

ekārṇave tadā vṛtte divye varṣasahasrake 
sraṣṭukāmaḥ prajā brahmā cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ ।। 

tasya cintayamānasya putrakāmasya vai prabhoḥ 
kṛṣṇaḥ samabhavadvarṇo dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

athāpaśyanmahātejāḥ prādurbhūtaṃ kumārakam 
kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ mahāvīryaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā ।। 

kṛṣṇāṃbaradharoṣṇīṣaṃ kṛṣṇayajñopavītinam 
kṛṣṇena maulinā yuktaṃ kṛṣṇasraganulepanam ।। 

sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānam aghoraṃ ghoravikramam 
vavande devadeveśam adbhutaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam ।। 

prāṇāyāmaparaḥ śrīmān hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram 
manasā dhyānuyuktena prapannastu tamīśvaram ।। 

aghoraṃ tu tato brahmā brahmarūpaṃ vyacintayat 
tathā vai dhyāyamānasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

pradadau darśanaṃ devo hy aghoro ghoravikramaḥ 
athāsya pārśvataḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇasraganulepanāḥ ।। 

catvārastu mahātmānaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ kumārakāḥ 
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaśikhaścaiva kṛṣṇāsyaḥ kṛṣṇavastradhṛk ।। 

tato varṣasahasraṃ tu yogataḥ parameśvaram 
upāsitvā mahāyogaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ pradaduḥ punaḥ ।। 

yogena yogasampannāḥ praviśya manasā śivam 
amalaṃ nirguṇaṃ sthānaṃ praviṣṭā viśvamīśvaram ।। 

evametena yogena ye api cānye manīṣiṇaḥ 
cintayanti mahādevaṃ gantāro rudramavyayam ।। 

tatastasmin gate kalpe kṛṣṇavarṇe bhayānake 
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ brahmā taṃ brahmarūpiṇam ।। 

anugṛhya tatastuṣṭo brahmāṇamavadaddharaḥ 
anenaiva tu rūpeṇa saṃharāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

brahmahatyādikān ghorāṃs tathānyānapi pātakān 
hīnāṃścaiva mahābhāga tathaiva vividhānyapi ।। 

upapātakamapyevaṃ tathā pāpāni suvrata 
mānasāni sutīkṣṇāni vācikāni pitāmaha ।। 

kāyikāni sumiśrāṇi tathā prāsaṃgikāni ca 
buddhipūrvaṃ kṛtānyeva sahajāgantukāni ca ।। 

mātṛdehotthitānyevaṃ pitṛdehe ca pātakam 
saṃharāmi na saṃdehaḥ sarvaṃ pātakajaṃ vibho ।। 

lakṣaṃ japtvā hyaghorebhyo brahmahā mucyate prabho 
tadardhaṃ vācike vatsa tadardhaṃ mānase punaḥ ।। 

caturguṇaṃ buddhipūrve krodhādaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam 
vīrahā lakṣamātreṇa bhrūṇahā koṭimabhyaset ।। 

mātṛhā niyutaṃ japtvā śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca strīghnaḥ pāpayuto naraḥ ।। 

ayutāghoramabhyasya mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
surāpo lakṣamātreṇa buddhyābuddhyāpi vai prabho ।। 

mucyate nātra saṃdehas tadardhena ca vāruṇīm 
asnātāśī sahasreṇa ajapī ca tathā dvijaḥ ।। 

ahutāśī sahasreṇa adātā ca viśudhyati 
brāhmaṇasvāpahartā ca svarṇasteyī narādhamaḥ ।। 

niyutaṃ mānasaṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
gurutalparato vāpi mātṛghno vā narādhamaḥ ।। 

brahmaghnaś ca japedevaṃ mānasaṃ vai pitāmaha 
saṃparkātpāpināṃ pāpaṃ tatsamaṃ paribhāṣitam ।। 

tathāpyayutamātreṇa pātakādvai pramucyate 
saṃsargātpātakī lakṣaṃ japedvai mānasaṃ dhiyā ।। 

upāṃśu yaccaturdhā vai vācikaṃ cāṣṭadhā japet 
pātakādardhameva syād upapātakināṃ smṛtam ।। 

tadardhaṃ kevale pāpe nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ suvarṇasteyameva ca ।। 

kṛtvā ca gurutalpaṃ ca pāpakṛdbrāhmaṇo yadi 
rudragāyatriyā grāhyaṃ gomūtraṃ kāpilaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

gandhadvāreti tasyā vai gomayaṃ svastham āharet 
tejo asi śuktam ityājyaṃ kāpilaṃ saṃharedbudhaḥ ।। 

āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇeti cāharet 
gavyaṃ dadhi navaṃ sākṣāt kāpilaṃ vai pitāmaha ।। 

devasya tveti mantreṇa saṃgrahedvai kuśodakam 
ekasthaṃ hemapātre vā kṛtvāghoreṇa rājate ।। 

tāmre vā padmapātre vā pālāśe vā dale śubhe 
sakūrcaṃ sarvaratnāḍhyaṃ kṣiptvā tatraiva kāñcanam ।। 

japellakṣamaghorākhyaṃ hutvā caiva ghṛtādibhiḥ 
ghṛtena caruṇā caiva samidbhiś ca tilais tathā ।। 

yavaiś ca vrīhibhiścaiva juhuyādvai pṛthakpṛthak 
pratyekaṃ saptavāraṃ tu dravyālābhe ghṛtena tu ।। 

hutvāghoreṇa deveśaṃ snātvāghoreṇa vai dvijāḥ 
aṣṭadroṇaghṛtenaiva snāpya paścādviśodhya ca ।। 

ahorātroṣitaḥ snātaḥ pibetkūrcaṃ śivāgrataḥ 
brāhmaṃ brahmajapaṃ kuryād ācamya ca yathāvidhi ।। 

evaṃ kṛtvā kṛtaghno api brahmahā bhrūṇahā tathā 
vīrahā gurughātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ ।। 

steyī suvarṇasteyī ca gurutalparataḥ sadā 
madyapo vṛṣalīsaktaḥ paradāravidharṣakaḥ ।। 

brahmasvahā tathā goghno mātṛhā pitṛhā tathā 
devapracyāvakaścaiva liṅgapradhvaṃsakas tathā ।। 

tathānyāni ca pāpāni mānasāni dvijo yadi 
vācikāni tathānyāni kāyikāni sahasraśaḥ ।। 

kṛtvā vimucyate sadyo janmāntaraśatairapi 
etadrahasyaṃ kathitam aghoreśaprasaṃgataḥ ।। 

tasmājjapeddvijo nityaṃ sarvapāpaviśuddhaye ।। 

athānyo brahmaṇaḥ kalpo vartate munipuṅgavāḥ 
viśvarūpa iti khyāto nāmataḥ paramādbhutaḥ ।। 

vinivṛtte tu saṃhāre punaḥ sṛṣṭe carācare 
brahmaṇaḥ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

prādurbhūtā mahānādā viśvarūpā sarasvatī 
viśvamālyāṃbaradharā viśvayajñopavītinī ।। 

viśvoṣṇīṣā viśvagandhā viśvamātā mahoṣṭhikā 
tathāvidhaṃ sa bhagavān īśānaṃ parameśvaram ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
atha taṃ manasā dhyātvā yuktātmā vai pitāmahaḥ ।। 

vavande devamīśānaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvagaṃ prabhum 
omīśāna namaste astu mahādeva namo astu te ।। 

namo astu sarvavidyānām īśāna parameśvara 
namo astu sarvabhūtānām īśāna vṛṣavāhana ।। 

brahmaṇo adhipate tubhyaṃ brahmaṇe brahmarūpiṇe 
namo brahmādhipataye śivaṃ me astu sadāśiva ।। 

oṅkāramūrte deveśa sadyojāta namonamaḥ 
prapadye tvāṃ prapanno asmi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ।। 

abhave ca bhave tubhyaṃ tathā nātibhave namaḥ 
bhavodbhava bhaveśāna māṃ bhajasva mahādyute ।। 

vāmadeva namastubhyaṃ jyeṣṭhāya varadāya ca 
namo rudrāya kālāya kalanāya namo namaḥ ।। 

namo vikaraṇāyaiva kālavarṇāya varṇine 
balāya balināṃ nityaṃ sadā vikaraṇāya te ।। 

balapramathanāyaiva baline brahmarūpiṇe 
sarvabhūteśvareśāya bhūtānāṃ damanāya ca ।। 

manonmanāya devāya namastubhyaṃ mahādyute 
vāmadevāya vāmāya namastubhyaṃ mahātmane ।। 

jyeṣṭhāya caiva śreṣṭhāya rudrāya varadāya ca 
kālahantre namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ mahātmane ।। 

iti stavena deveśaṃ nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam 
yaḥ paṭhet sakṛdeveha brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyati ।। 

śrāvayedvā dvijān śrāddhe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
evaṃ dhyānagataṃ tatra praṇamantaṃ pitāmaham ।। 

uvāca bhagavānīśaḥ prīto ahaṃ te kimicchasi 
tatastu praṇato bhūtvā vāgviśuddhaṃ maheśvaram ।। 

uvāca bhagavān rudraṃ prītaṃ prītena cetasā 
yadidaṃ viśvarūpaṃ te viśvagauḥ śreyasīśvarī ।। 

etadveditumicchāmi yatheyaṃ parameśvara 
kaiṣā bhagavatī devī catuṣpādā caturmukhī ।। 

catuḥśṛṅgī caturvaktrā caturdaṃṣṭrā catuḥstanī 
caturhastā caturnetrā viśvarūpā kathaṃ smṛtā ।। 

kiṃnāmagotrā kasyeyaṃ kiṃvīryā cāpi karmataḥ 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। 

prāha devavṛṣaṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ cātmasaṃbhavam 
rahasyaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ pāvanaṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।। 

śṛṇuṣvaitatparaṃ guhyam ādisarge yathā tathā 
evaṃ yo vartate kalpo viśvarūpastvasau mataḥ ।। 

brahmasthānamidaṃ cāpi yatra prāptaṃ tvayā prabho 
tvattaḥ parataraṃ deva viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ śubham ।। 

vaikuṇṭhena viśuddhena mama vāmāṅgajena vā 
tadāprabhṛti kalpaś ca trayastriṃśattamo hyayam ।। 

śataṃ śatasahasrāṇām atītā ye svayaṃbhuvaḥ 
purastāttava deveśa tacchṛṇuṣva mahāmate ।। 

ānandastu sa vijñeya ānandatve vyavasthitaḥ 
māṇḍavyagotrastapasā mama putratvamāgataḥ ।। 

tvayi yogaṃ ca sāṃkhyaṃ ca tapovidyāvidhikriyāḥ 
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ dayā brahma ahiṃsā sanmatiḥ kṣamā ।। 

dhyānaṃ dhyeyaṃ damaḥ śāntir vidyāvidyā matirdhṛtiḥ 
kāntirnītiḥ prathā medhā lajjā dṛṣṭiḥ sarasvatī ।। 

tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva prasādaś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
dvātriṃśatsuguṇā hyeṣā dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃjñayā ।। 

prakṛtirvihitā brahmaṃs tvatprasūtirmaheśvarī 
viṣṇorbhagavataścāpi tathānyeṣāmapi prabho ।। 

saiṣā bhagavatī devī matprasūtiḥ pratiṣṭhitā 
caturmukhī jagadyoniḥ prakṛtir gauḥ pratiṣṭhitā ।। 

gaurī māyā ca vidyā ca kṛṣṇā haimavatīti ca 
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiścaiva yāmāhustattvacintakāḥ ।। 

ajāmekāṃ lohitāṃ śuklakṛṣṇāṃ viśvaprajāṃ sṛjamānāṃ sarūpām 
ajo ahaṃ māṃ viddhi tāṃ viśvarūpaṃ gāyatrīṃ gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ hi buddhyā ।। 

evamuktvā mahādevaḥ sasarja parameśvaraḥ 
tataś ca pārśvagā devyāḥ sarvarūpakumārakāḥ ।। 

jaṭī muṇḍī śikhaṇḍī ca ardhamuṇḍaś ca jajñire 
tatastena yathoktena yogena sumahaujasaḥ ।। 

divyavarṣasahasrānte upāsitvā maheśvaram 
dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā yogamayaṃ dṛḍham ।। 

śiṣṭāś ca niyatātmānaḥ praviṣṭā rudramīśvaram ।। 

evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ sahyādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān ।। 

sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ 
kathaṃ liṅgamabhūlliṅge samabhyarcyaḥ sa śaṅkaraḥ ।। 

kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī sūta vaktumihārhasi 
evaṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham ।। 

apṛcchan bhagavaṃlliṅgaṃ kathamāsīditi svayam 
liṅge maheśvaro rudraḥ samabhyarcyaḥ kathaṃ tviti ।। 

kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī so apyāha ca pitāmahaḥ 
pradhānaṃ liṅgamākhyātaṃ liṅgī ca parameśvaraḥ ।। 

rakṣārthamaṃbudhau mahyaṃ viṣṇostvāsīt surottamāḥ 
vaimānike gate sarge janalokaṃ saharṣibhiḥ ।। 

sthitikāle tadā pūrṇe tataḥ pratyāhṛte tathā 
caturyugasahasrānte satyalokaṃ gate surāḥ ।। 

vinādhipatyaṃ samatāṃ gate ante brahmaṇo mama 
śuṣke ca sthāvare sarve tv anāvṛṣṭyā ca sarvaśaḥ ।। 

paśavo mānuṣā vṛkṣāḥ piśācāḥ piśitāśanāḥ 
gandharvādyāḥ krameṇaiva nirdagdhā bhānubhānubhiḥ ।। 

ekārṇave mahāghore tamobhūte samantataḥ 
suṣvāpāṃbhasi yogātmā nirmalo nirupaplavaḥ ।। 

sahasraśīrṣā viśvātmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt 
sahasrabāhuḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadevabhavodbhavaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyagarbho rajasā tamasā śaṅkaraḥ svayam 
sattvena sarvago viṣṇuḥ sarvātmatve maheśvaraḥ ।। 

kālātmā kālanābhastu śuklaḥ kṛṣṇastu nirguṇaḥ 
nārāyaṇo mahābāhuḥ sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ ।। 

tathābhūtamahaṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam 
māyayā mohitastasya tamavocamamarṣitaḥ ।। 

kastvaṃ vadeti hastena samutthāpya sanātanam 
tadā hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇa sa dṛḍhena tu ।। 

prabuddho ahīyaśayanāt samāsīnaḥ kṣaṇaṃ vaśī 
dadarśa nidrāviklinnanīrajāmalalocanaḥ ।। 

māmagre saṃsthitaṃ bhāsādhyāsito bhagavān hariḥ 
āha cotthāya bhagavān hasanmāṃ madhuraṃ sakṛt ।। 

svāgataṃsvāgataṃ vatsa pitāmaha mahādyute 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā smitapūrvaṃ surarṣabhāḥ ।। 

rajasā baddhavairaś ca tamavocaṃ janārdanam 
bhāṣase vatsa vatseti sargasaṃhārakāraṇam ।। 

mām ihāntaḥsmitaṃ kṛtvā guruḥ śiṣyamivānagha 
kartāraṃ jagatāṃ sākṣāt prakṛteś ca pravartakam ।। 

sanātanamajaṃ viṣṇuṃ viriñciṃ viśvasaṃbhavam 
viśvātmānaṃ vidhātāraṃ dhātāraṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam ।। 

kimarthaṃ bhāṣase mohād vaktumarhasi satvaram 
so api māmāha jagatāṃ kartāhamiti lokaya ।। 

bhartā hartā bhavān aṅgād avatīrṇo mamāvyayāt 
vismṛto asi jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।। 

puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam 
viṣṇumacyutamīśānaṃ viśvasya prabhavodbhavam ।। 

tavāparādho nāstyatra mama māyākṛtaṃ tvidam 
śṛṇu satyaṃ caturvaktra sarvadeveśvaro hyayam ।। 

kartā netā ca hartā ca na mayāsti samo vibhuḥ 
ahameva paraṃ brahma paraṃ tattvaṃ pitāmaha ।। 

ahameva paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā tvahaṃ vibhuḥ 
yadyaddṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācaram ।। 

tattadviddhi caturvaktra sarvaṃ manmayamityatha 
mayā sṛṣṭaṃ purāvyaktaṃ caturviṃśatikaṃ svayam ।। 

nityāntā hyaṇavo baddhāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ krodhodbhavādayaḥ 
prasādāddhi bhavānaṇḍāny anekānīha līlayā ।। 

sṛṣṭā buddhirmayā tasyām ahaṅkārastridhā tataḥ 
tanmātrāpañcakaṃ tasmān manaḥ ṣaṣṭhendriyāṇi ca ।। 

ākāśādīni bhūtāni bhautikāni ca līlayā 
ityuktavati tasmiṃś ca mayi cāpi vacas tathā ।। 

āvayoścābhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam 
pralayārṇavamadhye tu rajasā baddhavairayoḥ ।। 

etasminnantare liṅgam abhavaccāvayoḥ puraḥ 
vivādaśamanārthaṃ hi prabodhārthaṃ ca bhāsvaram ।। 

jvālāmālāsahasrāḍhyaṃ kālānalaśatopamam 
kṣayavṛddhivinirmuktam ādimadhyāntavarjitam ।। 

anaupamyamanirdeśyam avyaktaṃ viśvasaṃbhavam 
tasya jvālāsahasreṇa mohito bhagavān hariḥ ।। 

mohitaṃ prāha māmatra parīkṣāvo agnisaṃbhavam 
adhogamiṣyāmyanalastaṃbhasyānupamasya ca ।। 

bhavānūrdhvaṃ prayatnena gantumarhasi satvaram 
evaṃ vyāhṛtya viśvātmā svarūpamakarottadā ।। 

vārāhamahamapyāśu haṃsatvaṃ prāptavānsurāḥ 
tadāprabhṛti māmāhurh aṃsaṃ haṃso virāḍiti ।। 

haṃsahaṃseti yo brūyān māṃ haṃsaḥ sa bhaviṣyati 
suśveto hyanalākṣaś ca viśvataḥ pakṣasaṃyutaḥ ।। 

mano anilajavo bhūtvā gato ahaṃ cordhvataḥ surāḥ 
nārāyaṇo api viśvātmā nīlāñjanacayopamam ।। 

daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ śatayojanamāyatam 
meruparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ gauratīkṣṇāgradaṃṣṭriṇam ।। 

kālādityasamābhāsaṃ dīrghaghoṇaṃ mahāsvaram 
hrasvapādaṃ vicitrāṅgaṃ jaitraṃ dṛḍham anaupamam ।। 

vārāhamasitaṃ rūpam āsthāya gatavānadhaḥ 
evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaranviṣṇuradhogataḥ ।। 

nāpaśyadalpamapyasya mūlaṃ liṅgasya sūkaraḥ 
tāvatkālaṃ gato hyūrdhvam ahamapyarisūdanaḥ ।। 

satvaraṃ sarvayatnena tasyāntaṃ jñātumicchayā 
śrānto hyadṛṣṭvā tasyāntam ahaṅkārādadhogataḥ ।। 

tathaiva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃtrastalocanaḥ 
sarvadevabhavastūrṇam utthitaḥ saḥ mahāvapuḥ ।। 

samāgato mayā sārdhaṃ praṇipatya mahāmanāḥ 
māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhos tasthau saṃvignamānasaḥ ।। 

pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvataścaiva cāgrataḥ parameśvaram 
praṇipatya mayā sārdhaṃ sasmāra kimidaṃ tviti ।। 

tadā samabhavattatra nādo vai śabdalakṣaṇaḥ 
omomiti suraśreṣṭhāḥ suvyaktaḥ plutalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

kimidaṃ tviti saṃcintya mayā tiṣṭhanmahāsvanam 
liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tadāpaśyatsanātanam ।। 

ādyavarṇamakāraṃ tu ukāraṃ cottare tataḥ 
makāraṃ madhyataścaiva nādāntaṃ tasya caumiti ।। 

sūryamaṇḍalavaddṛṣṭvā varṇamādyaṃ tu dakṣiṇe 
uttare pāvakaprakhyam ukāraṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ ।। 

śītāṃśumaṇḍalaprakhyaṃ makāraṃ madhyamaṃ tathā 
tasyopari tadāpaśyac chuddhasphaṭikavat prabhum ।। 

turīyātītam amṛtaṃ niṣkalaṃ nirupaplavam 
nirdvandvaṃ kevalaṃ śūnyaṃ bāhyābhyantaravarjitam ।। 

sabāhyābhyantaraṃ caiva sabāhyābhyantarasthitam 
ādimadhyāntarahitam ānandasyāpi kāraṇam ।। 

mātrāstisrastvardhamātraṃ nādākhyaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam 
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedā vai mātrārūpeṇa mādhavaḥ ।। 

vedaśabdebhya eveśaṃ viśvātmānamacintayat 
tadābhavadṛṣirveda ṛṣeḥ sāratamaṃ śubham ।। 

tenaiva ṛṣiṇā viṣṇur jñātavān parameśvaram 
cintayā rahito rudro vāco yanmanasā saha ।। 

aprāpya taṃ nivartante vācyastvekākṣareṇa saḥ 
ekākṣareṇa tadvācyam ṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam ।। 

satyamānandamamṛtaṃ paraṃ brahma parātparam 
ekākṣarādakārākhyo bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ ।। 

ekākṣarādukārākhyo hariḥ paramakāraṇam 
ekākṣarānmakārākhyo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।। 

sargakartā tvakārākhyo hy ukārākhyastu mohakaḥ 
makārākhyas tayor nityam anugrahakaro abhavat ।। 

makārākhyo vibhurbījī hy akāro bījamucyate 
ukārākhyo hariryoniḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ ।। 

bījī ca bījaṃ tadyonir nādākhyaś ca maheśvaraḥ 
bījī vibhajya cātmānaṃ svecchayā tu vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

asya liṅgādabhūdbījam akāro bījinaḥ prabhoḥ 
ukārayonau nikṣiptam avardhata samantataḥ ।। 

sauvarṇamabhavaccāṇḍam āveṣṭyādyaṃ tadakṣaram 
anekābdaṃ tathā cāpsu divyamaṇḍaṃ vyavasthitam ।। 

tato varṣasahasrānte dvidhā kṛtamajodbhavam 
aṇḍam apsu sthitaṃ sākṣād ādyākhyeneśvareṇa tu ।। 

tasyāṇḍasya śubhaṃ haimaṃ kapālaṃ cordhvasaṃsthitam 
jajñe yaddyaustadaparaṃ pṛthivī pañcalakṣaṇā ।। 

tasmādaṇḍodbhavo jajñe tv akārākhyaścaturmukhaḥ 
sa sraṣṭā sarvalokānāṃ sa eva trividhaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

evamomomiti proktam ityāhuryajuṣāṃ varāḥ 
yajuṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā ṛcaḥ sāmāni sādaram ।। 

evameva hare brahmann ityāhuḥ śrutayastadā 
tato vijñāya deveśaṃ yathāvacchrutisaṃbhavaiḥ ।। 

mantrairmaheśvaraṃ devaṃ tuṣṭāva sumahodayam 
āvayoḥ stutisaṃtuṣṭo liṅge tasminnirañjanaḥ ।। 

divyaṃ śabdamayaṃ rūpam āsthāya prahasan sthitaḥ 
akārastasya mūrdhā tu lalāṭaṃ dīrghamucyate ।। 

ikāro dakṣiṇaṃ netram īkāro vāmalocanam 
ukāro dakṣiṇaṃ śrotram ūkāro vāmamucyate ।। 

ṛkāro dakṣiṇaṃ tasya kapolaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
vāmaṃ kapolam ṝkāro ḷ ḹ nāsāpuṭe ubhe ।। 

ekāram oṣṭhamūrddhvaś ca aikārastvadharo vibhoḥ 
okāraś ca tathaukāro dantapaṅktidvayaṃ kramāt ।। 

amastu tālunī tasya devadevasya dhīmataḥ 
kādipañcākṣarāṇyasya pañca hastāni dakṣiṇe ।। 

cādipañcākṣarāṇyevaṃ pañca hastāni vāmataḥ 
ṭādipañcākṣaraṃ pādas tādipañcākṣaraṃ tathā ।। 

pakāramudaraṃ tasya phakāraḥ pārśvamucyate 
bakāro vāmapārśvaṃ vai bhakāraṃ skandhamasya tat ।। 

makāraṃ hṛdayaṃ śaṃbhor mahādevasya yoginaḥ 
yakārādisakārāntaṃ vibhorvai sapta dhātavaḥ ।। 

hakāra ātmarūpaṃ vai kṣakāraḥ krodha ucyate 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā umayā sārdhaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram ।। 

praṇamya bhagavān viṣṇuḥ punaścāpaśyadūrddhvataḥ 
oṅkāraprabhavaṃ mantraṃ kalāpañcakasaṃyutam ।। 

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ subhāṣṭatriṃśadakṣaram 
medhākaram abhūdbhūyaḥ sarvadharmārthasādhakam ।। 

gāyatrīprabhavaṃ mantraṃ haritaṃ vaśyakārakam 
caturviṃśativarṇāḍhyaṃ catuṣkalamanuttamam ।। 

atharvamasitaṃ mantraṃ kalāṣṭakasamāyutam 
abhicārikamatyarthaṃ trayastriṃśacchubhākṣaram ।। 

yajurvedasamāyuktaṃ pañcatriṃśacchubhākṣaram 
kalāṣṭakasamāyuktaṃ suśvetaṃ śāntikaṃ tathā ।। 

trayodaśakalāyuktaṃ bālādyaiḥ saha lohitam 
sāmodbhavaṃ jagatyādyaṃ vṛddhisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। 

varṇāḥ ṣaḍadhikāḥ ṣaṣṭir asya mantravarasya tu 
pañca mantrāṃs tathā labdhvā jajāpa bhagavān hariḥ ।। 

atha dṛṣṭvā kalāvarṇam ṛgyajuḥsāmarūpiṇam 
īśānamīśamukuṭaṃ puruṣāsyaṃ purātanam ।। 

aghorahṛdayaṃ hṛdyaṃ vāmaguhyaṃ sadāśivam 
sadyaḥ pādaṃ mahādevaṃ mahābhogīndrabhūṣaṇam ।। 

viśvataḥ pādavadanaṃ viśvato akṣikaraṃ śivam 
brahmaṇo adhipatiṃ sargasthitisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। 

tuṣṭāva punariṣṭābhir vāgbhir varadamīśvaram ।। 

ekākṣarāya rudrāya akārāyātmarūpiṇe 
ukārāyādidevāya vidyādehāya vai namaḥ ।। 

tṛtīyāya makārāya śivāya paramātmane 
sūryāgnisomavarṇāya yajamānāya vai namaḥ ।। 

agnaye rudrarūpāya rudrāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ 
śivāya śivamantrāya sadyojātāya vedhase ।। 

vāmāya vāmadevāya varadāyāmṛtāya te 
aghorāyātighorāya sadyojātāya raṃhase ।। 

īśānāya śmaśānāya ativegāya vegine 
namo astu śrutipādāya ūrdhvaliṅgāya liṅgine ।। 

hemaliṅgāya hemāya vāriliṅgāya cāṃbhase 
śivāya śivaliṅgāya vyāpine vyomavyāpine ।। 

vāyave vāyuvegāya namaste vāyuvyāpine 
tejase tejasāṃ bhartre namastejo adhivyāpine ।। 

jalāya jalabhūtāya namaste jalavyāpine 
pṛthivyai cāntarikṣāya pṛthivīvyāpine namaḥ ।। 

śabdasparśasvarūpāya rasagandhāya gandhine 
gaṇādhipataye tubhyaṃ guhyādguhyatamāya te ।। 

anantāya virūpāya anantānāmayāya ca 
śāśvatāya variṣṭhāya vārigarbhāya yogine ।। 

saṃsthitāyāmbhasāṃ madhye āvayormadhyavarcase 
goptre hartre sadā kartre nidhanāyeśvarāya ca ।। 

acetanāya cintyāya cetanāyāsahāriṇe 
arūpāya surūpāya anaṅgāyāṅgahāriṇe ।। 

bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya bhānusomāgnihetave 
śvetāya śvetavarṇāya tuhinādricarāya ca ।। 

suśvetāya suvaktrāya namaḥ śvetaśikhāya ca 
śvetāsyāya mahāsyāya namaste śvetalohita ।। 

sutārāya viśiṣṭāya namo dundubhine hara 
śatarūpavirūpāya namaḥ ketumate sadā ।। 

ṛddhiśokaviśokāya pinākāya kapardine 
vipāśāya supāśāya namaste pāśanāśine ।। 

suhotrāya haviṣyāya subrahmaṇyāya sūriṇe 
sumukhāya suvaktrāya durdamāya damāya ca ।। 

kaṅkāya kaṅkarūpāya kaṅkaṇīkṛtapannaga 
sanakāya namastubhyaṃ sanātana sanandana ।। 

sanatkumārasāraṅgam āraṇāya mahātmane 
lokākṣiṇe tridhāmāya namo virajase sadā ।। 

śaṅkhapālāya śaṅkhāya rajase tamase namaḥ 
sārasvatāya meghāya meghavāhana te namaḥ ।। 

suvāhāya vivāhāya vivādavaradāya ca 
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya pradhānāya namonamaḥ ।। 

triguṇāya namastubhyaṃ caturvyūhātmane namaḥ 
saṃsārāya namastubhyaṃ namaḥ saṃsārahetave ।। 

mokṣāya mokṣarūpāya mokṣakartre namonamaḥ 
ātmane ṛṣaye tubhyaṃ svāmine viṣṇave namaḥ ।। 

namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ nāgānāṃ pataye namaḥ 
oṅkārāya namastubhyaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। 

sarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ namo nārāyaṇāya ca 
namo hiraṇyagarbhāya ādidevāya te namaḥ ।। 

namo astvajāya pataye prajānāṃ vyūhahetave 
mahādevāya devānām īśvarāya namo namaḥ ।। 

śarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ satyāya śamanāya ca 
brahmaṇe caiva bhūtānāṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। 

mahātmane namastubhyaṃ prajñārūpāya vai namaḥ 
citaye citirūpāya smṛtirūpāya vai namaḥ ।। 

jñānāya jñānagamyāya namaste saṃvide sadā 
śikharāya namastubhyaṃ nīlakaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ ।। 

ardhanārīśarīrāya avyaktāya namonamaḥ 
ekādaśavibhedāya sthāṇave te namaḥ sadā ।। 

namaḥ somāya sūryāya bhavāya bhavahāriṇe 
yaśaskarāya devāya śaṅkarāyeśvarāya ca ।। 

namo aṃbikādhipataye umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ 
hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ namaste hemaretase ।। 

nīlakeśāya vittāya śitikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ 
kapardine namastubhyaṃ nāgāṅgābharaṇāya ca ।। 

vṛṣārūḍhāya sarvasya hartre kartre namonamaḥ 
vīrarāmātirāmāya rāmanāthāya te vibho ।। 

namo rājādhirājāya rājñāmadhigatāya te 
namaḥ pālādhipataye pālāśākṛntate namaḥ ।। 

namaḥ keyūrabhūṣāya gopate te namonamaḥ 
namaḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthāya namo likucapāṇaye ।। 

bhuvaneśāya devāya vedaśāstra namo astu te 
sāraṅgāya namastubhyaṃ rājahaṃsāya te namaḥ ।। 

kanakāṅgadahārāya namaḥ sarpopavītine 
sarpakuṇḍalamālāya kaṭisūtrīkṛtāhine ।। 

vedagarbhāya garbhāya viśvagarbhāya te śiva 
virarāmeti saṃstutvā brahmaṇā sahito hariḥ ।। 

etatstotravaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
yaḥ paṭhecchrāvayedvāpi brāhmaṇān vedapāragān ।। 

sa yāti brahmaṇo loke pāpakarmarato api vai 
tasmājjapetpaṭhennityaṃ śrāvayedbrāhmaṇāñchubhān ।। 

sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam ।। 

athovāca mahādevaḥ prīto ahaṃ surasattamau 
paśyatāṃ māṃ mahādevaṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ vimucyatām ।। 

yuvāṃ prasūtau gātrābhyāṃ mama pūrvaṃ mahābalau 
ayaṃ me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। 

vāme pārśve ca me viṣṇur viśvātmā hṛdayodbhavaḥ 
prīto ahaṃ yuvayoḥ samyag varaṃ dadmi yathepsitam ।। 

evamuktvā tu taṃ viṣṇuṃ karābhyāṃ parameśvaraḥ 
pasparśa subhagābhyāṃ tu kṛpayā tu kṛpānidhiḥ ।। 

tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasā praṇipatya maheśvaram 
prāha nārāyaṇo nāthaṃ liṅgasthaṃ liṅgavarjitam ।। 

yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaś ca nau 
bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī ।। 

devaḥ pradattavān devāḥ svātmanyavyabhicāriṇīm 
brahmaṇe viṣṇave caiva śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

jānubhyāmavanīṃ gatvā punarnārāyaṇaḥ svayam 
praṇipatya ca viśveśaṃ prāha mandataraṃ vaśī ।। 

āvayordevadeveśa vivādamatiśobhanam 
ihāgato bhavān yasmād vivādaśamanāya nau ।। 

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ prāha haro harim 
praṇipatya sthitaṃ mūrdhnā kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ smayan ।। 

pralayasthitisargāṇāṃ kartā tvaṃ dharaṇīpate 
vatsa vatsa hare viṣṇo pālayaitaccarācaram ।। 

tridhā bhinno hyahaṃ viṣṇo brahmaviṣṇubhavākhyayā 
sargarakṣālayaguṇair niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

saṃmohaṃ tyaja bho viṣṇo pālayainaṃ pitāmaham 
pādme bhaviṣyati sutaḥ kalpe tava pitāmahaḥ ।। 

tadā drakṣyasi māṃ caivaṃ so api drakṣyati padmajaḥ 
evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 

tadāprabhṛti lokeṣu liṅgārcā supratiṣṭhitā 
liṅgavedī mahādevī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ ।। 

layanālliṅgamityuktaṃ tatraiva nikhilaṃ surāḥ 
yastu laiṅgaṃ paṭhennityam ākhyānaṃ liṅgasannidhau ।। 

sa yāti śivatāṃ vipro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

kathaṃ pādme purā kalpe brahmā padmodbhavo abhavat 
bhavaṃ ca dṛṣṭavāṃstena brahmaṇā puruṣottamaḥ ।।
