rathādyairvāpi deveśaṃ nītvā rudrālayaṃ prati ।। 

sarvātiśayasaṃyuktaiś chatracāmarabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
nivedayedvrataṃ caiva śivāya parameṣṭhine ।। 

sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nārī devyā yadi prabho 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī ।। 

varṣamekaṃ na bhuñjati kanyā vā vidhavāpi vā 
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ ।। 

pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ dattvā rudrālaye punaḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate ।। 

yā nāryevaṃ caredabdaṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ caturdaśīm 
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā yena kenāpi vā dvijāḥ ।। 

pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate 
amāvāsyāṃ nirāhārā bhavedabdaṃ suyantritā ।। 

śūlaṃ ca vidhinā kṛtvā varṣānte vinivedayet 
snāpyeśānaṃ yajedbhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ ।। 

rājataṃ kamalaṃ caiva jāṃbūnadasukarṇikam 
dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇām api ।। 

kāmato api kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhrūṇahatyādikaṃ ca yat 
tatsarvaṃ śūladānena bhindyānnārī na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

sāyujyaṃ caivamāpnoti bhavānyā dvijasattamāḥ 
kuryādyadvā naraḥ so api rudrasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।। 

paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ varṣamekamatandritā 
upavāsaratā nārī naro api dvijasattamāḥ ।। 

niyogādeva tatkāryaṃ bhartṝṇāṃ dvijasattamāḥ 
japaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ sarvam asvatantrā yataḥ striyaḥ ।। 

varṣānte sarvagandhāḍhyāṃ pratimāṃ saṃnivedayet 
sā bhavānyāś ca sāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ cāpi suvratā ।। 

labhate nātra saṃdehaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmyaham 
kārtikyāṃ vā tu yā nārī ekabhaktena vartate ।। 

kṣamāhiṃsādiniyamaiḥ saṃyuktā brahmacāriṇī 
dadyātkṛṣṇatilānāṃ ca bhāramekam atandritā ।। 

saghṛtaṃ saguḍaṃ caiva odanaṃ parameṣṭhine 
dattvā ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yathā vibhavavistaram ।। 

aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyām upavāsaratā ca sā 
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ sārūpyaṃ prāpya suvratā ।। 

kṣamā satyaṃ dayā dānaṃ śaucamindriyanigrahaḥ 
sarvavrateṣvayaṃ dharmaḥ sāmānyo rudrapūjanam ।। 

samāsādvaḥ pravakṣyāmi pratimāsamanukramāt 
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārttikāntaṃ yathākramam ।। 

vrataṃ suvipulaṃ puṇyaṃ nandinā paribhāṣitam 
mārgaśīrṣakamāse atha vṛṣaṃ pūrṇāṅgamuttamam ।। 

alaṃkṛtya yathānyāyaṃ śivāya vinivedayet 
sā ca sārdhaṃ bhavānyā vai modate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

puṣyamāse tu vai śūlaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya nivedayet 
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate ।। 

māghamāse rathaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam 
dadyāt sampūjya deveśaṃ brāhmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet ।। 

sā ca devyā mahābhāgā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
phālgune pratimāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi ।। 

rājatenāpi tāmreṇa yathāvibhavavistaram 
pratiṣṭhāpya samabhyarcya sthāpayecchaṅkarālaye ।। 

sā ca sārdhaṃ mahādevyā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
caitre bhavaṃ kumāraṃ ca bhavānīṃ ca yathāvidhi ।। 

tāmrādyairvidhivatkṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi 
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave ।। 

kṛtvālayaṃ hi kauberaṃ rājataṃ rajatena vai 
īśvaromāsamāyuktaṃ gaṇeśaiś ca samantataḥ ।। 

sarvaratnasamāyuktaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi 
sthāpayetparameśasya bhavasyāyatane śubhe ।। 

vaiśākhe vai cared evaṃ kailāsākhyaṃ vratottamam 
kailāsaparvataṃ prāpya bhavānyā saha modate ।। 

jyeṣṭhe māsi mahādevaṃ liṅgamūrtimumāpatim 
kṛtāñjalipuṭenaiva brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā ।। 

madhye bhavena saṃyuktaṃ liṅgamūrti dvijottamāḥ 
haṃsena ca varāheṇa kṛtvā tāmrādibhiḥ śubhām ।। 

pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ 
śivāya śivamāsādya śivasthāne yathāvidhi ।। 

brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitāṃ sthāpya devyāḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt 
āṣāḍhe ca śubhe māse gṛhaṃ kṛtvā suśobhanam ।। 

pakveṣṭakābhir vidhivad yathāvibhavavistaram 
sarvabījarasaiścāpi sampūrṇaṃ sarvaśobhanaiḥ ।। 

gṛhopakaraṇaiścaiva musalolūkhalādibhiḥ 
dāsīdāsādibhiścaiva śayanairaśanādibhiḥ ।। 

sampūrṇaiś ca gṛhaṃ vastrair ācchādya ca samantataḥ 
devaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevamumāpatim ।। 

brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayitvā yathāvidhi 
vidyāvinayasampannaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam ।। 

prathamāśramiṇaṃ bhaktyā sampūjya ca yathāvidhi 
kanyāṃ sumadhyamāṃ yāvat kālajīvanasaṃyutām ।। 

kṣetraṃ gomithunaṃ caiva tadgṛhe ca nivedayet 
sāyanair vividhair divyair meruparvatasannibhaiḥ ।। 

golokaṃ samanuprāpya bhavānyā saha modate 
bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarvakalpeṣu sāvyayā ।। 

bhavānyāścaiva sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
sarvadhātusamākīrṇaṃ vicitradhvajaśobhitam ।। 

nivedayīta śarvāya śrāvaṇe tilaparvatam 
vitānadhvajavastrādyair dhātubhiś ca nivedayet ।। 

brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet 
kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanaṃ śāliparvatam ।। 

vitānadhvajavastrādyair dhātubhiś ca nivedayet 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayecca yathāvidhi ।। 

sā ca sūryāṃśusaṃkāśā bhavānyā saha modate 
kṛtvā cāśvayuje māsi vipulaṃ dhānyaparvatam ।। 

suvarṇavastrasaṃyuktaṃ dattvā sampūjya śaṅkaram 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet ।। 

sarvadhānyasamāyuktaṃ sarvabījarasādibhiḥ 
sarvadhātusamāyuktaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam ।। 

śṛṅgaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ vitānacchatraśobhitam 
gandhamālyais tathā dhūpaiś citraiścāpi suśobhitam ।। 

vicitrairnṛtyageyaiś ca śaṅkhavīṇādibhis tathā 
brahmaghoṣairmahāpuṇyaṃ maṅgalaiś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। 

mahādhvajāṣṭasaṃyuktaṃ vicitrakusumojjvalam 
nagendraṃ merunāmānaṃ trailokyādhāramuttamam ।। 

tasya mūrdhni śivaṃ kuryān madhyato dhātunaiva tu 
dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca caturmukham ।। 

uttare devadeveśaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam 
indrādilokapālāṃś ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi ।। 

pratiṣṭhāpya tataḥ snāpya samabhyarcya maheśvaram 
devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlaṃ tridaśapūjitam ।। 

vāme pāśaṃ bhavānyāś ca kamalaṃ hemabhūṣitam 
viṣṇoś ca śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ ca gadāmabjaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। 

brahmaṇaścākṣasūtraṃ ca kamaṇḍalumanuttamam 
indrasya vajram agneś ca śaktyākhyaṃ paramāyudham ।। 

yamasya daṇḍaṃ nirṛteḥ khaḍgaṃ niśicarasya tu 
varuṇasya mahāpāśaṃ nāgākhyaṃ rudramadbhutam ।। 

vāyor yaṣṭiṃ kuberasya gadāṃ lokaprapūjitām 
ṭaṅkaṃ ceśānadevasya nivedyaivaṃ krameṇa ca ।। 

śivasya mahatīṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā carusamanvitām 
pūjayetsarvadevāṃś ca yathāvibhavavistaram ।। 

brāhmaṇānbhojayitvā ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ 
mahāmeruvrataṃ kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet ।। 

mahāmerumanuprāpya mahādevyā pramodate 
ciraṃ sāyujyam āpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

kārtikyāmapi yā nārī kṛtvā devīmumāṃ śubhām 
sarvābharaṇasampūrṇāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām ।। 

hematāmrādibhiścaiva pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ 
devaṃ ca kṛtvā deveśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। 

tayoragre hutāśaṃ ca sruvahastaṃ pitāmaham 
nārāyaṇaṃ ca dātāraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।। 

lokapālais tathā siddhaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ sthāpya yatnataḥ 
rudrālaye vrataṃ tasmai dāpayedbhaktipūrvakam ।। 

sā bhavānyāstanuṃ gatvā bhavena saha modate 
ekabhaktavrataṃ puṇyaṃ pratimāsamanukramāt ।। 

mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārtikāntaṃ pravartitam 
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ ।। 

naraḥ kṛtvā vrataṃ caiva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāmaheśvaravrataṃ nāma caturaśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

sarvavrateṣu sampūjya devadevamumāpatim 
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ ।। 

japādeva na saṃdeho vratānāṃ vai viśeṣataḥ 
samāptirnānyathā tasmāj japetpañcākṣarīṃ śubhām ।। 

kathaṃ pañcākṣarī vidyā prabhāvo vā kathaṃ vada 
kramopāyaṃ mahābhāga śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। 

purā devena rudreṇa devadevena śaṃbhunā 
pārvatyāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ pravadāmi samāsataḥ ।। 

bhagavandevadeveśa sarvalokamaheśvara 
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ ।। 

pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi 
na śakyaṃ kathituṃ devi tasmāt saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu ।। 

pralaye samanuprāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame 
naṣṭe devāsure caiva naṣṭe coragarākṣase ।। 

sarvaṃ prakṛtimāpannaṃ tvayā pralayameṣyati 
eko ahaṃ saṃsthito devi na dvitīyo asti kutracit ।। 

tasminvedāś ca śāstrāṇi mantre pañcākṣare sthitāḥ 
te nāśaṃ naiva samprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ ।। 

ahameko dvidhāpyāsaṃ prakṛtyātmaprabhedataḥ 
sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum ।। 

āsthāya yogaparyaṅkaśayane toyamadhyagaḥ 
tannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। 

sisṛkṣamāṇo lokānvai trīnaśakto asahāyavān 
daśa brahmā sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ ।। 

teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiprasiddhyarthaṃ māṃ provāca pitāmahaḥ 
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara ।। 

iti tena samādiṣṭaḥ pañcavaktradharo hyaham 
pañcākṣarānpañcamukhaiḥ proktavān padmayonaye ।। 

tānpañcavadanairgṛhṇan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānparameśvaram ।। 

vācyaḥ pañcākṣarairdevi śivastrailokyapūjitaḥ 
vācakaḥ paramo mantras tasya pañcākṣaraḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

jñātvā prayogaṃ vidhinā ca siddhiṃ labdhvā tathā pañcamukho mahātmā 
provāca putreṣu jagaddhitāya mantraṃ mahārthaṃ kila pañcavarṇam ।। 

te labdhvā mantraratnaṃ tu sākṣāllokapitāmahāt 
tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ parātparataraṃ śivam ।। 

tatastutoṣa bhagavān trimūrtīnāṃ paraḥ śivaḥ 
dattavānakhilaṃ jñānam aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam ।। 

te api labdhvā varānviprās tadārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ 
merostu śikhare ramye muñjavānnāma parvataḥ ।। 

matpriyaḥ satataṃ śrīmān madbhūtaiḥ parirakṣitaḥ 
tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokasṛṣṭisamutsukāḥ ।। 

divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran 
tiṣṭhanto anugrahārthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā ।। 

teṣāṃ bhaktimahaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ pratyakṣatāmiyām 
pañcākṣaram ṛṣicchando daivataṃ śaktibījavat ।। 

nyāsaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ digbandhaṃ viniyogamaśeṣataḥ 
proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 

tacchrutvā mantramāhātmyam ṛṣayaste tapodhanāḥ 
mantrasya viniyogaṃ ca kṛtvā sarvamanuṣṭhitāḥ ।। 

tanmāhātmyāt tadā lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān 
varṇānvarṇavibhāgāṃś ca sarvadharmāṃś ca śobhanān ।। 

pūrvakalpasamudbhūtāñ chrutavanto yathā purā 
pañcākṣaraprabhāvācca lokā vedā maharṣayaḥ ।। 

tiṣṭhanti śāśvatā dharmā devāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat 
tad idānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu cāvahitākhilam ।। 

alpākṣaraṃ mahārthaṃ ca vedasāraṃ vimuktidam 
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam ।। 

nānāsiddhiyutaṃ divyaṃ lokacittānurañjakam 
suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ me pārameśvaram ।। 

mantraṃ mukhasukhoccāryam aśeṣārthaprasādhakam 
tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ suśobhanam ।। 

atisūkṣmaṃ mahārthaṃ ca jñeyaṃ tadvaṭabījavat 
vedaḥ sa triguṇātītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛtprabhuḥ ।। 

omityekākṣaraṃ mantraṃ sthitaḥ sarvagataḥ śivaḥ 
mantre ṣaḍakṣare sūkṣme pañcākṣaratanuḥ śivaḥ ।। 

vācyavācakabhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣātsvabhāvataḥ 
vācyaḥ śivaḥ prameyatvān mantrastadvācakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

vācyavācakabhāvo ayam anādiḥ saṃsthitastayoḥ 
vede śivāgame vāpi yatra yatra ṣaḍakṣaraḥ ।। 

mantraḥ sthitaḥ sadā mukhyo loke pañcākṣaro mataḥ 
kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantraiḥ śāstrairvā bahuvistṛtaiḥ ।। 

yasyaivaṃ hṛdi saṃstho ayaṃ mantraḥ syātpārameśvaraḥ 
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam ।। 

yo vidvānvai japetsamyag adhītyaiva vidhānataḥ 
etāvaddhi śivajñānam etāvatparamaṃ padam ।। 

etāvad brahmavidyā ca tasmānnityaṃ japedbudhaḥ 
pañcākṣaraiḥ sapraṇavo mantro ayaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama ।। 

guhyādguhyataraṃ sākṣān mokṣajñānam anuttamam 
asya mantrasya vakṣyāmi ṛṣicchando adhidaivatam ।। 

bījaṃ śaktiṃ svaraṃ varṇaṃ sthānaṃ caivākṣaraṃ prati 
vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiśchanda udāhṛtaḥ ।। 

devatā śiva evāhaṃ mantrasyāsya varānane 
nakārādīni bījāni pañcabhūtātmakāni ca ।। 

ātmānaṃ praṇavaṃ viddhi sarvavyāpinamavyayam 
śaktistvameva deveśi sarvadevanamaskṛte ।। 

tvadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ kiṃcin madīyaṃ praṇavaṃ tathā 
tvadīyaṃ devi mantrāṇāṃ śaktibhūtaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

akārokāramakārā madīye praṇave sthitāḥ 
ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca akāraṃ ca krameṇa vai ।। 

tvadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ viddhi trimātraṃ plutamuttamam 
oṅkārasya svarodātta ṛṣirbrahma sitaṃ vapuḥ ।। 

chando devī ca gāyatrī paramātmādhidevatā 
udāttaḥ prathamastadvac caturthaś ca dvitīyakaḥ ।। 

pañcamaḥ svaritaścaiva madhyamo niṣadhaḥ smṛtāḥ 
nakāraḥ pītavarṇaś ca sthānaṃ pūrvamukhaṃ smṛtam ।। 

indro adhidaivataṃ chando gāyatrī gautama ṛṣiḥ 
makāraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇo asya sthānaṃ vai dakṣiṇāmukham ।। 

chando anuṣṭup ṛṣiścātrī rudro daivatamucyate 
śikāro dhūmravarṇo asya sthānaṃ vai paścimaṃ mukham ।। 

viśvāmitra ṛṣistriṣṭup chando viṣṇustu daivatam 
vākāro hemavarṇo asya sthānaṃ caivottaraṃ mukham ।। 

brahmādhidaivataṃ chando bṛhatī cāṅgirā ṛṣiḥ 
yakāro raktavarṇaś ca sthānam ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ virāṭ ।। 

chanda ṛṣirbharadvājaḥ skando daivatamucyate 
nyāsamasya pravakṣyāmi sarvasiddhikaraṃ śubham ।। 

sarvapāpaharaṃ caiva trividho nyāsa ucyate 
utpattisthitisaṃhārabhedatastrividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ kramaśo bhavet 
utpattirbrahmacāriṇāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ sthitiḥ sadā ।। 

yatīnāṃ saṃhṛtir nyāsaḥ siddhir bhavati nānyathā 
aṅganyāsaḥ karanyāso dehanyāsa iti tridhā ।। 

utpattyāditribhedena vakṣyate te varānane 
nyasetpūrvaṃ karanyāsaṃ dehanyāsam anantaram ।। 

aṅganyāsaṃ tataḥ paścād akṣarāṇāṃ vidhikramāt 
mūrdhādipādaparyantam utpattinyāsa ucyate ।। 

pādādimūrdhaparyantaṃ saṃhāro bhavati priye 
hṛdayāsyagalanyāsaḥ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ।। 

brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ caiva śobhane 
saśiraskaṃ tato dehaṃ sarvamantreṇa saṃspṛśet ।। 

sa dehanyāsa ityuktaḥ sarveṣāṃ sama eva sa 
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṅguṣṭhānta eva hi ।। 

nyasyate yattadutpattir viparītaṃ tu saṃhṛtiḥ 
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ nyasyate hastayor dvayoḥ ।। 

atīva bhogado devi sthitinyāsaḥ kuṭuṃbinām 
karanyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā dehanyāsam anantaram ।। 

aṅganyāsaṃ nyasetpaścād eṣa sādhāraṇo vidhiḥ 
oṅkāraṃ saṃpuṭīkṛtya sarvāṅgeṣu ca vinyaset ।। 

karayorubhayoścaiva daśāgrāṃguliṣu kramāt 
prakṣālya pādāvācamya śucirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।। 

prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi nyāsakarma samācaret 
smaret pūrvam ṛṣiṃ chando daivataṃ bījameva ca ।। 

śaktiṃ ca paramātmānaṃ guruṃ caiva varānane 
mantreṇa pāṇī saṃmṛjya talayoḥ praṇavaṃ nyaset ।। 

aṅgulīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tathā cādyantaparvasu 
sabindukāni bījāni pañca madhyamaparvasu ।। 

utpattyāditribhedena nyasedāśramataḥ kramāt 
ubhābhyāmeva pāṇibhyām āpādatalamastakam ।। 

mantreṇa saṃspṛśeddehaṃ praṇavenaiva saṃpuṭam 
mūrdhni vaktre ca kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye guhyake tathā ।। 

pādayor ubhayoścaiva guhye ca hṛdaye tathā 
kaṇṭhe ca mukhamadhye ca mūrdhni ca praṇavādikam ।। 

hṛdaye guhyake caiva pādayormūrdhni vāci vā 
kaṇṭhe caiva nyasedeva praṇavāditribhedataḥ ।। 

kṛtvāṅganyāsamevaṃ hi mukhāni parikalpayet 
pūrvādi cordhvaparyantaṃ nakārādi yathākramam ।। 

ṣaḍaṅgāni nyasetpaścād yathāsthānaṃ ca śobhanam 
namaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍḍhuṃ ca vauṣaṭphaṭkārakaiḥ saha ।। 

praṇavaṃ hṛdayaṃ vidyān nakāraḥ śira ucyate 
śikhā makāra ākhyātaḥ śikāraḥ kavacaṃ tathā ।। 

ākāro netramastraṃ tu yakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
itthamaṅgāni vinyasya tato vai bandhayeddiśaḥ ।। 

vighneśo mātaro durgā kṣetrajño devatā diśaḥ 
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu caturṣvapi yathākramam ।। 

aṅguṣṭhatarjanyagrābhyāṃ saṃsthāpya sumukhaṃ śubham 
rakṣadhvamiti coktvā tu namaskuryātpṛthakpṛthak ।। 

gale madhye tathāṅguṣṭhe tarjanyādyāṅgulīṣu ca 
aṅguṣṭhena karanyāsaṃ kuryādeva vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

evaṃ nyāsamimaṃ proktaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham 
sarvasiddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvarakṣākaraṃ śivam ।। 

nyaste mantre atha subhage śaṅkarapratimo bhavet 
janmāntarakṛtaṃ pāpam api naśyati tatkṣaṇāt ।। 

evaṃ vinyasya medhāvī śuddhakāyo dṛḍhavrataḥ 
japetpañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ ।। 

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mantrasaṃgrahaṇaṃ śubhe 
yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ nityaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet ।। 

ājñāhīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnam amānasam 
ājñaptaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam ।। 

ājñāsiddhaṃ kriyāsiddhaṃ śraddhāsiddhaṃ sumānasam 
evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāsiddhaṃ mantraṃ siddhaṃ yatastataḥ ।। 

upāgamya guruṃ vipraṃ mantratattvārthavedinam 
jñāninaṃ sadguṇopetaṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇam ।। 

toṣayettaṃ prayatnena bhāvaśuddhisamanvitaḥ 
vācā ca manasā caiva kāyena draviṇena ca ।। 

ācāryaṃ pūjayecchiṣyaḥ sarvadātiprayatnataḥ 
hastyaśvaratharatnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca ।। 

bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni vividhāni ca 
etāni gurave dadyād bhaktyā ca vibhave sati ।। 

vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ 
paścānnivedayeddevi ātmānaṃ saparicchadam ।। 

evaṃ sampūjya vidhivad yathāśakti tvavañcayan 
ādadīta gurormantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva krameṇa tu ।। 

evaṃ tuṣṭo guruḥ śiṣyaṃ pūjitaṃ vatsaroṣitam 
śuśrūṣum anahaṅkāram upavāsakṛśaṃ śucim ।। 

snāpayitvā tu śiṣyāya brāhmaṇānapi pūjya ca 
samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā ।। 

śucau deśe gṛhe vāpi kāle siddhikare tithau 
nakṣatre śubhayoge ca sarvadā doṣavarjite ।। 

anugṛhya tato dadyāc chivajñānam anuttamam 
svareṇoccārayet samyag ekānte api prasannadhīḥ ।। 

uccāryoccārayitvā tu ācāryaḥ siddhidaḥ svayam 
śivaṃ cāstu śubhaṃ cāstu śobhano astu priyo astviti ।। 

evaṃ labdhvā paraṃ mantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva gurostataḥ 
japennityaṃ sasaṃkalpaṃ puraścaraṇameva ca ।। 

yāvajjīvaṃ japennityam aṣṭottarasahasrakam 
anaśnaṃstatparo bhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

japedakṣaralakṣaṃ vai caturguṇitamādarāt 
naktāśī saṃyamī yaś ca pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

puraścaraṇajāpī vā api vā nityajāpakaḥ 
acirātsiddhikāṅkṣī tu tayoranyataro bhavet ।। 

yaḥ puraścaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nityajāpī bhavennaraḥ 
tasya nāsti samo loke sa siddhaḥ siddhido vaśī ।। 

āsanaṃ ruciraṃ baddhvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ 
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi japenmantramanuttamam ।। 

ādyāntayor japasyāpi kuryādvai prāṇasaṃyamān 
tathā cānte japedbījaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ śubham ।। 

catvāriṃśatsamāvṛtti prāṇānāyamya saṃsmaret 
pañcākṣarasya mantrasya prāṇāyāma udāhṛtaḥ ।। 

prāṇāyāmādbhavetkṣipraṃ sarvapāpaparikṣayaḥ 
indriyāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tasmātprāṇāṃś ca saṃyamet ।। 

gṛhe japaḥ samaṃ vidyād goṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ bhavet 
nadyāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu anantaḥ śivasannidhau ।। 

samudratīre devahrade girau devālayeṣu ca 
puṇyāśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭiguṇo bhavet ।। 

śivasya saṃnidhāne ca sūryasyāgre gurorapi 
dīpasya gorjalasyāpi japakarma praśasyate ।। 

aṅgulījapasaṃkhyānam ekamekaṃ śubhānane 
rekhairaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktaṃ putrajīvaphalair daśa ।। 

śataṃ vai śaṅkhamaṇibhiḥ pravālaiś ca sahasrakam 
sphāṭikair daśasāhasraṃ mauktikairlakṣamucyate ।। 

padmākṣairdaśalakṣaṃ tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate 
kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣair anantaguṇamucyate ।। 

pañcaviṃśati mokṣārthaṃ saptaviṃśati pauṣṭikam 
triṃśacca dhanasaṃpattyai pañcāśaccābhicārikam ।। 

tatpūrvābhimukhaṃ vaśyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cābhicārikam 
paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyād uttaraṃ śāntikaṃ bhavet ।। 

aṅguṣṭhaṃ mokṣadaṃ vidyāt tarjanī śatrunāśanī 
madhyamā dhanadā śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hy anāmikā ।। 

kaniṣṭhā rakṣaṇīyā sā japakarmaṇi śobhane 
aṅguṣṭhena japejjapyam anyairaṅgulibhiḥ saha ।। 

aṅguṣṭhena vinā karma kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ yataḥ 
śṛṇuṣva sarvayajñebhyo japayajño viśiṣyate ।। 

hiṃsayā te pravartante japayajño na hiṃsayā 
yāvantaḥ karmayajñāḥ syuḥ pradānāni tapāṃsi ca ।। 

sarve te japayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm 
māhātmyaṃ vācikasyaiva japayajñasya kīrtitam ।। 

tasmācchataguṇopāṃśuḥ sahasro mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ 
yad uccanīcasvaritaiḥ śabdaiḥ spaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ ।। 

mantramuccārayedvācā japayajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ 
śanairuccārayenmantram īṣad oṣṭhau tu cālayet ।। 

kiṃcit karṇāntaraṃ vidyād upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ 
dhiyā yadakṣaraśreṇyā varṇādvarṇaṃ padātpadam ।। 

śabdārthaṃ cintayedbhūyaḥ sa tūkto mānaso japaḥ 
trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyān syāduttarottaraḥ ।। 

bhavedyajñaviśeṣeṇa vaiśiṣṭyaṃ tatphalasya ca 
japena devatā nityaṃ stūyamānā prasīdati ।। 

prasannā vipulān bhogān dadyānmuktiṃ ca śāśvatīm 
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca grahāḥ sarve ca bhīṣaṇāḥ 
jāpinaṃ nopasarpanti bhayabhītāḥ samantataḥ ।। 
japena pāpaṃ śamayedaśeṣaṃ yattatkṛtaṃ janmaparaṃparāsu । 
japena bhogān jayate ca mṛtyuṃ japena siddhiṃ labhate ca muktim ।। 

evaṃ labdhvā śivaṃ jñānaṃ jñātvā japavidhikramam ।। 

sadācārī japannityaṃ dhyāyan bhadraṃ samaśnute 
sadācāraṃ pravakṣyāmi samyagdharmasya sādhanam ।। 

yasmādācārahīnasya sādhanaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet 
ācāraḥ paramo dharma ācāraḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। 

ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ 
sadācāravatāṃ puṃsāṃ sarvatrāpyabhayaṃ bhavet ।। 

tadvadācārahīnānāṃ sarvatraiva bhayaṃ bhavet 
sadācāreṇa devatvam ṛṣitvaṃ ca varānane ।। 

upayānti kuyonitvaṃ tadvad ācāralaṅghanāt 
ācārahīnaḥ puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ ।। 

tasmātsaṃsiddhimanvicchan samyagācāravān bhavet 
durvṛttaḥ śuddhibhūyiṣṭhaḥ pāpīyān jñānadūṣakaḥ ।। 

varṇāśramavidhānoktaṃ dharmaṃ kurvīta yatnataḥ ।। 

yasya yadvihitaṃ karma tatkurvanmatpriyaḥ sadā 
saṃdhyopāsanaśīlaḥ syāt sāyaṃ prātaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।। 

udayāstamayātpūrvam āramya vidhinā śuciḥ 
kāmānmohādbhayāllobhāt saṃdhyāṃ nātikrameddvijaḥ ।। 

saṃdhyātikramaṇādvipro brāhmaṇyātpatate yataḥ 
asatyaṃ na vadet kiṃcin na satyaṃ ca parityajet ।। 

yatsatyaṃ brahma ityāhur asatyaṃ brahmadūṣaṇam 
anṛtaṃ paruṣaṃ śāṭhyaṃ paiśunyaṃ pāpahetukam ।। 

paradārānparadravyaṃ parahiṃsāṃ ca sarvadā 
kvaciccāpi na kurvīta vācā ca manasā tathā ।। 

śūdrānnaṃ yātayāmānnaṃ naivedyaṃ śrāddhameva ca 
gaṇānnaṃ samudāyānnaṃ rājānnaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। 

annaśuddhau sattvaśuddhir na mṛdā na jalena vai 
sattvaśuddhau bhavetsiddhis tato annaṃ pariśodhayet ।। 

rājapratigrahair dagdhān brāhmaṇān brahmavādinaḥ 
svinnānāmapi bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate ।। 

rājapratigraho ghoro buddhvā cādau viṣopamaḥ 
budhena parihartavyaḥ śvamāṃsaṃ cāpi varjayet ।। 

asnātvā na ca bhuñjīyād ajapo agnimapūjya ca 
parṇapṛṣṭhe na bhuñjīyād rātrau dīpaṃ vinā tathā ।। 

bhinnabhāṇḍe ca rathyāyāṃ patitānāṃ ca saṃnidhau 
śūdraśeṣaṃ na bhuñjīyāt sahānnaṃ śiśukairapi ।। 

śuddhānnaṃ snigdham aśnīyāt saṃskṛtaṃ cābhimantritam 
bhoktā śiva iti smṛtvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ ।। 

āsyena na pibettoyaṃ tiṣṭhannañjalināpi vā 
vāmahastena śayyāyāṃ tathaivānyaṃkareṇa vā ।। 

vibhītakārkakārañjasnuhicchāyāṃ na cāśrayet 
staṃbhadīpamanuṣyāṇām anyeṣāṃ prāṇināṃ tathā ।। 

eko na gacchedadhvānaṃ bāhubhyāṃ nottarennadīm 
nāvaroheta kūpādiṃ nāroheduccapādapān ।। 

sūryāgnijaladevānāṃ gurūṇāṃ vimukhaḥ śubhe 
na kuryādiha kāryāṇi japakarma śubhāni vā ।। 

agnau na tāpayetpādau hastaṃ padbhyāṃ na saṃspṛśet 
agnernocchrayam āsīta nāgnau kiṃcin malaṃ tyajet ।। 

na jalaṃ tāḍayetpadbhyāṃ nāṃbhasyaṅgamalaṃ tyajet 
malaṃ prakṣālayet tīre prakṣālya snānamācaret ।। 

nakhāgrakeśanirdhūtasnānavastraghaṭodakam 
aśrīkaraṃ manuṣyāṇām aśuddhaṃ saṃspṛśedyadi ।। 

ajāśvānakhuroṣṭrāṇāṃ mārjanāt tuṣareṇukān 
saṃspṛśed yadi mūḍhātmā śriyaṃ hanti harerapi ।। 

mārjāraś ca gṛhe yasya so apyantyajasamo naraḥ 
bhojayedyastu viprendrān mārjārasaṃnidhau yadi ।। 

taccāṇḍālasamaṃ jñeyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
sphigvātaṃ śūrpavātaṃ ca vātaṃ prāṇamukhānilam ।। 

sukṛtāni harantyete saṃspṛṣṭāḥ puruṣasya tu 
uṣṇīṣī kañcukī nagno muktakeśo malāvṛtaḥ ।। 

apavitrakaro aśuddhaḥ pralapanna japet kvacit 
krodho madaḥ kṣudhā tandrā niṣṭhīvanavijṛmbhaṇe ।। 

śvanīcadarśanaṃ nidrā pralāpāste japadviṣaḥ 
eteṣāṃ saṃbhave vāpi kuryātsūryādidarśanam ।। 

ācamya vā japeccheṣaṃ kṛtvā vā prāṇasaṃyamam 
sūryo agniścandramāścaiva grahanakṣatratārakāḥ ।। 

ete jyotīṃṣi proktāni vidvadbhir brāhmaṇais tathā 
prasārya pādau na japet kukkuṭāsana eva ca ।। 

anāsanaḥ śayāno vā rathyāyāṃ śūdrasannidhau 
raktabhūmyāṃ ca khaṭvāyāṃ na japejjāpakas tathā ।। 

āsanastho japetsamyak mantrārthagatamānasaḥ 
kauśeyaṃ vyāghracarmaṃ vā cailaṃ taulamathāpi vā ।। 

dāravaṃ tālaparṇaṃ vā āsanaṃ parikalpayet 
trisaṃdhyaṃ tu guroḥ pūjā kartavyā hitamicchatā ।। 

yo guruḥ sa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ 
yathā śivas tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ ।। 

śivavidyāgurostasmād bhaktyā ca sadṛśaṃ phalam 
sarvadevamayo devi sarvaśaktimayo hi saḥ ।। 

saguṇo nirguṇo vāpi tasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet 
śreyo arthī yastu gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet ।। 

gurvājñāpālakaḥ samyak jñānasaṃpattimaśnute 
gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapan bhuñjan yadyatkarma samācaret ।। 

samakṣaṃ yadi tatsarvaṃ kartavyaṃ gurvanujñayā 
gurordevasamakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet ।। 

gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāt tadgṛhaṃ devamandiram 
pāpinā ca yathāsaṃgāt tatpāpaiḥ patanaṃ bhavet ।। 

tadvadācāryasaṃgena taddharmaphalabhāgbhavet 
yathaiva vahnisaṃparkān malaṃ tyajati kāñcanam ।। 

tathaiva gurusaṃparkāt pāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ 
yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakuṃbho vilīyate ।। 

tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta ācāryasya samīpataḥ 
yathā prajvalito vahnir viṣṭhāṃ kāṣṭhaṃ ca nirdahet ।। 

gurustuṣṭo dahatyevaṃ pāpaṃ tanmantratejasā 
brahmā haris tathā rudro devāś ca munayas tathā ।। 

kurvantyanugrahaṃ tuṣṭā gurau tuṣṭe na saṃśayaḥ 
karmaṇā manasā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet ।। 

tasya krodhena dahyante āyuḥśrījñānasatkriyāḥ 
tatkrodhaṃ ye kariṣyanti teṣāṃ yajñāś ca niṣphalāḥ ।। 

japānyaniyamāścaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
gurorviruddhaṃ yadvākyaṃ na vadetsarvayatnataḥ ।। 

vaded yadi mahāmohād rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet 
cittenaiva ca vittena tathā vācā ca suvratāḥ ।। 

mithyā na kārayeddevi kriyayā ca guroḥ sadā 
durguṇe khyāpite tasya nairguṇyaśatabhāgbhavet ।। 

guṇe tu khyāpite tasya sārvaguṇyaphalaṃ bhavet 
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryād ādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā ।। 

asamakṣaṃ samakṣaṃ vā guroḥ kāryaṃ samācaret 
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryān manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ ।। 

kurvanpatatyadho gatvā tatraiva parivartate 
tasmātsa sarvadopāsyo vandanīyaś ca sarvadā ।। 

samīpastho apyanujñāpya vadettadvimukho gurum 
evamācāravān bhakto nityaṃ japaparāyaṇaḥ ।। 

gurupriyakaro mantraṃ viniyoktuṃ tato arhati 
viniyogaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhamantraprayojanam ।। 

daurbalyaṃ yāti tanmantraṃ viniyogamajānataḥ 
yasya yena viyuñjīta kāryeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ ।। 

viniyogaḥ sa vijñeya aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam 
viniyogajamāyuṣyam ārogyaṃ tanunityatā ।। 

rājyaiśvaryaṃ ca vijñānaṃ svargo nirvāṇa eva ca 
prokṣaṇaṃ cābhiṣekaṃ ca aghamarṣaṇameva ca ।। 

snāne ca saṃdhyayoścaiva kuryādekādaśena vai 
śuciḥ parvatamāruhya japellakṣamatandritaḥ ।। 

mahānadyāṃ dvilakṣaṃ tu dīrghamāyuravāpnuyāt 
dūrvāṅkurāstilā vāṇī guḍūcī ghuṭikā tathā ।। 

teṣāṃ tu daśasāhasraṃ homamāyuṣyavardhanam 
aśvatthavṛkṣamāśritya japellakṣadvayaṃ sudhīḥ ।। 

śanaiścaradine spṛṣṭvā dīrghāyuṣyaṃ labhennaraḥ 
śanaiścaradine aśvatthaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ saṃspṛśetsudhīḥ ।। 

japedaṣṭottaraśataṃ somamṛtyuharo bhavet 
ādityābhimukho bhūtvā japellakṣamananyadhīḥ ।। 

arkairaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā juhvanvyādhervimucyate 
samastavyādhiśāntyarthaṃ palāśasamidhair naraḥ ।। 

hutvā daśasahasraṃ tu nirogī manujo bhavet 
nityamaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā pibed ambho arkasannidhau ।। 

audaryairvyādhibhiḥ sarvair māsenaikena mucyate 
ekādaśena bhuñjīyād annaṃ caivābhimantritam ।। 

bhakṣyaṃ cānyattathā peyaṃ viṣamapyamṛtaṃ bhavet 
japel lakṣaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe hutvā cāṣṭaśatena vai ।। 

sūryaṃ nityamupasthāya samyagārogyamāpnuyāt 
nadītoyena sampūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ saṃspṛśya śobhanam ।। 

japtvāyutaṃ ca tatsnānād rogāṇāṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavet 
aṣṭāviṃśajjapitvānnam aśnīyād anvahaṃ śuciḥ ।। 

hutvā ca tāvatpālāśair evaṃ vārogyam aśnute 
candrasūryagrahe pūrvam upoṣya vidhinā śuciḥ ।। 

yāvadgrahaṇamokṣaṃ tu tāvannadyāṃ samāhitaḥ 
japetsamudragāminyāṃ vimokṣe grahaṇasya tu ।। 

aṣṭottarasahasreṇa pibedbrāhmīrasaṃ dvijāḥ 
aihikāṃ labhate medhāṃ sarvaśāstradharāṃ śubhām ।। 

sārasvatī bhaveddevī tasya vāgatimānuṣī 
grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu japedbhaktyāyutaṃ naraḥ ।। 

hutvā cāṣṭasahasraṃ tu grahapīḍāṃ vyapohati 
duḥsvapnadarśane snātvā japedvai cāyutaṃ naraḥ ।। 

ghṛtenāṣṭaśataṃ hutvā sadyaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati 
candrasūryagrahe liṅgaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi ।। 

yat kiṃcit prārthayed devi japedayutamādarāt 
saṃnidhāvasya devasya śuciḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ ।। 

sarvānkāmānavāpnoti puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ 
gajānāṃ turagāṇāṃ tu gojātīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। 

vyādhyāgame śucirbhūtvā juhuyātsamidhāhutim 
māsamabhyarcya vidhinā-yutaṃ bhaktisamanvitaḥ ।। 

teṣāmṛddhiś ca śāntiś ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
utpāte śatrubādhāyāṃ juhuyādayutaṃ śuciḥ ।। 

pālāśasamidhair devi tasya śāntirbhaviṣyati 
ābhicārikabādhāyām etaddevi samācaret ।। 

pratyag bhavati tacchaktiḥ śatroḥ pīḍā bhaviṣyati 
vidveṣaṇārthaṃ juhuyād vaibhītasamidhāṣṭakam ।। 

akṣarapratilomyena ārdreṇa rudhireṇa vā 
viṣeṇa rudhirābhyakto vidveṣaṇakaraṃ nṛṇām ।। 

prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpaviśuddhaye 
pāpaśuddhiryathā samyak kartumabhyudyato naraḥ ।। 

pāpaśuddhir yataḥ samyag jñānasaṃpattihaitukī 
pāpaśuddhirna cetpuṃsaḥ kriyāḥ sarvāścaniṣphalāḥ ।। 

jñānaṃ ca hīyate tasmāt kartavyaṃ pāpaśodhanam 
vidyālakṣmīviśuddhyarthaṃ māṃ dhyātvāñjalinā śubhe ।। 

śivenaikādaśenādbhir abhiṣiñcetsamantataḥ 
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva snāyātpāpaviśuddhaye ।। 

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ tacca sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham 
saṃdhyopāsanavicchede japedaṣṭaśataṃ naraḥ ।। 

viḍvarāhaiś ca cāṇḍālair durjanaiḥ kukkuṭairapi 
spṛṣṭamannaṃ na bhuñjīta bhuktvā cāṣṭaśataṃ japet ।। 

brahmahatyāviśuddhyarthaṃ japellakṣāyutaṃ naraḥ 
pātakānāṃ tadardhaṃ syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

upapātakaduṣṭānāṃ tadardhaṃ parikīrtitam 
śeṣāṇāmapi pāpānāṃ japetpañcasahasrakam ।। 

ātmabodhaparaṃ guhyaṃ śivabodhaprakāśakam 
śivaḥ syātsa japenmantraṃ pañcalakṣam anākulaḥ ।। 

pañcavāyujayaṃ bhadre prāpnoti manujaḥ sukham 
japecca pañcalakṣaṃ tu vigṛhītendriyaḥ śuciḥ ।। 

pañcendriyāṇāṃ vijayo bhaviṣyati varānane 
dhyānayukto japedyastu pañcalakṣamanākulaḥ ।। 

viṣayāṇāṃ ca pañcānāṃ jayaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ 
caturthaṃ pañcalakṣaṃ tu yo japedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।। 

bhūtānāmiha pañcānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet 
caturlakṣaṃ japedyastu manaḥ saṃyamya yatnataḥ ।। 

samyagvijayamāpnoti karaṇānāṃ varānane 
pañcaviṃśatilakṣāṇāṃ japena kamalānane ।। 

pañcaviṃśatitattvānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet 
madhyarātre atinirvāte japedayutamādarāt ।। 

brahmasiddhimavāpnoti vratenānena suṃdari 
japellakṣamanālasyo nirvāte dhvanivarjite ।। 

madhyarātre ca śivayoḥ paśyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ 
andhakāravināśaś ca dīpasyeva prakāśanam ।। 

hṛdayāntarbahirvāpi bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhyarthaṃ japedayutamātmavān ।। 

sabījasaṃpuṭaṃ mantraṃ śatalakṣaṃ japecchuciḥ 
matsāyujyamavāpnoti bhaktimān kimataḥ param ।। 

iti te sarvamākhyātaṃ pañcākṣaravidhikramam 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

śrāvayecca dvijāñchuddhān pañcākṣaravidhikramam 
daive karmaṇi pitrye vā śivaloke mahīyate ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pañcākṣaramāhātmyaṃ nāma pañcāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

japācchreṣṭhatamaṃ prāhur brāhmaṇā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ 
viraktānāṃ prabuddhānāṃ dhyānayajñaṃ suśobhanam ।। 

tasmādvadasva sūtādya dhyānayajñamaśeṣataḥ 
vistārātsarvayatnena viraktānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 

teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām 
rudreṇa kathitaṃ prāha guhāṃ prāpya mahātmanām ।। 

saṃhṛtya kālakūṭākhyaṃ viṣaṃ vai viśvakarmaṇā 
guhāṃ prāpya sukhāsīnaṃ bhavānyā saha śaṅkaram ।। 

munayaḥ saṃśitātmānaḥ praṇemustaṃ guhāśrayam 
astuvaṃś ca tataḥ sarve nīlakaṇṭhamumāpatim ।। 

atyugraṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhagavaṃstvayā 
ataḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā deva vṛṣadhvaja ।। 

teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ 
prahasanprāha viśvātmā sanandanapurogamān ।। 

kimanena dvijaśreṣṭhā viṣaṃ vakṣye sudāruṇam 
saṃharettadviṣaṃ yastu sa samartho hyanena kim ।। 

na viṣaṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃsāro viṣamucyate 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena saṃhareta sudāruṇam ।। 

saṃsāro dvividhaḥ proktaḥ svādhikārānurūpataḥ 
puṃsāṃ saṃmūḍhacittānām asaṃkṣīṇaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।। 

īṣaṇārāgadoṣeṇa sargo jñānena suvratāḥ 
tadvaśādeva sarveṣāṃ dharmādharmau na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

asannikṛṣṭe tvarthe api śāstraṃ tacchravaṇātsatām 
buddhimutpādayatyeva saṃsāre viduṣāṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

tasmāddṛṣṭānuśravikaṃ duṣṭamityubhayātmakam 
saṃtyajetsarvayatnena viraktaḥ so abhidhīyate ।। 

śāstramityucyate bhāgaṃ śruteḥ karmasu taddvijāḥ 
mūrdhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sāram ṛṣīṇāṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam ।। 

nanu svabhāvaḥ sarveṣāṃ kāmo dṛṣṭo na cānyathā 
śrutiḥ pravartikā teṣām iti karmaṇyatadvidaḥ ।। 

nivṛttilakṣaṇo dharmaḥ samarthānām ihocyate 
tasmādajñānamūlo hi saṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām ।। 

kalā saṃśoṣamāyāti karmaṇānyasvabhāvataḥ 
sakalastrividho jīvo jñānahīnastvavidyayā ।। 

nārakī pāpakṛtsvargī puṇyakṛt puṇyagauravāt 
vyatimiśreṇa vai jīvaś caturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। 

udbhijjaḥ svedajaścaiva aṇḍajo vai jarāyujaḥ 
evaṃ vyavasthito dehī karmaṇājño hyanirvṛtaḥ ।। 

prajayā karmaṇā muktir dhanena ca satāṃ na hi 
tyāgenaikena muktiḥ syāt tadabhāvādbhramatyasau ।। 

evamajñānadoṣeṇa nānākarmavaśena ca 
ṣaṭkauśikaṃ samudbhūtaṃ bhajatyeṣa kalevaram ।। 

garbhe duḥkhānyanekāni yonimārge ca bhūtale 
kaumāre yauvane caiva vārddhake maraṇe api vā ।। 

vicārataḥ satāṃ duḥkhaṃ strīsaṃsargādibhir dvijāḥ 
duḥkhenaikena vai duḥkhaṃ praśāmyatīha duḥkhinaḥ ।। 

na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati 
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।। 

tasmādvicārato nāsti saṃyogādapi vai nṛṇām 
arthānām arjane apyevaṃ pālane ca vyaye tathā ।। 

paiśāce rākṣase duḥkhaṃ yākṣe caiva vicārataḥ 
gāndharve ca tathā cāndre saumyaloke dvijottamāḥ ।। 

prājāpatye tathā brāhme prākṛte pauruṣe tathā 
kṣayasātiśayādyaistu duḥkhairduḥkhāni suvratāḥ ।। 

tāni bhāgyānyaśuddhāni saṃtyajecca dhanāni ca 
tasmādaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhogaṃ tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitam ।। 

caturviṃśatprakāreṇa saṃsthitaṃ cāpi suvratāḥ 
dvātriṃśadbhedamanaghāś catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ punaḥ ।। 

tathāṣṭacatvāriṃśacca ṣaṭpañcāśatprakārataḥ 
catuḥṣaṣṭividhaṃ caiva duḥkhameva vivekinaḥ ।। 

pārthivaṃ ca tathāpyaṃ ca taijasaṃ ca vicārataḥ 
vāyavyaṃ ca tathā vyauma[ṃ] mānasaṃ ca yathākramam ।। 

ābhimānikamapyevaṃ bauddhaṃ prākṛtameva ca 
duḥkhameva na saṃdeho yogināṃ brahmavādinām ।। 

gauṇaṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ ca duḥkhameva vicārataḥ 
ādau madhye tathā cānte sarvalokeṣu sarvadā ।। 

vartamānāni duḥkhāni bhaviṣyāṇi yathātatham 
doṣaduṣṭeṣu deśeṣu duḥkhāni vividhāni ca ।। 

na bhāvayantyatītāni hy ajñāne jñānamāninaḥ 
kṣudvyādheḥ parihārārthaṃ na sukhāyānnamucyate ।। 

yathetareṣāṃ rogāṇām auṣadhaṃ na sukhāya tat 
śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyais tattatkāleṣu dehinām ।। 

duḥkhameva na saṃdeho na jānanti hyapaṇḍitāḥ 
svarge apyevaṃ muniśreṣṭhā hy aviśuddhakṣayādibhiḥ ।। 

rogair nānāvidhair grastā rāgadveṣabhayādibhiḥ 
chinnamūlataruryadvad avaśaḥ patati kṣitau ।। 

puṇyavṛkṣakṣayāttadvad gāṃ patanti divaukasaḥ 
duḥkhābhilāṣaniṣṭhānāṃ duḥkhabhogādisaṃpadām ।। 

asmāttu patatāṃ duḥkhaṃ kaṣṭaṃ svargāddivaukasām 
narake duḥkhamevātra narakāṇāṃ niṣevaṇāt ।। 

vihitākaraṇāccaiva varṇināṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। 

yathā mṛgo mṛtyubhayasya bhīta ucchinnavāso na labheta nidrām 
evaṃ yatirdhyānaparo mahātmā saṃsārabhīto na labheta nidrām ।। 

kīṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca paśūnāṃ gajavājinām 
dṛṣṭam evāsukhaṃ tasmāt tyajataḥ sukhamuttamam ।। 

vaimānikānāmapyevaṃ duḥkhaṃ kalpādhikāriṇām 
sthānābhimānināṃ caiva manvādīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ ।। 

devānāṃ caiva daityānām anyonyavijigīṣayā 
duḥkhameva nṛpāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ jagattraye ।। 

śramārthamāśramaścāpi varṇānāṃ paramārthataḥ 
āśramairna ca devaiś ca yajñaiḥ sāṃkhyairvratais tathā ।। 

ugraistapobhir vividhair dānairnānāvidhairapi 
na labhante tathātmānaṃ labhante jñāninaḥ svayam ।। 

tasmātsarvaprayatnena caretpāśupatavratam 
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ vrate pāśupate budhaḥ ।। 

pañcārthajñānasampannaḥ śivatattve samāhitaḥ 
kaivalyakaraṇaṃ yogavidhikarmacchidaṃ budhaḥ ।। 

pañcārthayogasampanno duḥkhāntaṃ vrajate sudhīḥ 
parayā vidyayā vedyaṃ vidantyaparayā na hi ।। 

dve vidye veditavye hi parā caivāparā tathā 
aparā tatra ṛgvedo yajurvedo dvijottamāḥ ।। 

sāmavedastathātharvo vedaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ 
śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chanda eva ca ।। 

jyotiṣaṃ cāparā vidyā parākṣaramiti sthitam 
tadadṛśyaṃ tadagrāhyam agotraṃ tadavarṇakam ।। 

tadacakṣustadaśrotraṃ tadapāṇi apādakam 
tadajātamabhūtaṃ ca tadaśabdaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

asparśaṃ tadarūpaṃ ca rasagandhavivarjitam 
avyayaṃ cāpratiṣṭhaṃ ca tannityaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum ।। 

mahāntaṃ tad bṛhantaṃ ca tadajaṃ cinmayaṃ dvijāḥ 
aprāṇamamanaskaṃ ca tadasnigdhamalohitam ।। 

aprameyaṃ tadasthūlam adīrghaṃ tadanulbaṇam 
ahrasvaṃ tadapāraṃ ca tadānandaṃ tadacyutam ।। 

anapāvṛtamadvaitaṃ tadanantamagocaram 
asaṃvṛtaṃ tadātmaikaṃ parā vidyā na cānyathā ।। 

parāpareti kathite naiveha paramārthataḥ 
ahameva jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ jagat ।। 

matta utpadyate tiṣṭhan mayi mayyeva līyate 
matto nānyaditīkṣeta manovākpāṇibhis tathā ।। 

sarvamātmani saṃpaśyet saccāsacca samāhitaḥ 
sarvaṃ hyātmani saṃpaśyan na bāhye kurute manaḥ ।। 

adhodṛṣṭyā vitastyāṃ tu nābhyāmuparitiṣṭhati 
hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyād viśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat ।। 

hṛdayasyāsya madhye tu puṇḍarīkamavasthitam 
dharmakandasamudbhūtaṃ jñānanālaṃ suśobhanam ।। 

aiśvaryāṣṭadalaṃ śvetaṃ paraṃ vairāgyakarṇikam 
chidrāṇi ca diśo yasya prāṇādyāś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। 

prāṇādyaiścaiva saṃyuktaḥ paśyate bahudhā kramāt 
daśaprāṇavahā nāḍyaḥ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। 

dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍyaḥ samparikīrtitāḥ 
netrasthaṃ jāgrataṃ vidyāt kaṇṭhe svapnaṃ samādiśet ।। 

suṣuptaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ tu turīyaṃ mūrdhani sthitam 
jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca svapne caiva yathākramāt ।। 

īśvarastu suṣupte tu turīye ca maheśvaraḥ 
vadanty evam athānye api samastakaraṇaiḥ pumān ।। 

vartamānastadā tasya jāgradityabhidhīyate 
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraṃ cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam ।। 

yadā vyavasthitastvetaiḥ svapna ityabhidhīyate 
karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā svātmani suvratāḥ ।। 

suṣuptaḥ karaṇairbhinnas turīyaḥ parikīrtyate 
parasturīyātīto asau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

jāgratsvapnasuṣuptiś ca turīyaṃ cādhibhautikam 
ādhyātmikaṃ ca viprendrāś cādhidaivikamucyate ।। 

tatsarvamaham eveti veditavyaṃ vijānatā 
buddhīndriyāṇi viprendrās tathā karmendriyāṇi ca ।। 

manobuddhir ahaṅkāraś cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam 
adhyātmaṃ pṛthagevedaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ smṛtam ।। 

draṣṭavyaṃ caiva śrotavyaṃ ghrātavyaṃ ca yathākramam 
rasitavyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

mantavyaṃ caiva boddhavyam ahaṃkartavyameva ca 
tathā cetayitavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। 

ādātavyaṃ ca gantavyaṃ visargāyitameva ca 
ānanditavyamityete hy adhibhūtamanukramāt ।। 

ādityo api diśaścaiva pṛthivī varuṇas tathā 
vāyuścandras tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajña eva ca ।। 

agnirindras tathā viṣṇur mitro devaḥ prajāpatiḥ 
ādhidaivikamevaṃ hi caturdaśavidhaṃ kramāt ।। 

rājñī sudarśanā caiva jitā saumyā yathākramam 
moghā rudrāmṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ ।। 

nāḍī rāśiśukā caiva asurā caiva kṛttikā 
bhāsvatī nāḍayaścaitāś caturdaśanibandhanāḥ ।। 

vāyavo nāḍimadhyasthā vāhakāś ca caturdaśa 
prāṇo vyānastvapānaś ca udānaś ca samānakaḥ ।। 

vairambhaś ca tathā mukhyo hy antaryāmaḥ prabhañjanaḥ 
kūrmakaś ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānilaḥ ।। 

nāga ityeva kathitā vāyavaś ca caturdaśa 
yaścakṣuḥṣvatha draṣṭavye tathāditye ca suvratāḥ ।। 

nāḍyāṃ prāṇe ca vijñāne tv ānande ca yathākramam 
hṛdyākāśe ya etasmin sarvasminnantare paraḥ ।। 

ātmā ekaś ca carati tamupāsīta māṃ prabhum 
ajaraṃ tamanantaṃ ca aśokamamṛtaṃ dhruvam ।। 

caturdaśavidheṣveva saṃcaratyeka eva saḥ 
līyante tāni tatraiva yadanyaṃ nāsti vai dvijāḥ ।। 

eka eva hi sarvajñaḥ sarveśastveka eva saḥ 
eṣa sarvādhipo devas tv antaryāmī mahādyutiḥ ।। 

upāsyamānaḥ sarvasya sarvasaukhyaḥ sanātanaḥ 
upāsyati na caiveha sarvasaukhyaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

upāsyamāno vedaiś ca śāstrairnānāvidhairapi 
na vaiṣa vedaśāstrāṇi sarvajño yāsyati prabhuḥ ।। 

asyaivānnamidaṃ sarvaṃ na so annaṃ bhavati svayam 
svātmanā rakṣitaṃ cādyād annabhūtaṃ na kutracit ।। 

sarvatra prāṇināmannaṃ prāṇināṃ granthirasmyaham 
praśāstā nayanaścaiva pañcātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ ।। 

annamayo asau bhūtātmā cādyate hyannamucyate 
prāṇamayaścendriyātmā saṃkalpātmā manomayaḥ ।। 

kālātmā soma eveha vijñānamaya ucyate 
sadānandamayo bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

so aham evaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ sthitam 
paratantraṃ svatantre api tadabhāvādvicārataḥ ।। 

ekatvamapi nāstyeva dvaitaṃ tatra kutastvaho 
evaṃ nāstyatha martyaṃ ca kuto amṛtamajodbhavaḥ ।। 

nāntaḥprajño bahiḥprajño na cobhayagatas tathā 
na prajñānaghanastvevaṃ na prājño jñānapūrvakaḥ ।। 

viditaṃ nāsti vedyaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ paramārthataḥ 
nirvāṇaṃ caiva kaivalyaṃ niḥśreyasamanāmayam ।। 

amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma paramātmā parāparam 
nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ paryāyavācakam ।। 

prasannaṃ ca yadekāgraṃ tadā jñānamiti smṛtam 
ajñānamitaratsarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

itthaṃ prasannaṃ vijñānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam 
rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhaṃ kāmatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā ।। 

aparāmṛṣṭamadyaiva vijñeyaṃ muktidaṃ tvidam 
ajñānamalapūrvatvāt puruṣo malinaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

tatkṣayāddhi bhavenmuktir nānyathā janmakoṭibhiḥ 
jñānamekaṃ vinā nāsti puṇyapāpaparikṣayaḥ ।। 

jñānam evābhyaset tasmān muktyarthaṃ brahmavittamāḥ 
jñānābhyāsāddhi vai puṃsāṃ buddhirbhavati nirmalā ।। 

tasmātsadābhyasejjñānaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ 
jñānenaikena tṛptasya tyaktasaṃgasya yoginaḥ ।। 

kartavyaṃ nāsti viprendrā asti cettattvavinna ca 
iha loke pare cāpi kartavyaṃ nāsti tasya vai ।। 

jīvanmukto yatas tasmād brahmavit paramārthataḥ 
jñānābhyāsarato nityaṃ jñānatattvārthavit svayam ।। 

kartavyābhyāsamutsṛjya jñānamevādhigacchati 
varṇāśramābhimānī yas tyaktakrodho dvijottamāḥ ।। 

anyatra ramate mūḍhaḥ so ajñānī nātra saṃśayaḥ 
saṃsāraheturajñānaṃ saṃsārastanusaṃgrahaḥ ।। 

mokṣahetus tathā jñānaṃ muktaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ 
ajñāne sati viprendrāḥ krodhādyā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

krodho harṣas tathā lobho moho dambho dvijottamāḥ 
dharmādharmau hi teṣāṃ ca tadvaśāttanusaṃgrahaḥ ।। 

śarīre sati vai kleśaḥ so avidyāṃ saṃtyajedbudhaḥ 
avidyāṃ vidyayā hitvā sthitasyaiva ca yoginaḥ ।। 

krodhādyā nāśamāyānti dharmādharmau ca vai dvijāḥ 
tatkṣayācca śarīreṇa na punaḥ samprayujyate ।। 

sa eva muktaḥ saṃsārād duḥkhatrayavivarjitaḥ 
evaṃ jñānaṃ vinā nāsti dhyānaṃ dhyātur dvijarṣabhāḥ ।। 

jñānaṃ gurorhi saṃparkān na vācā paramārthataḥ 
caturvyūhamiti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samabhyaset ।। 

sahajāgantukaṃ pāpam asthivāgudbhavaṃ tathā 
jñānāgnirdahate kṣipraṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥ ।। 

jñānātparataraṃ nāsti sarvapāpavināśanam 
abhyasecca sadā jñānaṃ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ ।। 

jñāninaḥ sarvapāpāni jīryante nātra saṃśayaḥ 
krīḍannapi na lipyeta pāpairnānāvidhairapi ।। 

jñānaṃ yathā tathā dhyānaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samabhyaset 
dhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ proktam ādau saviṣayaṃ tathā ।। 

ṣaṭprakāraṃ samabhyasya catuḥṣaḍdaśabhis tathā 
tathā dvādaśadhā caiva punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt ।। 

dvidhābhyasya ca yogīndro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śuddhajāṃbūnadākāraṃ vidhūmāṅgārasannibham ।। 

pītaṃ raktaṃ sitaṃ vidyut koṭikoṭisamaprabham 
athavā brahmarandhrasthaṃ cittaṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ ।। 

na sitaṃ vāsitaṃ pītaṃ na smared brahmavid bhavet 
ahiṃsakaḥ satyavādī asteyī sarvayatnataḥ ।। 

parigrahavinirmukto brahmacārī dṛḍhavrataḥ 
saṃtuṣṭaḥ śaucasampannaḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ sadā ।। 

madraktaścābhyaseddhyānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam 
na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

na cābhimanyate yogī na paśyati samantataḥ 
na ghrāti na śṛṇotyeva līnaḥ svātmani yaḥ svayam ।। 

na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti sa vai samarasaḥ smṛtaḥ 
pārthive paṭale brahmā vāritattve hariḥ svayam ।। 

vāhneye kālarudrākhyo vāyutattve maheśvaraḥ 
suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣāt kramādevaṃ vicintayet ।। 

kṣitau śarvaḥ smṛto devo hy apāṃ bhava iti smṛtaḥ 
rudra eva tathā vahnau ugro vāyau vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

bhīmaḥ suṣiranāke asau bhāskare maṇḍale sthitaḥ 
īśānaḥ somabimbe ca mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ ।। 

puṃsāṃ paśupatirdevaś cāṣṭadhāhaṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
kāṭhinyaṃ yattanau sarvaṃ pārthivaṃ parigīyate ।। 

āpyaṃ dravamiti proktaṃ varṇākhyo vahnirucyate 
yatsaṃcarati tadvāyuḥ suṣiraṃ yaddvijottamāḥ ।। 

tadākāśaṃ ca vijñānaṃ śabdajaṃ vyomasaṃbhavam 
tathaiva viprā vijñānaṃ sparśākhyaṃ vāyusaṃbhavam ।। 

rūpaṃ vāhneyamityuktam āpyaṃ rasamayaṃ dvijāḥ 
gandhākhyaṃ pārthivaṃ bhūyaś cintayedbhāskaraṃ kramāt ।। 

netre ca dakṣiṇe vāme somaṃ hṛdi vibhuṃ dvijāḥ 
ājānu pṛthivītattvam ānābher vārimaṇḍalam ।। 

ākaṇṭhaṃ vahnitattvaṃ syāl lalāṭāntaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vāyavyaṃ vai lalāṭādyaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vā śikhāgrakam ।। 

haṃsākhyaṃ ca tato brahma vyomnaścordhvaṃ tataḥ param 
vyomākhyo vyomamadhyastho hy ayaṃ prāthamikaḥ smaret ।। 

na jīvaḥ prakṛtiḥ sattvaṃ rajaścātha tamaḥ punaḥ 
mahāṃstathābhimānaś ca tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca ।। 

vyomādīni ca bhūtāni naiveha paramārthataḥ 
vyāpya tiṣṭhadyato viśvaṃ sthāṇurityabhidhīyate ।। 

udeti sūryo bhītaś ca pavate vāta eva ca 
dyotate candramā vahnir jvalatyāpo vahanti ca ।। 

dadhāti bhūmirākāśam avakāśaṃ dadāti ca 
tadājñayā tataṃ sarvaṃ tasmādvai cintayeddvijāḥ ।। 

tenaivādhiṣṭhitaṃ tasmād etatsarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
sarvarūpamayaḥ śarva iti matvā smaredbhavam ।। 

saṃsāraviṣataptānāṃ jñānadhyānāmṛtena vai 
pratīkāraḥ samākhyāto nānyathā dvijasattamāḥ ।। 

jñānaṃ dharmodbhavaṃ sākṣāj jñānād vairāgyasaṃbhavaḥ 
vairāgyātparamaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthaprakāśakam ।। 

jñānavairāgyayuktasya yogasiddhirdvijottamāḥ 
yogasiddhyā vimuktiḥ syāt sattvaniṣṭhasya nānyathā ।। 

tamovidyāpadacchannaṃ citraṃ yatpadamavyayam 
sattvaśaktiṃ samāsthāya śivamabhyarcayeddvijāḥ ।। 

yaḥ sattvaniṣṭho madbhakto madarcanaparāyaṇaḥ 
sarvato dharmaniṣṭhaś ca sadotsāhī samāhitaḥ ।। 

sarvadvandvasaho dhīraḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ 
ṛjusvabhāvaḥ satataṃ svasthacitto mṛduḥ sadā ।। 

amānī buddhimāñchāntas tyaktaspardho dvijottamāḥ 
sadā mumukṣurdharmajñaḥ svātmalakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

ṛṇatrayavinirmuktaḥ pūrvajanmani puṇyabhāk 
jarāyukto dvijo bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt ।। 

anyathā vāpi śuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā kṛtrimavarjitaḥ 
svargalokamanuprāpya bhuktvā bhogānanukramāt ।। 

āsādya bhārataṃ varṣaṃ brahmavijjāyate dvijāḥ 
saṃparkājjñānamāsādya jñānino yogavidbhavet ।। 

kramo ayaṃ malapūrṇasya jñānaprāpterdvijottamāḥ 
tasmādanena mārgeṇa tyaktasaṃgo dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। 

saṃsārakālakūṭākhyān mucyate munipuṅgavāḥ 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mayā yuṣmākamacyutam ।। 

jñānasyaiveha māhātmyaṃ prasaṃgādiha śobhanam 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kathitaṃ tvīśvareṇa tu ।। 

na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi śivoktaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
dātavyaṃ yogine nityaṃ bhasmaniṣṭhāya supriyam ।। 

yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃsāraśamanaṃ naraḥ 
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge saṃsāraviṣakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍaśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

niśamya te mahāprājñāḥ kumārādyāḥ pinākinam 
procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannaṃ parameśvaram ।। 

evaṃ cedanayā devyā haimavatyā maheśvara 
krīḍase vividhairbhogaiḥ kathaṃ vaktumihārhasi ।। 

evamuktaḥ prahasyeśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ 
prāha tām aṃbikāṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān ।। 

bandhamokṣau na caiveha mama svecchā śarīriṇaḥ 
akartajñaḥ paśurjīvo vibhurbhoktā hyaṇuḥ pumān ।। 

māyī ca māyayā baddhaḥ karmabhir yujyate tu saḥ 
jñānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca bandhaś ca mokṣo nāstyātmano dvijāḥ ।। 

yadaivaṃ mayi vidvān yas tasyāpi na ca sarvataḥ 
eṣā vidyā hyahaṃ vedyaḥ prajñaiṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ ।। 

dhṛtireṣā mayā niṣṭhā jñānaśaktiḥ kriyā tathā 
icchākhyā ca tathā hyājñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ ।। 

na hyeṣā prakṛtirjaivī vikṛtiś ca vicārataḥ 
vikāro naiva māyaiṣā sadasadvyaktivarjitā ।। 

purā mamājñā madvaktrāt samutpannā sanātanī 
pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagatāmabhayapradā ।। 

tāmājñāṃ sampraviśyāhaṃ cintayan jagatāṃ hitam 
saptaviṃśatprakāreṇa sarvaṃ vyāpyānayā śivaḥ ।। 

tadāprabhṛti vai mokṣapravṛttirdvijasattamāḥ 
evamuktvā tadāpaśyad bhavānīṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

bhavānī ca tamālokya māyāmaharadavyayā 
te māyāmalanirmuktā munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm ।। 

prītā babhūvurmuktāś ca tasmādeṣā parā gatiḥ 
umāśaṅkarayorbhedo nāstyeva paramārthataḥ ।। 

dvidhāsau rūpamāsthāya sthita eva na saṃśayaḥ 
yadā vidvānasaṃgaḥ syād ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

tadā muktiḥ kṣaṇādeva nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ 
kramo avivakṣito bhūtavivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

prasādena kṣaṇānmuktiḥ pratijñaiṣā na saṃśayaḥ 
garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇo api vā ।। 

vṛddho vā mucyate jantuḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ 
aṇḍajaś codbhijjo vāpi svedajo vāpi mucyate ।। 

prasādāddevadevasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
eṣa eva jagannātho bandhamokṣakaraḥ śivaḥ ।। 

bhūrbhūvaḥsvarmahaś caiva janaḥ sākṣāttapaḥ svayam 
satyalokas tathāṇḍānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ca ।। 

vigrahaṃ devadevasya tathāṇḍāvaraṇāṣṭakam 
saptadvīpeṣu sarveṣu parvateṣu vaneṣu ca ।। 

samudreṣu ca sarveṣu vāyuskandheṣu sarvataḥ 
tathānyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasanti ca carācarāḥ ।। 

sarve bhavāṃśajā nūnaṃ gatistveṣāṃ sa eva vai 
sarvo rudro namastasmai puruṣāya mahātmane ।। 

viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ tathā jātaṃ bahudhā rudra eva saḥ 
rudrājñaiṣā sthitā devī hy anayā muktiraṃbikā ।। 

ityevaṃ khecarāḥ siddhā jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ 
yadāvalokya tān sarvān prasādādanayāṃbikā ।। 

tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyaṃ prāptāste khecarāḥ prabhoḥ ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge munimohaśamanaṃ nāma saptāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

kena yogena vai sūta guṇaprāptiḥ satāmiha 
aṇimādiguṇopetā bhavantyeveha yoginaḥ 
tatsarvaṃ vistarātsūta vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham 
pañcadhā saṃsmaredādau sthāpya citte sanātanam ।। 

kalpayeccāsanaṃ padmaṃ somasūryāgnisaṃyutam 
ṣaḍviṃśacchaktisaṃyuktam aṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ ।। 

tataḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva punardvādaśadhā dvijāḥ 
smarec ca tat tathā madhye devyā devam umāpatim ।। 

aṣṭaśaktisamāyuktam aṣṭamūrtimajaṃ prabhum 
tābhiścāṣṭavidhā rudrāś catuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punaḥ ।। 

śaktayaś ca tathā sarvā guṇāṣṭakasamanvitāḥ 
evaṃ smaretkrameṇaiva labdhvā jñānamanuttamam ।। 

evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ mokṣasiddhipradāyakam 
tasyāṇimādayo viprā nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ ।। 

tatrāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ yogināṃ samudāhṛtam 
tatsarvaṃ kramayogena hy ucyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। 

aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca 
prākāmyaṃ caiva sarvatra īśitvaṃ caiva sarvataḥ ।। 

vaśitvamatha sarvatra yatra kāmāvasāyitā 
taccāpi trividhaṃ jñeyam aiśvaryaṃ sārvakāmikam ।। 

sāvadyaṃ niravadyaṃ ca sūkṣmaṃ caiva pravartate 
sāvadyaṃ nāma yattatra pañcabhūtātmakaṃ smṛtam ।। 

indriyāṇi manaścaiva ahaṅkāraś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ 
tatra sūkṣmapravṛttistu pañcabhūtātmikā punaḥ ।। 

indriyāṇi manaścittabuddhyahaṅkārasaṃjñitam 
tathā sarvamayaṃ caiva ātmasthā khyātireva ca ।। 

saṃyoga eva trividhaḥ sūkṣmeṣveva pravartate 
punaraṣṭaguṇaścāpi sūkṣmeṣveva vidhīyate ।। 

tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāha bhagavānprabhuḥ 
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yathāsya niyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 

aṇimādyaṃ tathāvyaktaṃ sarvatraiva pratiṣṭhitam 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ duṣprāpyaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। 

tat tasya bhavati prāpyaṃ prathamaṃ yogināṃ balam 
laṅghanaṃ plavanaṃ loke rūpamasya sadā bhavet ।। 

śīghratvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dvitīyaṃ tu padaṃ smṛtam 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ mahimnā caiva vanditam ।। 

mahitvaṃ cāpi loke asmiṃs tṛtīyo yoga ucyate 
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yatheṣṭagamanaṃ smṛtam ।। 

prākāmān viṣayān bhuṅkte tathāpratihataḥ kvacit 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ sukhaduḥkhaṃ pravartate ।। 

īśo bhavati sarvatra pravibhāgena yogavit 
vaśyāni cāsya bhūtāni trailokye sacarācare ।। 

icchayā tasya rūpāṇi bhavanti na bhavanti ca 
yatra kāmāvasāyitvaṃ trailokye sacarācare ।। 

śabdaḥ sparśo raso gandho rūpaṃ caiva manas tathā 
pravartante asya cecchāto na bhavanti yathecchayā ।। 

na jāyate na mriyate chidyate na ca bhidyate 
na dahyate na muhyeta līyate na ca lipyate ।। 

na kṣīyate na kṣarati khidyate na kadācana 
kriyate vā na sarvatra tathā vikriyate na ca ।। 

agandharasarūpastu asparśaḥ śabdavarjitaḥ 
avarṇo hyasvaraś caiva asavarṇastu karhicit ।। 

sa bhuṅkte viṣayāṃścaiva viṣayairna ca yujyate 
aṇutvāttu paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmatvād apavargikaḥ ।। 

vyāpakastvapavargācca vyāpakātpuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ 
puruṣaḥ sūkṣmabhāvāttu aiśvarye parame sthitaḥ ।। 

guṇottaramathaiśvarye sarvataḥ sūkṣmamucyate 
aiśvaryaṃ cāpratīghātaṃ prāpya yogamanuttamam ।। 

apavargaṃ tato gacchet sūkṣmaṃ tatparamaṃ padam 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ jñātavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। 

svargāpavargaphaladaṃ śivasāyujyakāraṇam 
athavā gatavijñāno rāgātkarma samācaret ।। 

rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ vāpi bhuktvā tatraiva mucyate 
tathā sukṛtakarmā tu phalaṃ svarge samaśnute ।। 

tasmātsthānātpunaḥ śreṣṭho mānuṣyamupapadyate 
tasmādbrahma paraṃ saukhyaṃ brahma śāśvatam uttamam ।। 

brahma eva hi seveta brahmaiva hi paraṃ sukham 
pariśramo hi yajñānāṃ mahatārthena vartate ।। 

bhūyo mṛtyuvaśaṃ yāti tasmānmokṣaḥ paraṃ sukham 
athavā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmatattvaparāyaṇaḥ ।। 

na tu cyāvayituṃ śakyo manvantaraśatairapi 
dṛṣṭvā tu puruṣaṃ divyaṃ viśvākhyaṃ viśvatomukham ।। 

viśvapādaśirogrīvaṃ viśveśaṃ viśvarūpiṇam 
viśvagandhaṃ viśvamālyaṃ viśvāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum ।। 

gobhir mahīṃ saṃpatate patatriṇo naivaṃ bhūyo janayatyevameva 
kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāraṃ sūkṣmācca sūkṣmaṃ mahato mahāntam ।। 

yogena paśyenna ca cakṣuṣā punar nirindriyaṃ puruṣaṃ rukmavarṇam 
aliṅginaṃ nirguṇaṃ cetanaṃ ca nityaṃ sadā sarvagaṃ sarvasāram ।। 
paśyanti yuktyā hyacalaprakāśaṃ tadbhāvitāstejasā dīpyamānam । 
apāṇipādodarapārśvajihvo hyatīndriyo vāpi susūkṣma ekaḥ ।। 
paśyatyacakṣuḥ sa śṛṇotyakarṇo na cāstyabuddhaṃ na ca buddhir asti । 
sa veda sarvaṃ na ca sarvavedyaṃ tamāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntam ।। 

acetanāṃ sarvagatāṃ sūkṣmāṃ prasavadharmiṇīm 
prakṛtiṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yuktāḥ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।। 

sarvataḥ pāṇipādaṃ tat sarvato akṣiśiromukham 
sarvataḥ śrutimal loke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। 

yukto yogena ceśānaṃ sarvataś ca sanātanam 
puruṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ taṃ vidvānna vimuhyati ।। 

bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ paramātmānamavyayam 
sarvātmānaṃ paraṃ brahma tadvai dhyātā na muhyati ।। 

pavano hi yathā grāhyo vicaransarvamūrtiṣu 
puri śete sudurgrāhyas tasmātpuruṣa ucyate ।। 

atha celluptadharmā tu sāvaśeṣaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ 
tatastu brahmagarbhe vai śukraśoṇitasaṃyute ।। 

strīpuṃsoḥ saṃprayoge hi jāyate hi tataḥ prabhuḥ 
tatastu garbhakālena kalalaṃ nāma jāyate ।। 

kālena kalalaṃ cāpi budbudaṃ samprajāyate 
mṛtpiṇḍastu yathā cakre cakrāvartena pīḍitaḥ ।। 

hastābhyāṃ kriyamāṇastu biṃbatvamanugacchati 
evamādhyātmikairyuktā vāyunā saṃprapūritaḥ ।। 

yadi yoniṃ vimuñcāmi tatprapadye maheśvaram 
yāvaddhi vaiṣṇavo vāyur jātamātraṃ na saṃspṛśet ।। 

tāvatkālaṃ mahādevam arcayāmīti cintayet 
jāyate mānuṣastatra yathārūpaṃ yathāvayaḥ ।। 

vāyuḥ saṃbhavate khāttu vātādbhavati vai jalam 
jalāt sambhavati prāṇaḥ prāṇācchukraṃ vivardhate ।। 

raktabhāgās trayastriṃśad retobhāgāś caturdaśa 
bhāgato ardhaphalaṃ kṛtvā tato garbho niṣicyate ।। 

tatastu garbhasaṃyuktaḥ pañcabhir vāyubhir vṛtaḥ 
pituḥ śarīrātpratyaṅgaṃ rūpamasyopajāyate ।। 

tato asya māturāhārāt pītalīḍhapraveśanāt 
nābhideśena vai prāṇās te hy ādhārā hi dehinām ।। 

navamāsāt parikliṣṭaḥ saṃveṣṭitaśirodharaḥ 
veṣṭitaḥ sarvagātraiś ca aparyāptapraveśanaḥ ।। 

navamāsoṣitaścāpi yonicchidrādavāṅmukhaḥ 
tataḥ svakarmabhiḥ pāpair nirayaṃ samprapadyate ।। 

asipatravanaṃ caiva śālmalicchedanaṃ tathā 
tāḍanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ caiva pūyaśoṇitabhakṣaṇam ।। 

yathā hyāpastu saṃchinnāḥ saṃśleṣmam upayānti vai 
tathā chinnāś ca bhinnāśca yātanāsthānam āgatāḥ ।। 

evaṃ jīvāstu taiḥ pāpais tapyamānāḥ svayaṃkṛtaiḥ 
prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣair duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vetarat ।। 

ekenaiva tu gantavyaṃ sarvamutsṛjya vai janam 
ekenaiva tu bhoktavyaṃ tasmātsukṛtamācaret ।। 

na hyenaṃ prasthitaṃ kaścid gacchantam anugacchati 
yadanena kṛtaṃ karma tadenamanugacchati ।। 

te nityaṃ yamaviṣayeṣu sampravṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatamaniṣṭasaṃprayogaiḥ 
śuṣyante parigatavedanāḥ śarīrā bahvībhiḥ subhṛśamanantayātanābhiḥ ।। 

karmaṇā manasā vācā yadabhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevate 
tadabhyāso haratyenaṃ tasmātkalyāṇamācaret ।। 

anādimānprabandhaḥ syāt pūrvakarmaṇi dehinaḥ 
saṃsāraṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ pratipadyate ।। 

mānuṣyātpaśubhāvaś ca paśubhāvān mṛgo bhavet 
mṛgatvātpakṣibhāvaś ca tasmāccaiva sarīsṛpaḥ ।। 

sarīsṛpatvādgacchedvai sthāvaratvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
sthāvaratve punaḥ prāpte yāvad unmilate janaḥ ।। 

kulālacakravadbhrāntas tatraiva parivartate 
ityevaṃ hi manuṣyādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarāntikaḥ ।। 

vijñeyastāmaso nāma tatraiva parivartate 
sāttvikaścāpi saṃsāro brahmādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 

piśācāntaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svargasthāneṣu dehinām 
brāhme tu kevalaṃ sattvaṃ sthāvare kevalaṃ tamaḥ ।। 

caturdaśānāṃ sthānānāṃ madhye viṣṭambhakaṃ rajaḥ 
marmasu chidyamāneṣu vedanārtasya dehinaḥ ।। 

tatastatparamaṃ brahma kathaṃ vipraḥ smariṣyati 
saṃsāraḥ pūrvadharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ ।। 

mānuṣaṃ bhajate nityaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret 
caturdaśavidhaṃ hyetad buddhvā saṃsāramaṇḍalam ।। 

nityaṃ samārabheddharmaṃ saṃsārabhayapīḍitaḥ 
tatastarati saṃsāraṃ krameṇa parivartitaḥ ।। 

tasmācca satataṃ yukto dhyānatatparayuñjakaḥ 
tathā samārabhedyogaṃ yathātmānaṃ sa paśyati ।। 

eṣa āpaḥ paraṃ jyotir eṣa seturanuttamaḥ 
vivṛtyā hyeṣa saṃbhedād bhūtānāṃ caiva śāśvataḥ ।। 

tadenaṃ setumātmānam agniṃ vai viśvatomukham 
hṛdisthaṃ sarvabhūtānām upāsīta maheśvaram ।। 

tathāntaḥ saṃsthitaṃ devaṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam 
aṣṭadhā cāṣṭadhā caiva tathā cāṣṭavidhena ca ।। 

sṛṣṭyarthaṃ saṃsthitaṃ vahniṃ saṃkṣipya ca hṛdi sthitam 
dhyātvā yathāvaddeveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam ।। 

hutvā pañcāhutīḥ samyak taccintāgatamānasaḥ 
vaiśvānaraṃ hṛdisthaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। 

āpaḥ pūtāḥ sakṛtprāśya tūṣṇīṃ hutvā hyupāviśan 
prāṇāyeti tatastasya prathamā hyāhutiḥ smṛtā ।। 

apānāya dvitīyā ca vyānāyeti tathā parā 
udānāya caturthī syāt samānāyeti pañcamī ।। 

svāhākāraiḥ pṛthagghutvā śeṣaṃ bhuñjīta kāmataḥ 
apaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprāśya ācamya hṛdayaṃ spṛśet ।। 

prāṇānāṃ granthirasyātmā rudro hyātmā viśāntakaḥ 
rudro vai hyātmanaḥ prāṇa evamāpyāyayetsvayam ।। 

prāṇe niviṣṭo vai rudras tasmātprāṇamayaḥ svayam 
prāṇāya caiva rudrāya juhotyamṛtamuttamam ।। 

śivāviśeha māmīśa svāhā brahmātmane svayam 
evaṃ pañcāhutīścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ ।। 

puruṣo asi pure śeṣe tvaṃ aṅguṣṭhapramāṇataḥ 
āśritaścaiva cāṅguṣṭham īśaḥ paramakāraṇam ।। 

sarvasya jagataścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ 
tvaṃ devānāmasi jyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca puro vṛṣā ।। 

mṛdustvamannamasmabhyam etadastu hutaṃ tava 
ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ ।। 

yogācāraḥ svayaṃ tena brahmaṇā kathitaḥ purā 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ ।। 

bhasmasnāyī bhaven nityaṃ bhasmaliptaḥ sadā bhavet 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān ।। 

daive karmaṇi pitrye vā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge aṇimādyaṣṭasiddhitriguṇasaṃsāraprāgnau homādivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śaucācārasya lakṣaṇam 
yadanuṣṭhāya śuddhātmā paretya gatimāpnuyāt ।। 

brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūtahitāya vai 
saṃkṣepātsarvavedārthaṃ saṃcayaṃ brahmavādinām ।। 

udayārthaṃ tu śaucānāṃ munīnāmuttamaṃ padam 
yastatrāthāpramattaḥ syāt sa munirnāvasīdati ।। 

mānāvamānau dvāvetau tāvevāhur viṣāmṛte 
avamāno amṛtaṃ tatra sanmāno viṣamucyate ।। 

gurorapi hite yuktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaraṃ vaset 
niyameṣvapramattastu yameṣu ca sadā bhavet ।। 

prāpyānujñāṃ tataścaiva jñānayogamanuttamam 
avirodhena dharmasya careta pṛthivīmimām ।। 

cakṣuḥpūtaṃ carenmārgaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet 
satyapūtaṃ vadedvākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret ।। 

matsyagṛhyasya yatpāpaṃ ṣaṇmāsābhyantare bhavet 
ekāhaṃ tatsamaṃ jñeyam apūtaṃ yajjalaṃ bhavet ।। 

apūtodakapāne tu japecca śatapañcakam 
aghoralakṣaṇaṃ mantraṃ tataḥ śuddhimavāpnuyāt ।। 

athavā pūjayecchaṃbhuṃ ghṛtasnānādivistaraiḥ 
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ātithyaśrāddhayajñeṣu na gacchedyogavitkvacit 
evaṃ hyahiṃsako yogī bhavediti vicāritam ।। 

vahnau vidhūme atyaṅgāre sarvasminbhuktavajjane 
carettu matimān bhaikṣyaṃ na tu teṣveva nityaśaḥ ।। 

athainam avamanyante pare paribhavanti ca 
tathā yuktaṃ caredbhaikṣyaṃ satāṃ dharmamadūṣayan ।। 

bhaikṣyaṃ caredvanastheṣu yāyāvaragṛheṣu ca 
śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hīyaṃ vṛttirasyopajāyate ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ gṛhastheṣu śīlīneṣu careddvijāḥ 
śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu ।। 

ata ūrdhvaṃ punaścāpi aduṣṭāpatiteṣu ca 
bhaikṣyacaryā hi varṇeṣu jaghanyā vṛttirucyate ।। 

bhaikṣyaṃ yavāgūstakraṃ vā payo yāvakameva ca 
phalamūlādi pakvaṃ vā kaṇapiṇyākasaktavaḥ ।। 

ityeva te mayā proktā yogināṃ siddhivarddhanāḥ 
āhārāsteṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭhaṃ bhaikṣyamiti smṛtam ।। 

abbinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māsi māsi samaśnute 
nyāyato yaścaredbhaikṣyaṃ pūrvoktātsa viśiṣyate ।। 

jarāmaraṇagarbhebhyo bhītasya narakādiṣu 
evaṃ dāyayate tasmāt tadbhaikṣyamiti saṃsmṛtam ।। 

dadhibhakṣāḥ payobhakṣā ye cānye jīvakṣīṇakāḥ 
sarve te bhaikṣyabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। 

bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ bhikṣācārī jitendriyaḥ 
ya icchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret ।। 

yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ bhavet 
ekaṃ dve trīṇi catvāri śaktito vā samācaret ।। 

asteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca alobhastyāga eva ca 
vratāni pañca bhikṣūṇām ahiṃsā paramā tviha ।। 

akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucamāhāralāghavam 
nityaṃ svādhyāya ityete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। 

bījayoniguṇā vastubandhaḥ karmabhir eva ca 
yathā dvipa ivāraṇye manuṣyāṇāṃ vidhīyate ।। 

devaistulyāḥ sarvayajñakriyāstu yajñājjāpyaṃ jñānamāhuś ca jāpyāt 
jñānād dhyānaṃ saṃgarāgādapetaṃ tasminprāpte śāśvatasyopalambhaḥ ।। 

damaḥ śamaḥ satyamakalmaṣatvaṃ maunaṃ ca bhūteṣvakhileṣu cārjavam 
atīndriyaṃ jñānamidaṃ tathā śivaṃ prāhus tathā jñānaviśuddhabuddhayaḥ ।। 
samāhito brahmaparo apramādī śucis tathaikāntaratir jitendriyaḥ । 
samāpnuyādyogamimaṃ mahātmā maharṣayaścaivam aninditāmalāḥ ।। 

prāpyate abhimatān deśān aṅkuśena nivāritaḥ 
etanmārgeṇa śuddhena dagdhabījo hyakalmaṣaḥ ।। 

sadācāraratāḥ śāntāḥ svadharmaparipālakāḥ 
sarvāṃllokān vinirjitya brahmalokaṃ vrajanti te ।। 

pitāmahenopadiṣṭo dharmaḥ sākṣātsanātanaḥ 
sarvalokopakārārthaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ pravadāmi vaḥ ।। 

gurūpadeśayuktānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ kramavarttinām 
abhyutthānādikaṃ sarvaṃ praṇāmaṃ caiva kārayet ।। 

aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātena tridhā nyastena suvratāḥ 
triḥpradakṣiṇayogena vandyo vai brahmaṇo guruḥ ।। 

jyeṣṭhānye api ca te sarve vandanīyā vijānatā 
ājñābhaṅgaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchet siddhim uttamām ।। 

dhātuśūnyabilakṣetrakṣudramantropajīvanam 
viṣagrahaviḍambādīn varjayet sarvayatnataḥ ।। 

kaitavaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ ca paiśunyaṃ varjayetsadā 
atihāsam avaṣṭambhaṃ līlāsvecchāpravartanam ।। 

varjayetsarvayatnena gurūṇāmapi saṃnidhau 
tadvākyapratikūlaṃ ca ayuktaṃ vai gurorvacaḥ ।। 

na vadetsarvayatnena aniṣṭaṃ na smaretsadā 
yatīnāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ daṇḍādyaṃ pāduke tathā ।। 

mālyaṃ ca śayanasthānaṃ pātraṃ chāyāṃ ca yatnataḥ 
yajñopakaraṇāṅgaṃ ca na spṛśed vai padena ca ।। 

devadrohaṃ gurudrohaṃ na kuryātsarvayatnataḥ 
kṛtvā pramādato viprāḥ praṇavasyāyutaṃ japet ।। 

devadrohagurudrohāt koṭimātreṇa śudhyati 
mahāpātakaśuddhyarthaṃ tathaiva ca yathāvidhi ।। 

pātakī ca tadardhena śudhyate vṛttavānyadi 
upapātakinaḥ sarve tadardhenaiva suvratāḥ ।। 

saṃdhyālope kṛte vipraḥ trirāvṛttyaiva śudhyati 
āhnikacchedane jāte śatamekamudāhṛtam ।। 

laṅghane samayānāṃ tu abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe 
avācyavācane caiva sahasrācchuddhirucyate ।। 

kākolūkakapotānāṃ pakṣiṇāmapi ghātane 
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

yaḥ punastattvavettā ca brahmavid brāhmaṇottamaḥ 
smaraṇācchuddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

naivamātmavidāmasti prāyaścittāni codanā 
viśvasyaiva hi te śuddhā brahmavidyāvido janāḥ ।। 

yogadhyānaikaniṣṭhāś ca nirlepāḥ kāñcanaṃ yathā 
śuddhānāṃ śodhanaṃ nāsti viśuddhā brahmavidyayā ।। 

uddhṛtānuṣṇaphenābhiḥ pūtābhir vastracakṣuṣā 
adbhiḥ samācaretsarvaṃ varjayetkaluṣodakam ।। 

gandhavarṇarasairduṣṭam aśucisthānasaṃsthitam 
paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam ।। 

saśaivālaṃ tathānyairvā doṣairduṣṭaṃ vivarjayet 
vastraśaucānvitaḥ kuryāt sarvakāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ ।। 

namaskārādikaṃ sarvaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇādikam 
vastraśaucavihīnātmā hy aśucirnātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

devakāryopayuktānāṃ pratyahaṃ śaucamiṣyate 
itareṣāṃ hi vastrāṇāṃ śaucaṃ kāryaṃ malāgame ।। 

varjayetsarvayatnena vāso anyair vidhṛtaṃ dvijāḥ 
kauśeyāvikayo rūkṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ ।। 

śrīphalairaṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kutapānāmariṣṭakaiḥ 
carmaṇāṃ vidalānāṃ ca vetrāṇāṃ vastravanmatam ।। 

valkalānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ chatracāmarayorapi 
cailavacchaucamākhyātaṃ brahmavidbhir munīśvaraiḥ ।। 

bhasmanā śudhyate kāṃsyaṃ kṣāreṇāyasam ucyate 
tāmramamlena vai viprās trapusīsakayorapi ।। 

haimam adbhiḥ śubhaṃ pātraṃ raupyapātraṃ dvijottamāḥ 
maṇyaśmaśaṅkhamuktānāṃ śaucaṃ taijasavatsmṛtam ।। 

agner apāṃ ca saṃyogād atyantopahatasya ca 
rasānāmiha sarveṣāṃ śuddhirutplavanaṃ smṛtam ।। 

tṛṇakāṣṭhādivastūnāṃ śubhenābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam 
uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhis tathā sruksruvayorapi ।। 

tathaiva yajñapātrāṇāṃ muśalolūkhalasya ca 
śṛṅgāsthidārudantānāṃ takṣaṇenaiva śodhanam ।। 

saṃhatānāṃ mahābhāgā dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ smṛtam 
asaṃhatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ śaucamucyate ।। 

abhuktarāśidhānyānām ekadeśasya dūṣaṇe 
tāvanmātraṃ samuddhṛtya prokṣayedvai kuśāṃbhasā ।। 

śākamūlaphalādīnāṃ dhānyavacchuddhiriṣyate 
mārjanonmārjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam ।। 

ullekhanenāñjanena tathā saṃmārjanena ca 
gonivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā ।। 

bhūmistham udakaṃ śuddhaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yatra gaurvrajet 
avyāptaṃ yadamedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitam ।। 

vatsaḥ śuciḥ prasravaṇe śakuniḥ phalapātane 
svadārāsyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ratau bhāryābhikāṅkṣayā ।। 

hastābhyāṃ kṣālitaṃ vastraṃ kāruṇā ca yathāvidhi 
kuśāṃbunā susaṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāddharmavittamaḥ ।। 

paṇyaṃ prasāritaṃ caiva varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ 
śucirākarajaṃ teṣāṃ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ ।। 

chāyā ca vipluṣo viprā makṣikādyā dvijottamāḥ 
rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā ।। 

suptvā bhuktvā ca vai viprāḥ kṣuttvā pītvā ca vai tathā 
ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanādau ca śucirapyācametpunaḥ ।। 

pādau spṛśanti ye cāpi parācamanabindavaḥ 
te pārthivaiḥ samā jñeyā na tairaprayato bhavet ।। 

kṛtvā ca maithunaṃ spṛṣṭvā patitaṃ kukkuṭādikam 
sūkaraṃ caiva kākādi śvānamuṣṭraṃ kharaṃ tathā ।। 

yūpaṃ cāṇḍālakādyāṃś ca spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati 
rajasvalāṃ sūtikāṃ ca na spṛśedantyajāmapi ।। 

sūtikāśaucasaṃyuktaḥ śāvāśaucasamanvitaḥ 
saṃspṛśenna rajastāsāṃ spṛṣṭvā snātvaiva śudhyati ।। 

naivāśaucaṃ yatīnāṃ ca vanasthabrahmacāriṇām 
naiṣṭhikānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca maṇḍalīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ ।। 

tataḥ kāryavirodhāddhi nṛpāṇāṃ nānyathā bhavet 
vaikhānasānāṃ viprāṇāṃ patitānāmasaṃbhavāt ।। 

asaṃcayād dvijānāṃ ca snānamātreṇa nānyathā 
tathā saṃnihitānāṃ ca yajñārthaṃ dīkṣitasya ca ।। 

ekāhād yajñayājināṃ śuddhiruktā svayaṃbhuvā 
tatastvadhītaśākhānāṃ caturbhiḥ sarvadehinām ।। 

sūtakaṃ pretakaṃ nāsti tryahād ūrdhvam amutra vai 
arvāg ekādaśāhāntaṃ bāndhavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

snānamātreṇa vai śuddhir maraṇe samupasthite 
tata ṛtutrayādarvāg ekāhaḥ parigīyate ।। 

saptavarṣāt tataścārvāk trirātraṃ hi tataḥ param 
daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ vai prathame ahani vā pituḥ ।। 

daśāhaṃ sūtikāśaucaṃ māturapyevamavyayāḥ 
arvāk trivarṣātsnānena bāndhavānāṃ pituḥ sadā ।। 

aṣṭābdād ekarātreṇa śuddhiḥ syād bāndhavasya tu 
dvādaśābdāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ strīṣu suvratāḥ ।। 

sapiṇḍatā ca puruṣe saptame vinivartate 
atikrānte daśāhe tu trirātramaśucirbhavet ।। 

tataḥ saṃnihito vipraś cārvāk pūrvaṃ tadeva vai 
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snānamātreṇa śudhyati ।। 

spṛṣṭvā pretaṃ trirātreṇa dharmārthaṃ snānamucyate 
dāhakānāṃ ca netṝṇāṃ snānamātramabāndhave ।। 

anugamya ca vai snātvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati 
ācāryamaraṇe caiva trirātraṃ śrotriye mṛte ।। 

pakṣiṇī mātulānāṃ ca sodarāṇāṃ ca vā dvijāḥ 
bhūpānāṃ maṇḍalīnāṃ ca sadyo nīrāṣṭravāsinām ।। 

kevalaṃ dvādaśāhena kṣattriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ 
nābhiṣiktasya cāśaucaṃ saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe ।। 

vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktā dravyaśuddhiranuttamā ।। 

aśaucaṃ cānupūrvyeṇa yatīnāṃ naiva vidyate 
tretāprabhṛti nārīṇāṃ māsi māsyārtavaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

kṛte sakṛd yugavaśāj jāyante vai sahaiva tu 
prayānti ca mahābhāgā bhāryābhiḥ kuravo yathā ।। 

varṇāśramavyavasthā ca tretāprabhṛti suvratāḥ 
bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā netareṣvatha ।। 

mahāvīte suvīte ca jaṃbūdvīpe tathāṣṭasu 
śākadvīpādiṣu prokto dharmo vai bhārate yathā ।। 

rasollāsā kṛte vṛttis tretāyāṃ gṛhavṛkṣajā 
saivārtavakṛtād doṣād rāgadveṣādibhir nṛṇām ।। 

maithunātkāmato viprās tathaiva paruṣādibhiḥ 
yavādyāḥ samprajāyante grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa ।। 

oṣadhyaś ca rajodoṣāḥ strīṇāṃ rāgādibhir nṛṇām 
akālakṛṣṭā vidhvastāḥ punarutpāditās tathā ।। 

tasmātsarvaprayatnena na saṃbhāṣyā rajasvalā 
prathame ahani cāṇḍālī yathā varjyā tathāṅganā ।। 

dvitīye ahani viprā hi yathā vai brahmaghātinī 
tṛtīye ahni tadardhena caturthe ahani suvratāḥ ।। 

snātvārdhamāsāt saṃśuddhā tataḥ śuddhirbhaviṣyati 
ā ṣoḍaśāt tataḥ strīṇāṃ mūtravacchaucamiṣyate ।। 

pañcarātraṃ tathāspṛśyā rajasā vartate yadi 
sā viṃśaddivasādūrdhvaṃ rajasā pūrvavattathā ।। 

snānaṃ śaucaṃ tathā gānaṃ rodanaṃ hasanaṃ tathā 
yānamabhyañjanaṃ nārī dyūtaṃ caivānulepanam ।। 

divāsvapnaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā vai dantadhāvanam 
maithunaṃ mānasaṃ vāpi vācikaṃ devatārcanam ।। 

varjayetsarvayatnena namaskāraṃ rajasvalā 
rajasvalāṅganāsparśasaṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā ।। 

saṃtyāgaṃ caiva vastrāṇāṃ varjayetsarvayatnataḥ 
snātvānyapuruṣaṃ nārī na spṛśettu rajasvalā ।। 

īkṣayedbhāskaraṃ devaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ tataḥ pibet 
kevalaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā cātmaśuddhaye ।। 

caturthyāṃ strī na gamyā tu gato alpāyuḥ prasūyate 
vidyāhīnaṃ vratabhraṣṭaṃ patitaṃ pāradārikam ।। 

dāridryārṇavamagnaṃ ca tanayaṃ sā prasūyate 
kanyārthinaiva gantavyā pañcamyāṃ vidhivatpunaḥ ।। 

raktādhikyādbhavennārī śukrādhikye bhavetpumān 
same napuṃsakaṃ caiva pañcamyāṃ kanyakā bhavet ।। 

ṣaṣṭhyāṃ gamyā mahābhāgā satputrajananī bhavet 
putratvaṃ vyañjayettasya jātaputro mahādyutiḥ ।। 

pumiti narakasyākhyā duḥkhaṃ ca narakaṃ viduḥ 
puṃsastrāṇānvitaṃ putraṃ tathābhūtaṃ prasūyate ।। 

saptamyāṃ caiva kanyārthī gacchetsaiva prasūyate 
aṣṭamyāṃ sarvasampannaṃ tanayaṃ samprasūyate ।। 

navamyāṃ dārikāyārthī daśamyāṃ paṇḍito bhavet 
ekādaśyāṃ tathā nārīṃ janayetsaiva pūrvavat ।। 

dvādaśyāṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ śrautasmārtapravartakam 
trayodaśyāṃ jaḍāṃ nārīṃ sarvasaṃkarakāriṇīm ।। 

janayatyaṅganā yasmān na gacchetsarvayatnataḥ 
caturdaśyāṃ yadā gacchet sā putrajananī bhavet ।। 

pañcadaśyāṃ ca dharmiṣṭhāṃ ṣoḍaśyāṃ jñānapāragam 
strīṇāṃ vai maithune kāle vāmapārśve prabhañjanaḥ ।। 

caredyadi bhavennārī pumāṃsaṃ dakṣiṇe labhet 
strīṇāṃ maithunakāle tu pāpagrahavivarjite ।। 

uktakāle śucirbhūtvā śuddhāṃ gacchecchucismitām 
ityevaṃ saṃprasaṃgena yatīnāṃ dharmasaṃgrahe ।। 

sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ sadācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi sadācāraṃ śucirnaraḥ ।। 

śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān dagdhakilbiṣān 
brahmalokamanuprāpya brahmaṇā saha modate ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sadācārakathanaṃ nāmaikonanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yatīnāmiha niścitam 
prāyaścittaṃ śivaproktaṃ yatīnāṃ pāpaśodhanam ।। 

pāpaṃ hi trividhaṃ jñeyaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavam 
satataṃ hi divā rātrau yenedaṃ veṣṭyate jagat ।। 

tatkarmaṇā vināpyeṣa tiṣṭhatīti parā śrutiḥ 
kṣaṇamevaṃ prayojyaṃ tu āyuṣyaṃ tu vidhāraṇam ।। 

bhavedyogo apramattasya yogo hi paramaṃ balam 
na hi yogātparaṃ kiṃcin narāṇāṃ dṛśyate śubham ।। 

tasmād yogaṃ praśaṃsanti dharmayuktā manīṣiṇaḥ 
avidyāṃ vidyayā jitvā prāpyaiśvaryamanuttamam ।। 

dṛṣṭvā parāvaraṃ dhīrāḥ paraṃ gacchanti tatpadam 
vratāni yāni bhikṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca ।। 

ekaikātikrame teṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate 
upetya tu striyaṃ kāmāt prāyaścittaṃ vinirdiśet ।। 

prāṇāyāmasamāyuktaṃ caretsāṃtapanaṃ vratam 
tataścarati nirdeśāt kṛcchraṃ cānte samāhitaḥ ।। 

punar āśramam āgatya caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ 
na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। 

tathāpi na ca kartavyaṃ prasaṃgo hyeṣa dāruṇaḥ 
ahorātropavāsaś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā ।। 

asadvādo na kartavyo yatinā dharmalipsunā 
paramāpadgatenāpi na kāryaṃ steyamapyuta ।। 

steyādabhyadhikaḥ kaścin nāstyadharma iti śrutiḥ 
hiṃsā hyeṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyaṃ vai kathitaṃ tathā ।। 

yadetaddraviṇaṃ nāma prāṇā hyete bahiścarāḥ 
sa tasya harate prāṇān yo yasya harate dhanam ।। 

evaṃ kṛtvā suduṣṭātmā bhinnavṛtto vratāccyutaḥ 
bhūyo nirvedamāpannaś careccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam ।। 

vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena saṃvatsaramiti śrutiḥ 
tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte bhūyaḥ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ 
punarnirvedamāpannaś caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ ।। 

ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ karmaṇā manasā girā 
akāmādapi hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn ।। 

kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ kurvīta cāndrāyaṇamathāpi vā 
skandedindriyadaurbalyāt striyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiryadi ।। 

tena dhārayitavyā vai prāṇāyāmāstu ṣoḍaśa 
divā skannasya viprasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ।। 

trirātramupavāsāś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā 
rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśaiva tu dhāraṇā ।। 

prāṇāyāmena śuddhātmā virajā jāyate dvijāḥ 
ekānnaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ vā aśṛtānnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

abhojyāni yatīnāṃ tu pratyakṣalavaṇāni ca 
ekaikātikramātteṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ।। 

prājāpatyena kṛcchreṇa tataḥ pāpātpramucyate 
vyatikramāś ca ye kecid vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavāḥ ।। 

sadbhiḥ saha viniścitya yadbrūyustatsamācaret ।। 

careddhi śuddhaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ samastabhūteṣu ca satsamāhitaḥ 
sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ śāśvatamavyayaṃ tu paraṃ hi gatvā na punarhi jāyate ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yatiprāyaścittaṃ nāma navatitamo adhyāyaḥ

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ariṣṭāni nibodhata 
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।। 

arundhatīṃ dhruvaṃ caiva somachāyāṃ mahāpatham 
yo na paśyenna jīvetsa naraḥ saṃvatsarātparam ।। 

ariśmavantam ādityaṃ raśmivantaṃ ca pāvakam 
yaḥ paśyati na jīvedvai māsādekādaśātparam ।। 

vamenmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā 
pratyakṣamathavā svapne daśamāsānna jīvati ।। 

rukmavarṇaṃ drumaṃ paśyed gandharvanagarāṇi ca 
paśyet pretapiśācāṃś ca navamāsān sa jīvati ।। 

akasmācca bhavetsthūlo hy akasmācca kṛśo bhavet 
prakṛteś ca nivarteta cāṣṭau māsāṃś ca jīvati ।। 

agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi khaṇḍaṃ yasya padaṃ bhavet 
pāṃsuke kardame vāpi saptamāsānsa jīvati ।। 

kākaḥ kapoto gṛdhro vā nilīyedyasya mūrdhani 
kravyādo vā khago yasya ṣaṇmāsān nātivartate ।। 

gacched vāyasapaṅktībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā punaḥ 
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyec catuḥpañca sa jīvati ।। 

anabhre vidyutaṃ paśyed dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāsthitām 
udake dhanur aindraṃ vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati ।। 

apsu vā yadi vādarśe yo hyātmānaṃ na paśyati 
aśiraskaṃ tathā paśyen māsād ūrdhvaṃ na jīvati ।। 

śavagandhi bhavedgātraṃ vasāgandhamathāpi vā 
mṛtyurhyupāgatastasya ardhamāsānna jīvati ।। 

yasya vai snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pariśuṣyati 
dhūmaṃ vā mastakātpaśyed daśāhānna sa jīvati ।। 

saṃbhinno māruto yasya marmasthānāni kṛntati 
adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। 

ṛkṣavānarayuktena rathenāśāṃ ca dakṣiṇām 
gāyannṛtyan vrajet svapne vidyānmṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। 

kṛṣṇāṃbaradharā śyāmā gāyantī vāpyathāṅganā 
yaṃ nayeddakṣiṇāmāśāṃ svapne so api na jīvati ।। 

chidraṃ vā svasya kaṇṭhasya svapne yo vīkṣate naraḥ 
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyānmṛtyumupasthitam ।। 

ā mastakatalādyas tu nimajjetpaṅkasāgare 
dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśaṃ svapnaṃ sadya eva na jīvati ।। 

bhasmāṅgārāṃś ca keśāṃś ca nadīṃ śuṣkāṃ bhujaṅgamān 
paśyedyo daśarātraṃ tu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ ।। 

kṛṣṇaiś ca vikaṭaiścaiva puruṣairudyatāyudhaiḥ 
pāṣāṇaistāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyo na sa jīvati ।। 

sūryodaye pratyuṣasi pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ 
krośantyabhimukhaṃ pretya sa gatāyurbhavennaraḥ ।। 

yasya vā snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate bhṛśam 
jāyate dantaharṣaś ca taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet ।। 

bhūyobhūyastrasedyastu rātrau vā yadi vā divā 
dīpagandhaṃ ca nāghrāti vidyānmṛtyum upasthitam ।। 

rātrau cendradhanuḥ paśyed divā nakṣatramaṇḍalam 
paranetreṣu cātmānaṃ na paśyenna sa jīvati ।। 

netramekaṃ sravedyasya karṇau sthānācca bhraśyataḥ 
vakrā ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyo gatajīvitaḥ ।। 

yasya kṛṣṇā kharā jihvā padmābhāsaṃ ca vai mukham 
gaṇḍe vā piṇḍikārakte tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। 

muktakeśo hasaṃścaiva gāyannṛtyaṃś ca yo naraḥ 
yāmyāmabhimukhaṃ gacchet tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। 

yasya śvetaghanābhāsā śvetasarṣapasaṃnibhā 
śvetā ca mūrtirhyasakṛt tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। 

uṣṭrā vā rāsabhā vābhiyuktāḥ svapne rathe śubhāḥ 
yasya so api na jīvettu dakṣiṇābhimukho gataḥ ।। 

dve vātha parame ariṣṭe ekībhūtaḥ paraṃ bhavet 
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotir netre na paśyati ।। 

śvabhre yo nipatetsvapne dvāraṃ cāpi pidhīyate 
na cottiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāt tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। 
ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭirna ca sampratiṣṭhā raktā punaḥ samparivartamānā । 
mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiratyuṣṇamūtro viṣamastha eva ।। 

divā vā yadi vā rātrau pratyakṣaṃ yo nihanyate 
hantāraṃ na ca paśyecca sa gatāyurna jīvati ।। 

agnipraveśaṃ kurute svapnānte yastu mānavaḥ 
smṛtiṃ nopalabheccāpi tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। 

yastu prāvaraṇaṃ śuklaṃ svakaṃ paśyati mānavaḥ 
kṛṣṇaṃ raktamapi svapne tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ ।। 

ariṣṭe sūcite dehe tasminkāla upasthite 
tyaktvā khedaṃ viṣādaṃ ca upekṣed buddhimān naraḥ ।। 

prācīṃ vā yadi vodīcīṃ diśaṃ niṣkramya vai śuciḥ 
same atisthāvare deśe vivikte jantuvarjite ।। 

udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā svasthaś cācānta eva ca 
svastikenopaviṣṭastu namaskṛtvā maheśvaram ।। 

samakāyaśirogrīvo dhārayan nāvalokayet 
yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā ।। 

prāgudakpravaṇe deśe tathā yuñjīta śāstravit 
kāmaṃ vitarkaṃ prītiṃ ca sukhaduḥkhe ubhe tathā ।। 

nigṛhya manasā sarvaṃ śuklaṃ dhyānam anusmaret 
ghrāṇe ca rasane nityaṃ cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā ।। 

śrotre manasi buddhau ca tatra vakṣasi dhārayet 
kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣveva nityaśaḥ ।। 

dvādaśādhyātmamityevaṃ yogadhāraṇamucyate 
śatamardhaśataṃ vāpi dhāraṇāṃ mūrdhni dhārayet ।। 

khinnasya dhāraṇāyogād vāyurūrdhvaṃ pravartate 
tataścāpūrayed deham oṅkāreṇa samanvitaḥ ।। 

tathauṃkāramayo yogī akṣare tvakṣarī bhavet 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi oṅkāraprāptilakṣaṇam ।। 

eṣa trimātro vijñeyo vyañjanaṃ cātra ceśvaraḥ 
prathamā vidyutī mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā ।। 

tṛtīyāṃ nirguṇāṃ caiva mātrāmakṣaragāminīm 
gāndhārī caiva vijñeyā gāndhārasvarasaṃbhavā ।। 

pipīlikāgatisparśā prayuktā mūrdhni lakṣyate 
yathā prayukta oṅkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani ।। 

tathauṃkāramayo yogī tv akṣarī tvakṣarī bhavet 
praṇavo dhanuḥ śaro hyātmā brahmalakṣaṇamucyate ।। 

apramattena veddhavyaṃ śaravat tanmayo bhavet 
omityekākṣaraṃ hyetad guhāyāṃ nihitaṃ padam ।। 

omityetattrayo lokās trayo vedāstrayo agnayaḥ 
viṣṇukramāstrayastvete ṛksāmāni yajūṃṣi ca ।। 

mātrā cārdhaṃ ca tisrastu vijñeyāḥ paramārthataḥ 
tatprayuktastu yo yogī tasya sālokyamāpnuyāt ।। 

akāro hyakṣaro jñeya ukāraḥ sahitaḥ smṛtaḥ 
makārasahitauṃkāras trimātra iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। 

akāras tveṣa bhūrloka ukāro bhuva ucyate 
savyañjano makārastu svarloka iti gīyate ।। 

oṅkārastu trayo lokāḥ śirastasya triviṣṭapam 
bhuvanāṅgaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ brāhmaṃ tatpadamucyate ।। 

mātrāpādo rudraloko hy amātraṃ tu śivaṃ padam 
evaṃ jñānaviśeṣeṇa tatpadaṃ samupāsyate ।। 

tasmāddhyānaratirnityam amātraṃ hi tadakṣaram 
upāsyaṃ hi prayatnena śāśvataṃ sukhamicchatā ।। 

hrasvā tu prathamā mātrā tato dīrghā tvanantaram 
tataḥ plutavatī caiva tṛtīyā copadiśyate ।। 

etāstu mātrā vijñeyā yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
yāvadeva tu śakyante dhāryante tāvadeva hi ।। 

indriyāṇi mano buddhiṃ dhyāyannātmani yaḥ sadā 
ardhaṃ tanmātram api cec chṛṇu yat phalamāpnuyāt ।। 

māse māse aśvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ 
tena yatprāpyate puṇyaṃ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt ।। 

na tathā tapasogreṇa na yajñairbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ 
yatphalaṃ prāpyate samyaṅ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt ।। 

tatra caiṣā tu yā mātrā plutā nāmopadiśyate 
eṣā eva bhavetkāryā gṛhasthānāṃ tu yoginām ।। 

eṣāṃ caiva viśeṣeṇa aiśvarye hyaṣṭalakṣaṇe 
aṇimādye tu vijñeyā tasmādyuñjīta tāṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

evaṃ hi yogasaṃyuktaḥ śucir dānto jitendriyaḥ 
ātmānaṃ vidyate yastu sa sarvaṃ vindate dvijāḥ ।। 

tasmātpāśupatairyogair ātmānaṃ cintayedbudhaḥ 
ātmānaṃ jānate ye tu śucayaste na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni vedopaniṣadas tathā 
yogajñānādavāpnoti brāhmaṇo adhyātmacintakaḥ ।। 

sarvadevamayo bhūtvā abhūtaḥ sa tu jāyate 
yonisaṃkramaṇaṃ tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvataṃ padam ।। 

yathā vṛkṣāt phalaṃ pakvaṃ pavanena samīritam 
namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati ।। 

yatra rudranamaskāraḥ sarvakarmaphalo dhruvaḥ 
anyadevanamaskārān na tatphalamavāpnuyāt ।। 

tasmāttriḥpravaṇaṃ yogī upāsīta maheśvaram 
daśavistārakaṃ brahma tathā ca brahmavistaraiḥ ।। 

evaṃ dhyānasamāyuktaḥ svadehaṃ yaḥ parityajet 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ samuddhṛtya kulatrayam ।। 

athavāriṣṭamālokya maraṇe samupasthite 
avimukteśvaraṃ gatvā vārāṇasyāṃ tu śodhanam ।। 

yena kenāpi vā dehaṃ saṃtyajen mucyate naraḥ 
śrīparvate vā viprendrāḥ saṃtyajetsvatanuṃ naraḥ ।। 

sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
avimuktaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ jantūnāṃ muktidaṃ sadā ।। 

seveta satataṃ dhīmān viśeṣānmaraṇāntike ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ariṣṭakathanaṃ nāma ekanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

evaṃ vārāṇasī puṇyā yadi sūta mahāmate 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatprabhāvaṃ hi sāṃpratam ।। 

kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śobhanam 
vistareṇa yathānyāyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। 

vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ samyak vārāṇasyāḥ suśobhanam 
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ yathāha bhagavān bhavaḥ ।। 

vistareṇa mayā vaktuṃ brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā 
śakyate naiva viprendrā varṣakoṭiśatairapi ।। 

devaḥ purā kṛtodvāhaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ 
himavacchikharāddevyā haimavatyā gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। 

vārāṇasīmanuprāpya darśayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ 
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vāsaṃ tatra cakāra saḥ ।। 

vārāṇasīkurukṣetraśrīparvatamahālaye 
tuṅgeśvare ca kedāre tatsthāne yo yatirbhavet ।। 

yoge pāśupate samyak dinamekaṃ yatirbhavet 
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya caret pāśupataṃ vratam ।। 

devodyāne vasettatra śarvodyānamanuttamam 
manasā nirmame rudro vimānaṃ ca suśobhanam ।। 

darśayāmāsa ca tadā devodyānamanuttamam 
haimavatyāḥ svayaṃ devaḥ sanandī parameśvaraḥ ।। 

kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śaṅkaraḥ 
uktavānparameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prītaye bhavaḥ ।। 

praphullanānāvidhagulmaśobhitaṃ latāpratānādimanoharaṃ bahiḥ 
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiś ca ketakaiḥ ।। 

tamālagulmairnicitaṃ sugandhibhir nikāmapuṣpairvakulaiś ca sarvataḥ 
aśokapunnāgaśataiḥ supuṣpitair dvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ ।। 

kvacit praphullāmbujareṇubhūṣitair vihaṅgamaiś cānukalapraṇādibhiḥ 
vināditaṃ sārasacakravākaiḥ pramattadātyūhavaraiś ca sarvataḥ ।। 

kvacicca kekārutanāditaṃ śubhaṃ kvacicca kāraṇḍavanādanāditam 
kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtaṃ madākulābhir bhramarāṅganādibhiḥ ।। 

niṣevitaṃ cārusugandhipuṣpakaiḥ kvacit supuṣpaiḥ sahakāravṛkṣaiḥ 
latopagūḍhaistilakaiś ca gūḍhaṃ pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇam ।। 

pravṛttanṛttānugatāpsarogaṇaṃ prahṛṣṭanānāvidhapakṣisevitam 
pranṛttahārītakulopanāditaṃ mṛgendranādākulamattamānasaiḥ ।। 

kvacit kvacid gandhakadambakair mṛgair vilūnadarbhāṅkurapuṣpasaṃcayam 
praphullanānāvidhacārupaṅkajaiḥ sarastaḍāgairupaśobhitaṃ kvacit ।।
