viṭapanicayalīnaṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhirāmaṃ madamuditavihaṅgaṃ prāptanādābhirāmam 
kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephaṃ navakisalayaśobhāśobhitaṃ prāṃśuśākham ।। 
kvacicca dantakṣatacāruvīrudhaṃ kvacillatāliṅgitacāruvṛkṣakam । 
kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhir niṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ ।। 

pārāvatadhvanivikūjitacāruśṛṅgair abhraṅkaṣaiḥ sitamanoharacārurūpaiḥ 
ākīrṇapuṣpanikarapravibhaktahaṃsair vibhrājitaṃ tridaśadivyakulairanekaiḥ ।। 

phullotpalāṃbujavitānasahasrayuktaṃ toyāśayaiḥ samanuśobhitadevamārgam 
mārgāntarākalitapuṣpavicitrapaṅktisambaddhagulmaviṭapair vividhairupetam ।। 

tuṅgāgrair nīlapuṣpastabakabharanataprāṃśuśākhair aśokair dolāprāntāntanīlaśrutisukhajanakair bhāsitāntaṃ manojñaiḥ 
rātrau candrasya bhāsā kusumitatilakairekatāṃ samprayātaṃ chāyāsuptaprabuddhasthitahariṇakulāluptadūrvāṅkurāgram ।। 

haṃsānāṃ pakṣavātapracalitakamalasvacchavistīrṇatoyaṃ toyānāṃ tīrajātapracakitakadalīcāṭunṛtyanmayūram 
māyūraiḥ pakṣacandraiḥ kvacidavanigatai rañjitakṣmāpradeśaṃ deśe deśe vilīnapramuditavilasanmattahārītavṛndam ।। 

sāraṅgaiḥ kvacidupaśobhitapradeśaṃ pracchannaṃ kusumacayaiḥ kvacidvicitraiḥ 
hṛṣṭābhiḥ kvacidapi kinnarāṅganābhir vīṇābhiḥ sumadhuragītanṛttakaṇṭham ।। 

saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupaliptakīrṇapuṣpair āvāsaiḥ parivṛtapādapaṃ munīnām 
ā mūlāt phalanicitaiḥ kvacidviśālair uttuṅgaiḥ panasamahīruhairupetam ।। 
phullātimuktakalatāgṛhanītasiddhasiddhāṅganākanakanūpurarāvaramyam । 
ramyaṃ priyaṅgutarumañjarisaktabhṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgāvalīkavalitāmrakadambapuṣpam ।। 

puṣpotkarānilavighūrṇitavāriramyaṃ ramyadvirephavinipātitamañjugulmam 
gulmāntaraprasabhabhītamṛgīsamūhaṃ vāteritaṃ tanubhṛtāmapavargadātṛ ।। 

candrāṃśujālaśabalais tilakair manojñaiḥ sindūrakuṅkumakusumbhanibhair aśokaiḥ 
cāmīkaradyutisamairatha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpotkarairupacitaṃ suviśālaśākhaiḥ ।। 

kvacidañjanacūrṇābhaiḥ kvacid vidrumasannibhaiḥ 
kvacitkāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpair ācitabhūtalam ।। 

punnāgeṣu dvijaśatavirutaṃ raktāśokastabakabharanatam 
ramyopāntaklamahārabhavanaṃ phullābjeṣu bhramaravilasitam ।। 

sakalabhuvanabhartā lokanāthastadānīṃ tuhinaśikharaputryā sārdhamiṣṭairgaṇeśaiḥ 
vividhataruviśālaṃ mattahṛṣṭānnapuṣṭair upavanam atiramyaṃ darśayāmāsa devyāḥ ।। 

puṣpairvanyaiḥ śubhaśubhatamaiḥ kalpitairdivyabhūṣair devīṃ divyāmupavanagatāṃ bhūṣayāmāsa śarvaḥ 
sā cāpyenaṃ tuhinagirisutā śaṅkaraṃ devadevaṃ puṣpairdivyaiḥ śubhataratamair bhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā ।। 

sampūjya pūjyaṃ tridaśeśvarāṇāṃ samprekṣya codyānam atīva ramyam 
gaṇeśvarair nandimukhaiś ca sārdham uvāca devaṃ praṇipatya devī ।। 

udyānaṃ darśitaṃ deva prabhayā parayā yutam 
kṣetrasya ca guṇānsarvān punarme vaktumarhasi ।। 

asya kṣetrasya māhātmyam avimuktasya sarvathā 
vaktumarhasi deveśa devadeva vṛṣadhvaja ।। 

devyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo varaprabhuḥ 
āghrāya vadanāmbhojaṃ tadāha girijāṃ hasan ।। 

idaṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ sadā vārāṇasī mama 
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā ।। 

asminsiddhāḥ sadā devi madīyaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ 
nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। 

abhyasyanti paraṃ yogaṃ yuktātmāno jitendriyāḥ 
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagaśobhite ।। 

kamalotpalapuṣpāḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte 
apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ sadā saṃsevite śubhe ।। 

rocate me sadā vāso yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu 
manmanā mama bhaktaś ca mayi nityārpitakriyaḥ ।। 

yathā mokṣamavāpnoti anyatra na tathā kvacit 
kāmaṃ hyatra mṛto devi janturmokṣāya kalpate ।। 

etanmama puraṃ divyaṃ guhyādguhyatamaṃ mahat 
brahmādayo vijānanti ye ca siddhā mumukṣavaḥ ।। 

ataḥ paramidaṃ kṣetraṃ parā ceyaṃ gatirmama 
vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmān mokṣyate vā kadācana ।। 

mama kṣetramidaṃ tasmād avimuktamiti smṛtam 
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare ।। 

snānātsaṃsevanādvāpi na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yataḥ 
iha samprāpyate yena tata etadviśiṣyate ।। 

prayāge vā bhavenmokṣa iha vā matparigrahāt 
prayāgādapi tīrthāgryād avimuktamidaṃ śubham ।। 

dharmasyopaniṣat satyaṃ mokṣasyopaniṣac chamaḥ 
kṣetratīrthopaniṣadaṃ na vidurbudhasattamāḥ ।। 

kāmaṃ bhuñjan svapan krīḍan kurvan hi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ 
avimukte tyajetprāṇān janturmokṣāya kalpate ।। 

kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām 
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā ।। 

tasmātsaṃsevanīyaṃ hi avimuktaṃ hi muktaye 
jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ gato yatra mahātapāḥ ।। 

asya kṣetrasya māhātmyād bhaktyā ca mama bhāvitaḥ 
jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānamiṣyate ।। 

dhyāyantastatra māṃ nityaṃ yogāgnirdīpyate bhṛśam 
kaivalyaṃ paramaṃ yāti devānāmapi durlabham ।। 

avyaktaliṅgairmunibhiḥ sarvasiddhāntavedibhiḥ 
iha samprāpyate mokṣo durlabho anyatra karhicit ।। 

tebhyaścāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaiśvaryamanuttamam 
ātmanaścaiva sāyujyam īpsitaṃ sthānameva ca ।। 

kubero atra mama kṣetre mayi sarvārpitakriyaḥ 
kṣetrasaṃsevanādeva gaṇeśatvamavāpa ha ।। 

saṃvarto bhavitā yaś ca so api bhakto mamaiva tu 
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām ।। 

parāśarasutau yogī ṛṣirvyāso mahātapāḥ 
mama bhakto bhaviṣyaś ca vedasaṃsthāpravartakaḥ ।। 

raṃsyate so api padmākṣi kṣetre asminmunipuṅgavaḥ 
brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāpi divākaraḥ ।। 

devarājastathā śakro ye api cānye divaukasaḥ 
upāsate mahātmānaḥ sarve māmiha suvrate ।। 

anye api yogino divyāś channarūpā mahātmanaḥ 
ananyamanaso bhūtvā māmihopāsate sadā ।। 

viṣayāsaktacitto api tyaktadharmaratirnaraḥ 
iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ so api saṃsāre na punarbhavet ।। 

ye punarnirmamā dhīrāḥ sattvasthā vijitendriyāḥ 
vratinaś ca nirārambhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ ।। 

devadevaṃ samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṃgavarjitāḥ 
gatā iha paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate ।। 

janmāntarasahasreṣu yaṃ na yogī samāpnuyāt 
tamihaiva paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate ।। 

goprekṣakam idaṃ kṣetraṃ brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ purā 
kailāsabhavanaṃ cātra paśya divyaṃ varānane ।। 

goprekṣakam athāgamya dṛṣṭvā māmatra mānavaḥ 
na durgatimavāpnoti kalmaṣaiś ca vimucyate ।। 

kapilāhradam ityevaṃ tathā vai brahmaṇā kṛtam 
gavāṃ stanyajatoyena tīrthaṃ puṇyatamaṃ mahat ।। 

atrāpi svayamevāhaṃ vṛṣadhvaja iti smṛtaḥ 
sānnidhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sadāhaṃ dṛśyate tvayā ।। 

bhadratoyaṃ ca paśyeha brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ hradam 
sarvairdevairahaṃ devi asmindeśe prasāditaḥ ।। 

gacchopaśamam īśeti upaśāntaḥ śivas tathā 
atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā ।। 

brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punaḥ 
brahmaṇāpi tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā ।। 

mayānītamidaṃ liṅgaṃ kasmāt sthāpitavān asi 
tamuvāca punar viṣṇur brahmāṇaṃ kupitānanam ।। 

rudre deve mamātyantaṃ parā bhaktirmahattarā 
mayaiva sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ tava nāmnā bhaviṣyati ।। 

hiraṇyagarbha ityevaṃ tato atrāhaṃ samāsthitaḥ 
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ ।। 

tataḥ punarapi brahmā mama liṅgamidaṃ śubham 
sthāpayāmāsa vidhivad bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ ।। 

svarlīneśvara ityevam atrāhaṃ svayamāgataḥ 
prāṇān iha narastyaktvā na punarjāyate kvacit ।। 

ananyā sā gatistasya yogināṃ caiva yā smṛtā 
asminnapi mayā deśe daityo daivatakaṇṭakaḥ ।। 

vyāghrarūpaṃ samāsthāya nihato darpito balī 
vyāghreśvara iti khyāto nityamatrāhamāsthitaḥ ।। 

na punardurgatiṃ yāti dṛṣṭvainaṃ vyāghramīśvaram 
utpalo vidalaścaiva yau daityau brahmaṇā purā ।। 

strīvadhyau darpitau dṛṣṭvā tvayaiva nihatau raṇe 
sāvajñaṃ kandukenātra tasyedaṃ dehamāsthitam ।। 

ādāvatrāhamāgamya prasthito gaṇapaiḥ saha 
jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃ tasmād etanme puṇyadarśanam ।। 

devaiḥ samantād etāni liṅgāni sthāpitānyataḥ 
dṛṣṭvāpi niyato martyo dehabhede gaṇo bhavet ।। 

pitrā te śailarājena purā himavatā svayam 
mama priyahitaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। 

śaileśvaramiti khyātaṃ dṛśyatāmiha cādarāt 
dṛṣṭvaitanmanujo devi na durgatimato vrajet ।। 

nadyeṣā varuṇā devi puṇyā pāpapramocanī 
kṣetrametad alaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā ।। 

sthāpitaṃ brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgame liṅgamuttamam 
saṃgameśvaram ityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām ।। 

saṃgame devanadyā hi yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ 
arcayet saṃgameśvaraṃ tasya janmabhayaṃ kutaḥ ।। 

idaṃ manye mahākṣetraṃ nivāso yogināṃ param 
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvāgramāsthitaḥ ।। 

madhyameśvaramityevaṃ khyātaḥ sarvasurāsuraiḥ 
siddhānāṃ sthānametaddhi madīyavratadhāriṇām ।। 

yogināṃ mokṣalipsūnāṃ jñānayogaratātmanām 
dṛṣṭvainaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janma prati na śocati ।। 

sthāpitaṃ liṅgametattu śukreṇa bhṛgusūnunā 
nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam ।। 

dṛṣṭvainaṃ niyataḥ sadyo mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ 
mṛtaś ca na punarjantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavennaraḥ ।। 

purā jambūkarūpeṇa asuro devakaṇṭakaḥ 
brahmaṇo hi varaṃ labdhvā gomāyurbandhaśaṅkitaḥ ।। 

nihato himavatputri jambūkeśastato hyaham 
adyāpi jagati khyātaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।। 

dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt 
grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiś ca etāni sthāpitāni ha ।। 

paśya puṇyāni liṅgāni sarvakāmapradāni tu 
evametāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati ।। 

kathitāni mama kṣetre guhyaṃ cānyadidaṃ śṛṇu 
catuḥkrośaṃ caturdikṣu kṣetrametatprakīrtitam ।। 

yojanaṃ viddhi cārvaṅgi mṛtyukāle amṛtapradam 
mahālayagiristhaṃ māṃ kedāre ca vyavasthitam ।। 

gaṇatvaṃ labhate dṛṣṭvā hy asminmokṣo hyavāpyate 
gāṇapatyaṃ labhedyasmād yataḥ sā muktiruttamā ।। 

tato mahālayāt tasmāt kedārānmadhyamādapi 
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetram avimuktaṃ varānane ।। 

kedāraṃ madhyamaṃ kṣetraṃ sthānaṃ caiva mahālayam 
mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam ।। 

yataḥ sṛṣṭāstvime lokās tataḥ kṣetramidaṃ śubham 
kadācinna mayā muktam avimuktaṃ tato abhavat ।। 

avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mama dṛṣṭveha mānavaḥ 
sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate ।। 

śaileśaṃ saṃgameśaṃ ca svarlīnaṃ madhyameśvaram 
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। 

upaśāntaṃ śivaṃ caiva jyeṣṭhasthānanivāsinam 
śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jambukeśvaram ।। 

dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare 
evam uktvā mahādevo diśaḥ sarvā vyalokayat ।। 

vilokya saṃsthite paścād devadeve maheśvare 
akasmādabhavatsarvaḥ sa deśojjvalito yathā ।। 

tataḥ pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmābhyaṅgasitaprabhāḥ 
māheśvarā mahātmānas tathā vai niyatavratāḥ ।। 

bahavaḥ śataśo abhyetya namaścakrurmaheśvaram 
punarnirīkṣya yogeśaṃ dhyānayogaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। 

tasthurātmānamāsthāya līyamānā iveśvare 
sthitānāṃ sa tadā teṣāṃ devadeva umāpatiḥ ।। 

sa bibhratparamāṃ mūrtiṃ babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ 
kṛtsnaṃ jagadihaikasthaṃ kartum anta iva sthitaḥ ।। 

tasya tāṃ paramāṃ mūrtim āsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ 
na śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ hṛṣṭaromā girīndrajā ।। 

tatastvadṛṣṭamākāraṃ buddhvā sā prakṛtisthitam 
prakṛtermūrtimāsthāya yogena parameśvarī ।। 

taṃ śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ harasya ca mahātmanaḥ 
tataste layamādhāya yoginaḥ puruṣasya tu ।। 

viviśurhṛdayaṃ sarve dagdhasaṃsārabījinaḥ 
pañcākṣarasya vai bījaṃ saṃsmarantaḥ suśobhanam ।। 

sarvapāpaharaṃ divyaṃ purā caiva prakāśitam 
nīlalohitamūrtisthaṃ punaścakre vapuḥ śubham ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhā 
stuvatī caraṇau natvā ka ime bhagavanniti ।। 

tāmuvāca suraśreṣṭhas tadā devīṃ girīndrajām 
madīyaṃ vratamāśritya bhaktimadbhir dvijottamaiḥ ।। 

yairyairyogā ihābhyastās teṣām ekena janmanā 
kṣetrasyāsya prabhāvena bhaktyā ca mama bhāmini ।। 

anugraho mayā hyevaṃ kriyate mūrtitaḥ svayam 
tasmād etan mahat kṣetraṃ brahmādyaiḥ sevitaṃ tathā ।। 

śrutimadbhiś ca viprendraiḥ saṃsiddhaiś ca tapasvibhiḥ 
pratimāsaṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ pratimāsaṃ caturdaśīm ।। 

ubhayoḥ pakṣayordevi vārāṇasyāmupāsyate 
śaśibhānūparāge ca kārtikyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। 

sarvaparvasu puṇyeṣu viṣuveṣvayaneṣu ca 
pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrthāni vārāṇasyāṃ tu jāhnavīm ।। 

uttarapravahāṃ puṇyāṃ mama mauliviniḥsṛtām 
pituste girirājasya śubhāṃ himavataḥ sutām ।। 

puṇyasthānasthitāṃ puṇyāṃ puṇyadikpravahāṃ sadā 
bhajante sarvato abhyetya ye tāñchṛṇu varānane ।। 

saṃnihatya kurukṣetraṃ sārdhaṃ tīrthaśatais tathā 
puṣkaraṃ nimiṣaṃ caiva prayāgaṃ ca pṛthūdakam ।। 

drumakṣetraṃ kurukṣetraṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthasaṃyutam 
kṣetrāṇi sarvato devi devatā ṛṣayas tathā ।। 

saṃdhyā ca ṛtavaścaiva sarvā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca 
samudrāḥ sapta caivātra devatīrthāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। 

bhāgīrathīṃ sameṣyanti sarvaparvasu suvrate 
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā caiva triviṣṭapam ।। 

kālabhairavamāsādya dhūtapāpāni sarvaśaḥ 
bhavanti hi sureśāni sarvaparvasu parvasu ।। 

pṛthivyāṃ yāni puṇyāni mahāntyāyatanāni ca 
praviśanti sadābhyetya puṇyaṃ parvasu parvasu 
avimuktaṃ kṣetravaraṃ mahāpāpanibarhaṇam ।। 

kedāre caiva yalliṅgaṃ yacca liṅgaṃ mahālaye ।। 

madhyameśvarasaṃjñaṃ ca tathā pāśupateśvaram 
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ caiva gokarṇau ca tathā hyubhau ।। 

drumacaṇḍeśvaraṃ nāma bhadreśvaram anuttamam 
sthāneśvaraṃ tathaikāgraṃ kāleśvaram ajeśvaram ।। 

bhairaveśvaram īśānaṃ tathauṃkārakasaṃjñitam 
amareśaṃ mahākālaṃ jyotiṣaṃ bhasmagātrakam ।। 

yāni cānyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhūtale 
aṣṭaṣaṣṭisamākhyāni rūḍhānyanyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। 

tāni sarvāṇyaśeṣāṇi vārāṇasyāṃ viśanti mām 
sarvaparvasu puṇyeṣu guhyaṃ caitadudāhṛtam ।। 

teneha labhate jantur mṛto divyāmṛtaṃ padam 
snātasya caiva gaṅgāyāṃ dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe ।। 

sarvayajñaphalaistulyam iṣṭaiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ 
sadya eva samāpnoti kiṃ tataḥ paramādbhutam ।। 

sarvāyatanamukhyāni divi bhūmau giriṣv api 
parātparataraṃ devī budhyasveti mayoditam ।। 

aviśabdena pāpastu vedoktaḥ kathyate dvijaiḥ 
tena muktaṃ mayā juṣṭam avimuktam ata ucyate ।। 

ityuktvā bhagavān rudraḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ 
sudṛṣṭaṃ kuru deveśi avimuktaṃ gṛhaṃ mama ।। 

ityuktvā bhagavān devas tayā sārdham umāpatiḥ 
darśayāmāsa bhagavān śrīparvatamanuttamam ।। 

avimukteśvare nityam avasacca sadā tayā 
sarvagatvācca sarvatvāt sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ ।। 

śrīparvatamanuprāpya devyā deveśvaro haraḥ 
kṣetrāṇi darśayāmāsa sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ ।। 

kuṇḍīprabhaṃ ca paramaṃ divyaṃ vaiśravaṇeśvaram 
āśāliṅgaṃ ca deveśaṃ divyaṃ yacca bileśvaram ।। 

rāmeśvaraṃ ca paramaṃ viṣṇunā yatpratiṣṭhitam 
dakṣiṇadvārapārśve tu kuṇḍaleśvaramīśvaram ।। 

pūrvadvārasamīpasthaṃ tripurāntakamuttamam 
vivṛddhaṃ giriṇā sārdhaṃ devadevanamaskṛtam ।। 

madhyameśvaramityuktaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam 
amareśvaraṃ ca varadaṃ devaiḥ pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। 

gocarmeśvaram īśānaṃ tathendreśvaram adbhutam 
karmeśvaraṃ ca vipulaṃ kāryārthaṃ brahmaṇā kṛtam ।। 

śrīmatsiddhavaṭaṃ caiva sadāvāso mamāvyaye 
ajena nirmitaṃ divyaṃ sākṣādajabilaṃ śubham ।। 

tatraiva pāduke divye madīye ca bileśvare 
tatra śṛṅgāṭakākāraṃ śṛṅgāṭācalamadhyame ।। 

śṛṅgāṭakeśvaraṃ nāma śrīdevyā tu pratiṣṭhitam 
mallikārjunakaṃ caiva mama vāsamidaṃ śubham ।। 

rajeśvaraṃ ca paryāye rajasā supratiṣṭhitam 
gajeśvaraṃ ca vaiśākhaṃ kapoteśvaramavyayam ।। 

koṭīśvaraṃ mahātīrthaṃ rudrakoṭigaṇaiḥ purā 
sevitaṃ devi paśyādya sarvasmādadhikaṃ śubham ।। 

dvidevakulasaṃjñaṃ ca brahmaṇā dakṣiṇe śubham 
uttare sthāpitaṃ caiva viṣṇunā caiva śailajam ।। 

mahāpramāṇaliṅgaṃ ca mayā pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
paścime parvate paśya brahmeśvaramaleśvaram ।। 

alaṃkṛtaṃ tvayā brahman purastān munibhiḥ saha 
ityuktvā tadgṛhe tiṣṭhad alaṃgṛhamiti smṛtam ।। 

tatrāpi tīrthaṃ tīrthajñe vyomaliṅgaṃ ca paśya me 
kadambeśvaram etaddhi skandenaiva pratiṣṭhitam ।। 

gomaṇḍaleśvaraṃ caiva nandādyaiḥ supratiṣṭhitam 
devaiḥ sarvaistu śakrādyaiḥ sthāpitāni varānane ।। 

śrīmaddevahradaprānte sthānānīmāni paśya me 
tathā hārapure devi tava hāre nipātite ।। 

tvayā hitāya jagatāṃ hārakuṇḍamidaṃ kṛtam 
śivarudrapure caiva tatkāyopari suvrate ।। 

tatra pitrā suśailena sthāpitaṃ tvacaleśvaram 
alaṃkṛtaṃ mayā brahma purastān munibhiḥ saha ।। 

caṇḍikeśvarakaṃ devi caṇḍikeśā tavātmajā 
caṇḍikānirmitaṃ sthānam aṃbikātīrtham uttamam ।। 

rucikeśvarakaṃ caiva dhāraiṣā kapilā śubhā 
eteṣu devi sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca ।। 

pūjayenmāṃ sadā bhaktyā mayā sārdhaṃ hi modate 
śrīśaile saṃtyajed dehaṃ brāhmaṇo dagdhakilbiṣaḥ ।। 

mucyate nātra saṃdeho hy avimukte yathā śubham 
mahāsnānaṃ ca yaḥ kuryād ghṛtena vidhinaiva tu ।। 

sa yāti mama sāyujyaṃ sthāneṣveteṣu suvrate 
snānaṃ palaśataṃ jñeyam abhyaṅgaṃ pañcaviṃśati ।। 

palānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahāsnānaṃ prakīrtitam 
snāpya liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ tu gavyenaiva ghṛtena ca ।। 

viśodhya sarvadravyaistu vāribhir abhiṣiñcati 
saṃmārjya śatayajñānāṃ snānena prayutaṃ tathā ।। 

pūjayā śatasāhasram anantaṃ gītavādinām 
mahāsnāne prasaktaṃ tu snānamaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam ।। 

jalena kevalenaiva gandhatoyena bhaktitaḥ 
anulepanaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ pañcaviṃśatpalena vai ।। 

śamīpuṣpaṃ ca vidhinā bilvapatraṃ ca paṅkajam 
anyānyapi ca puṣpāṇi bilvapatraṃ na saṃtyajet ।। 

caturdroṇair mahādevam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā 
daśadroṇais tu naivedyam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā ।। 

śatadroṇasamaṃ puṇyam āḍhake api vidhīyate 
vittahīnasya viprasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

bherīmṛdaṅgamurajatimirāpaṭahādibhiḥ 
vāditrairvividhaiścānyair ninādairvividhairapi ।। 

jāgaraṃ kārayedyastu prārthayecca yathākramam 
sa bhṛtyaputradāraiś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ ।। 

sārdhaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā prārthayelliṅgam uttamam 
dravyahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ sureśvara ।। 

kṛtaṃ vā na kṛtaṃ vāpi kṣantumarhasi śaṅkara 
ityuktvā vai japedrudraṃ tvaritaṃ śāntimeva ca ।। 

japitvaivaṃ mahābījaṃ tathā pañcākṣarasya vai 
sa evaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam ।। 

tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti vārāṇasyāṃ yathā mṛtaḥ 
tathaiva mama sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 

matpriyārthamidaṃ kāryaṃ madbhaktairvidhipūrvakam 
ye na kurvanti te bhaktā na bhavanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

niśamya vacanaṃ devī gatvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm 
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ payasā ca ghṛtena ca ।। 

arcayāmāsa deveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam 
avimukte ca tapasā mandarasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 

kalpayāmāsa vai kṣetraṃ mandare cārukandare 
tatrāndhakaṃ mahādaityaṃ hiraṇyākṣasutaṃ prabhuḥ ।। 

anugṛhya gaṇatvaṃ ca prāpayāmāsa līlayā 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamādarāt ।। 

yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam 
sarvakṣetreṣu yatpuṇyaṃ tatsarvaṃ sahasā labhet ।। 

śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān kṛtaśaucān jitendriyān 
sa eva sarvayajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vārāṇasīśrīśailamāhātmyakathanaṃ nāma dvinavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

andhako nāma daityendro mandare cārukandare 
damitastu kathaṃ lebhe gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt ।। 

vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāśrutam 
andhakānugrahaṃ caiva mandare śoṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। 

varalābhamaśeṣaṃ ca pravadāmi samāsataḥ 
hiraṇyākṣasya tanayo hiraṇyanayanopamaḥ ।। 

purāndhaka iti khyātas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ 
prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ sākṣād avadhyatvamavāpya ca ।। 

trailokyamakhilaṃ bhuktvā jitvā cendrapuraṃ purā 
līlayā cāprayatnena trāsayāmāsa vāsavam ।। 

bādhitāstāḍitā baddhāḥ pātitāstena te surāḥ 
viviśurmandaraṃ bhītā nārāyaṇapurogamāḥ ।। 

evaṃ saṃpīḍya vai devān andhako api mahāsuraḥ 
yadṛcchayā giriṃ prāpto mandaraṃ cārukandaram ।। 

tataste samastāḥ surendrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sureśaṃ maheśaṃ puretyāhurevam 
drutaṃ cālpavīryaprabhinnāṅgabhinnā vayaṃ daityarājasya śastrairnikṛttāḥ ।। 

itīdamakhilaṃ śrutvā daityāgamam anaupamam 
gaṇeśvaraiś ca bhagavān andhakābhimukhaṃ yayau ।। 
tatrendrapadmodbhavaviṣṇumukhyāḥ sureśvarā vipravarāś ca sarve । 
jayeti vācā bhagavantam ūcuḥ kirīṭabaddhāñjalayaḥ samantāt ।। 

athāśeṣāsurāṃstasya koṭikoṭiśatais tataḥ 
bhasmīkṛtya mahādevo nirbibhedāndhakaṃ tadā ।। 

śūlena śūlinā protaṃ dagdhakalmaṣakañcukam 
dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ nanādeśaṃ praṇamya sa pitāmahaḥ ।। 

tannādaśravaṇānnedur devā devaṃ praṇamya tam 
nanṛturmunayaḥ sarve mumudurgaṇapuṅgavāḥ ।। 

sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi devāḥ śaṃbhostadopari 
trailokyamakhilaṃ harṣān nananda ca nanāda ca ।। 

dagdho agninā ca śūlena protaḥ preta ivāndhakaḥ 
sāttvikaṃ bhāvamāsthāya cintayāmāsa cetasā ।। 

janmāntare api devena dagdho yasmācchivena vai 
ārādhito mayā śaṃbhuḥ purā sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ ।। 

tasmādetanmayā labdham anyathā nopapadyate 
yaḥ smarenmanasā rudraṃ prāṇānte sakṛdeva vā ।। 

sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ kiṃ punarbahuśaḥ smaran 
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।। 

śaraṇaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti tameva śaraṇaṃ vrajet 
evaṃ saṃcintya tuṣṭātmā so andhakaś cāndhakārdanam ।। 

sagaṇaṃ śivamīśānam astuvatpuṇyagauravāt 
prārthitastena bhagavān paramārtiharo haraḥ ।। 

hiraṇyanetratanayaṃ śūlāgrasthaṃ sureśvaraḥ 
provāca dānavaṃ prekṣya ghṛṇayā nīlalohitaḥ ।। 

tuṣṭo asmi vatsa bhadraṃ te kāmaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi te 
varānvaraya daityendra varado ahaṃ tavāndhaka ।। 

śrutvā vākyaṃ tadā śaṃbhor hiraṇyanayanātmajaḥ 
harṣagadgadayā vācā provācedaṃ maheśvaram ।। 

bhagavandevadeveśa bhaktārtihara śaṅkara 
tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeśa yadi deyo varaś ca me ।। 

śrutvā bhavo api vacanam andhakasya mahātmanaḥ 
pradadau durlabhāṃ śraddhāṃ daityendrāya mahādyutiḥ ।। 

gāṇapatyaṃ ca daityāya pradadau cāvaropya tam 
praṇemustaṃ surendrādyā gāṇapatye pratiṣṭhitam ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge andhakagāṇapatyātmako nāma trinavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

kathamasya pitā daityo hiraṇyākṣaḥ sudāruṇaḥ 
viṣṇunā sūdito viṣṇur vārāhatvaṃ kathaṃ gataḥ ।। 

tasya śṛṅgaṃ maheśasya bhūṣaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ gatam 
etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। 

hiraṇyakaśiporbhrātā hiraṇyākṣa iti smṛtaḥ 
purāndhakāsureśasya pitā kālāntakopamaḥ ।। 

devāñjitvātha daityendro baddhvā ca dharaṇīmimām 
nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre vandīm indīvaraprabhām ।। 

tataḥ sabrahmakā devāḥ parimlānamukhaśriyaḥ 
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhvā hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai ।। 

balinā daityamukhyena krūreṇa sudurātmanā 
praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ daityakoṭivimardanam ।। 

sarve vijñāpayāmāsur dharaṇībandhanaṃ hareḥ 
śrutvaitadbhagavān viṣṇur dharaṇībandhanaṃ hariḥ ।। 

bhūtvā yajñavarāho asau yathā liṅgodbhave tathā 
daityaiś ca sārdhaṃ daityendraṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābalam ।। 

daṃṣṭrāgrakoṭyā hatvainaṃ reje daityāntakṛtprabhuḥ 
kalpādiṣu yathāpūrvaṃ praviśya ca rasātalam ।। 

ānīya vasudhāṃ devīm aṅkasthāmakarodbahiḥ 
tatas tuṣṭāva deveśaṃ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। 

śakrādyaiḥ sahito bhūtvā harṣagadgadayā girā 
śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ ।। 

nārāyaṇāya sarvāya brahmaṇe paramātmane 
kartre dhartre dharāyāstu hartre devāriṇāṃ svayam 
kartre netre surendrāṇāṃ śāstre ca sakalasya ca ।। 

tvamaṣṭamūrtistvamanantamūrtis tvamādidevastvamanantaveditaḥ 
tvayā kṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo ।। 

tathaikadaṃṣṭrāgramukhāgrakoṭibhāgaikabhāgārdhatamena viṣṇo 
hatāḥ kṣaṇāt kāmada daityamukhyāḥ svadaṃṣṭrakoṭyā saha putrabhṛtyaiḥ ।। 

tvayoddhṛtā deva dharā dhareśa dharādharākāra dhṛtāgradaṃṣṭre 
dharādharaiḥ sarvajanaiḥ samudraiḥ surāsuraiḥ sevitacandravaktra ।। 

tvayaiva deveśa vibho kṛtaś ca jayaḥ surāṇāmasureśvarāṇām 
aho pradattastu varaḥ prasīda vāgdevatā vārijasaṃbhavāya ।। 
tava romṇi sakalāmareśvarānayanadvaye śaśiravī padadvaye । 
nihitā rasātalagatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ ।। 

jagatāṃ hitāya bhavatā vasuṃdharā bhagavan rasātalapuṭaṃ gatā tadā 
abaloddhṛtā ca bhagavaṃstavaiva sakalaṃ tvayaiva hi dhṛtaṃ jagadguro ।। 

iti vākpatirbahuvidhaistavārcanaiḥ praṇipatya viṣṇumamaraiḥ prajāpatiḥ 
vividhānvarān harimukhāttu labdhavān harinābhivārijadehabhṛt svayam ।। 

atha tāmuddhṛtāṃ tena dharāṃ devā munīśvarāḥ 
mūrdhnyāropya namaścakruś cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā ।। 

anenaiva varāheṇa coddhṛtāsi varaprade 
kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakāryeṇa śatahastena viṣṇunā ।। 

dharaṇi tvaṃ mahābhoge bhūmistvaṃ dhenuravyaye 
lokānāṃ dhāriṇī tvaṃ hi mṛttike hara pātakam ।। 

manasā karmaṇā vācā varade vārijekṣaṇe 
tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmastvatprasādataḥ ।। 

ityuktā sā tadā devī dharā devair athābravīt 
varāhadaṃṣṭrābhinnāyāṃ dharāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

mantreṇānena yo bibhrat mūrdhni pāpātpramucyate 
āyuṣmān balavān dhanyaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ।। 

kramādbhuvi divaṃ prāpya karmānte modate suraiḥ 
atha deve gate tyaktvā varāhe kṣīrasāgaram ।। 

vārāharūpamanaghaṃ cacāla ca dharā punaḥ 
tasya daṃṣṭrābharākrāntā devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।। 

yadṛcchayā bhavaḥ paśyan jagāma jagadīśvaraḥ 
daṃṣṭrāṃ jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhūṣaṇārthamathātmanaḥ ।। 

dadhāra ca mahādevaḥ kūrcānte vai mahorasi 
devāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sendrā devadevasya vaibhavam ।। 

dharā pratiṣṭhitā hyevaṃ devadevena līlayā 
bhūtānāṃ saṃplave cāpi viṣṇoścaiva kalevaram ।। 

brahmaṇaś ca tathānyeṣāṃ devānāmapi līlayā 
vibhuraṅgavibhāgena bhūṣito na yadi prabhuḥ ।। 

kathaṃ vimuktirviprāṇāṃ tasmāddaṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge varāhaprādurbhāvo nāma caturnavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

nṛsiṃhena hataḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣāgrajaḥ śrutam 
kathaṃ niṣūditastena hiraṇyakaśipurvada ।। 

hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrāda iti viśrutaḥ 
dharmajñaḥ satyasampannas tapasvī cābhavatsudhīḥ ।। 

janmaprabhṛti deveśaṃ pūjayāmāsa cāvyayam 
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam ।। 

tamādipuruṣaṃ bhaktyā parabrahmasvarūpiṇam 
brahmaṇo adhipatiṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakāraṇam ।। 

so api viṣṇostathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ samāhitam 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti govindeti muhurmuhuḥ ।। 

stuvantaṃ prāha devāriḥ pradahanniva pāpadhīḥ 
na māṃ jānāsi durbuddhe sarvadaityāmareśvaram ।। 

prahrāda vīra duṣputra dvijadevārtikāraṇam 
ko viṣṇuḥ padmajo vāpi śakraś ca varuṇo athavā ।। 

vāyuḥ somastatheśānaḥ pāvako mama yaḥ samaḥ 
māmevārcaya bhaktyā ca svalpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ sadā ।। 

prahrāda jīvite vāñchā tavaiṣā śṛṇu cāsti cet 
śrutvāpi tasya vacanaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ ।। 

prahrādaḥ pūjayāmāsa namo nārāyaṇeti ca 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti sarvadaityakumārakān ।। 

adhyāpayāmāsa ca tāṃ brahmavidyāṃ suśobhanām 
durlaṅghyāṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā śakrādibhir api svayam ।। 

putreṇa laṅghitāmājñāṃ hiraṇyaḥ prāha dānavān 
etaṃ nānāvidhairvadhyaṃ duṣputraṃ hantumarhatha ।। 

evamuktāstadā tena daityena sudurātmanā 
nijaghnurdevadevasya bhṛtyaṃ prahrādamavyayam ।। 

tatra tatpratikṛtaṃ tadā surair daityarājatanayaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
kṣīravārinidhiśāyinaḥ prabhor niṣphalaṃ tvatha babhūva tejasā ।। 

tadātha garvabhinnasya hiraṇyakaśipoḥ prabhuḥ 
tatraivāvirabhūddhantuṃ nṛsiṃhākṛtimāsthitaḥ ।। 

jaghāna ca sutaṃ prekṣya pitaraṃ dānavādhamam 
bibheda tatkṣaṇādeva karajair niśitaiḥ śataiḥ ।। 

tato nihatya taṃ daityaṃ sabāndhavamaghāpahaḥ 
pīḍayāmāsa daityendraṃ yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ ।। 

nādaistasya nṛsiṃhasya ghorairvitrāsitaṃ jagat 
ā brahmabhuvanād viprāḥ pracacāla ca suvratāḥ ।। 

dṛṣṭvā surāsuramahoragasiddhasādhyās tasmin kṣaṇe hariviriñcimukhā nṛsiṃham 
dhairyaṃ balaṃ ca samavāpya yayurvisṛjya ā diṅmukhāntam asurakṣaṇatatparāś ca ।। 

tatastairgataiḥ saiṣa devo nṛsiṃhaḥ sahasrākṛtiḥ sarvapāt sarvabāhuḥ 
sahasrekṣaṇaḥ somasūryāgninetras tadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvamāvṛtya māyī ।। 

taṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ suraśreṣṭhā lokā lokācale sthitāḥ 
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sayamāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ ।। 

parātparataraṃ brahma tattvāt tattvatamaṃ bhavān 
jyotiṣāṃ tu paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā jaganmayaḥ ।। 

sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ susūkṣmaṃ ca śabdabrahmamayaḥ śubhaḥ 
vāgatīto nirālaṃbo nirdvandvo nirupaplavaḥ ।। 

yajñabhugyajñamūrtistvaṃ yajñināṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ 
bhavānmatsyākṛtiḥ kaurmam āsthāya jagati sthitaḥ ।। 

vārāhīṃ caiva tāṃ saiṃhīm āsthāyehavyavasthitaḥ 
devānāṃ devarakṣārthaṃ nihatya ditijeśvaram ।। 

dvijaśāpacchalenaivam avatīrṇo asi līlayā 
na dṛṣṭaṃ yattvadanyaṃ hi bhavān sarvaṃ carācaram ।। 

bhavānviṣṇurbhavān rudro bhavāneva pitāmahaḥ 
bhavānādirbhavānanto bhavāneva vayaṃ vibho ।। 

bhavāneva jagatsarvaṃ pralāpena kimīśvara 
māyayā bahudhā saṃstham advitīyamayaṃ prabho ।। 

stoṣyāmastvāṃ kathaṃ bhāsi devadeva mṛgādhipa 
stuto api vividhaiḥ stutyair bhāvairnānāvidhaiḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

na jagāma dvijāḥ śāntiṃ mānayanyonimātmanaḥ 
yo nṛsiṃhastavaṃ bhaktyā paṭhedvārthaṃ vicārayet ।। 

śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
tadantare śivaṃ devāḥ sendrāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhum ।। 

samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvaṃ vijñāpya mṛgarūpiṇaḥ 
tato brahmādayastūrṇaṃ saṃstūya parameśvaram ।। 

ātmatrāṇāya śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ paramakāraṇam 
mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ krīḍamānaṃ sahomayā ।। 

sevitaṃ gaṇagandharvaiḥ siddhairapsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ 
devatābhiḥ saha brahmā bhītabhītaḥ sagadgadam 
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। 

namaste kālakālāya namaste rudra manyave 
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te ।। 

ugro asi sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantāsi śivo asi naḥ 
namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṅkarāyārttihāriṇe ।। 

mayaskarāya viśvāya viṣṇave brahmaṇe namaḥ 
antakāya namastubhyam umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyabāhave sākṣād dhiraṇyapataye namaḥ 
śarvāya sarvarūpāya puruṣāya namonamaḥ ।। 

sadasadvyaktihīnāya mahataḥ kāraṇāya te 
nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ ।। 

jātāya bahudhā loke prabhūtāya namonamaḥ 
rudrāya nīlarudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase ।। 

kālāya kālarūpāya namaḥ kālāṅgahāriṇe 
mīḍhuṣṭamāya devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।। 

mahīyase namastubhyaṃ hantre devāriṇāṃ sadā 
tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namonamaḥ ।। 

harikeśāya devāya śaṃbhave paramātmane 
devānāṃ śaṃbhave tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhave namaḥ ।। 

śambhave haimavatyāś ca manyave rudrarūpiṇe 
kapardine namastubhyaṃ kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyāya maheśāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ 
bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya daṇḍamuṇḍīśvarāya ca ।। 

namo hrasvāya dīrghāya vāmanāya namonamaḥ 
nama ugratriśūlāya ugrāya ca namo namaḥ ।। 

bhīmāya bhīmarūpāya bhīmakarmaratāya te 
agrevadhāya vai bhūtvā namo dūrevadhāya ca ।। 

dhanvine śūline tubhyaṃ gadine haline namaḥ 
cakriṇe varmiṇe nityaṃ daityānāṃ karmabhedine ।। 

sadyāya sadyarūpāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ 
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmanetrāya te namaḥ ।। 
aghorarūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭaśarīrāya te namaḥ । 
puruṣarūpāya puruṣaikatatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ ।। 

puruṣārthapradānāya pataye parameṣṭhine 
īśānāya namastubhyam īśvarāya namonamaḥ ।। 

brahmaṇe brahmarūpāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te 
sarvaviṣṇurnṛsiṃhasya rūpamāsthāya viśvakṛt ।। 

hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatvā karajairniśitaiḥ svayam 
daityendrairbahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hitārthaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ ।। 

saiṃhīṃ samānayanyoniṃ bādhate nikhilaṃ jagat 
yatkṛtyamatra deveśa tatkuruṣva bhavāniha ।। 

ugro asi sarvaduṣṭānāṃ niyantāsi śivo asi naḥ 
kālakūṭādivapuṣā trāhi naḥ śaraṇāgatān ।। 

śukraṃ tu vṛttaṃ viśveśa krīḍā vai kevalaṃ vayam 
tavonmeṣanimeṣābhyām asmākaṃ pralayodayau ।। 

unmīlayet tvayi brahman vināśo asti na te śiva 
saṃtaptāsmo vayaṃ deva hariṇāmitatejasā ।। 

sarvalokahitāyainaṃ tattvaṃ saṃhartumicchasi 
vijñāpitas tathā devaḥ prahasanprāha tān surān ।। 

abhayaṃ ca dadau teṣāṃ haniṣyāmīti taṃ prabhuḥ 
so api śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇipatya yathāgatam ।। 

jagāma bhagavān brahmā tathānye ca surottamāḥ 
athotthāya mahādevaḥ śārabhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।। 

yayau prānte nṛsiṃhasya garvitasya mṛgāśinaḥ 
apahṛtya tadā prāṇān śarabhaḥ surapūjitaḥ ।। 

siṃhāttato naro bhūtvā jagāma ca yathākramam 
evaṃ stutastadā devair jagāma sa yathākramam ।। 

yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃstavaṃ śārvamuttamam 
rudralokamanuprāpya rudreṇa saha modate ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nārasiṃhe pañcanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

kathaṃ devo mahādevo viśvasaṃhārakārakaḥ 
śarabhākhyaṃ mahāghoraṃ vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।। 

kiṃ kiṃ dhairyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena brūhi sarvam aśeṣataḥ 
evamabhyarthito devair matiṃ cakre kṛpālayaḥ ।। 

yattejastu nṛsiṃhākhyaṃ saṃhartuṃ parameśvaraḥ 
tadarthaṃ smṛtavān rudro vīrabhadraṃ mahābalam ।। 

ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ mahāpralayakārakam 
ājagāma purā sadyo gaṇānāmagrato hasan ।। 

sāṭṭahāsair gaṇavarair utpatadbhir itastataḥ 
nṛsiṃharūpairatyugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। 

tāvadbhir abhito vīrair nṛtyadbhiś ca mudānvitaiḥ 
krīḍadbhiś ca mahādhīrair brahmādyaiḥ kandukairiva ।। 

adṛṣṭapūrvairanyaiś ca veṣṭito vīravanditaḥ 
kalpāntajvalanajvālo vilasallocanatrayaḥ ।। 

āttaśastro jaṭājūṭe jvaladbālendumaṇḍitaḥ 
bālendudvitayākāratīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṅkuradvayaḥ ।। 

ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥkhaṇḍasaṃnibhabhrūlatāyutaḥ 
mahāpracaṇḍahuṅkārabadhirīkṛtadiṅmukhaḥ ।। 

nīlameghāñjanākārabhīṣaṇaśmaśruradbhutaḥ 
vādakhaṇḍam akhaṇḍābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃstriśikhaṃ muhuḥ ।। 

vīrabhadro api bhagavān vīraśaktivijṛmbhitaḥ 
svayaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa kimatra smṛtikāraṇam ।। 

ājñāpaya jagatsvāmin prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi 
akāle bhayamutpannaṃ devānāmapi bhairava ।। 

jvalitaḥ sa nṛsiṃhāgniḥ śamayainaṃ durāsadam 
sāntvayan bodhayādau taṃ tena kiṃ nopaśāmyati ।। 

tato matparamaṃ bhāvaṃ bhairavaṃ saṃpradarśaya 
sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlaṃ sthūlena tejasā ।। 

vaktramānaya kṛttiṃ ca vīrabhadra mamājñayā 
ityādiṣṭo gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśāntavapurāsthitaḥ ।। 

jagāma raṃhasā tatra yatrāste narakesarī 
tatastaṃ bodhayāmāsa vīrabhadro haro harim ।। 

uvāca vākyamīśānaḥ pitā putramivaurasam 
jagatsukhāya bhagavann avatīrṇo asi mādhava ।। 

sthityarthena ca yukto asi pareṇa parameṣṭhinā 
jantucakraṃ bhagavatā rakṣitaṃ matsyarūpiṇā ।। 

pucchenaiva samābadhya bhramannekārṇave purā 
bibharṣi kūrmarūpeṇa vārāheṇoddhṛtā mahī ।। 

anena harirūpeṇa hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ 
vāmanena balirbaddhas tvayā vikramatā punaḥ ।। 

tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhāvaḥ prabhur avyayaḥ 
yadā yadā hi lokasya duḥkhaṃ kiṃcit prajāyate ।। 

tadā tadāvatīrṇastvaṃ kariṣyasi nirāmayam 
nādhikastvatsamo apyasti hare śivaparāyaṇa ।। 

tvayā dharmāś ca vedāś ca śubhe mārge pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
yadartham avatāro ayaṃ nihataḥ so api keśava ।। 

atyantaghoraṃ bhagavan narasiṃha vapustava 
upasaṃhara viśvātmaṃs tvameva mama saṃnidhau ।। 

ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ śāntayā girā 
tato adhikaṃ mahāghoraṃ kopaṃ prajvālayaddhariḥ ।। 

āgato asi yatastatra gaccha tvaṃ mā hitaṃ vada 
idānīṃ saṃhariṣyāmi jagadetaccarācaram ।। 

saṃhartur na hi saṃhāraḥ svato vā parato api vā 
śāsitaṃ mama sarvatra śāstā ko api na vidyate ।। 

matprasādena sakalaṃ samaryādaṃ pravartate 
ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ ।। 

yad yad vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmadūrjitameva vā 
tattadviddhi gaṇādhyakṣa mama tejovijṛmbhitam ।। 

devatāparamārthajñā mamaiva paramaṃ viduḥ 
madaṃśāḥ śaktisampannā brahmaśakrādayaḥ surāḥ ।। 

mannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ purā brahmā caturmukhaḥ 
tallalāṭasamutpanno bhagavānvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। 

rajasādhiṣṭhitaḥ sraṣṭā rudrastāmasa ucyate 
ahaṃ niyantā sarvasya matparaṃ nāsti daivatam ।। 

viśvādhikaḥ svatantraś ca kartā hartākhileśvaraḥ 
idaṃ tu matparaṃ tejaḥ kaḥ punaḥ śrotumicchati ।। 

ato māṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpya gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ 
avehi paramaṃ bhāvam idaṃ bhūtamaheśvaraḥ ।। 

kālo asmyahaṃ kālavināśahetur lokān samāhartum ahaṃ pravṛttaḥ 
mṛtyormṛtyuṃ viddhi māṃ vīrabhadra jīvantyete matprasādena devāḥ ।। 

sāhaṅkāramidaṃ śrutvā harer amitavikramaḥ 
vihasyovāca sāvajñaṃ tato visphuritādharaḥ ।। 

kiṃ na jānāsi viśveśaṃ saṃhartāraṃ pinākinam 
asadvādo vivādaś ca vināśastvayi kevalaḥ ।। 

tavānyonyāvatārāṇi kāni śeṣāṇi sāṃpratam 
kṛtāni yena kenāpi kathāśeṣo bhaviṣyati ।। 

doṣaṃ tvaṃ paśya etattvam avasthāmīdṛśīṃ gataḥ 
tena saṃhāradakṣeṇa kṣaṇātsaṃkṣayameṣyasi ।। 

prakṛtistvaṃ pumān rudras tvayi vīryaṃ samāhitam 
tvannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। 

sṛṣṭyarthena jagatpūrvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam 
lalāṭe cintayāmāsa tapasyugre vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

tallalāṭādabhūcchaṃbhoḥ sṛṣṭyarthaṃ tanna dūṣaṇam 
aṃśo ahaṃ devadevasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ ।। 

tvatsaṃhāre niyukto asmi vinayena balena ca 
evaṃ rakṣo vidāryaiva tvaṃ śaktikalayā yutaḥ ।। 

ahaṅkārāvalepena garjasi tvamatandritaḥ 
upakāro hyasādhūnām apakārāya kevalam ।। 

yadi siṃha maheśānaṃ svapunarbhūta manyase 
na tvaṃ sraṣṭā na saṃhartā na svatantro hi kutracit ।। 

kulālacakravacchaktyā prerito asi pinākinā 
adyāpi tava nikṣiptaṃ kapālaṃ kūrmarūpiṇaḥ ।। 

harahāralatāmadhye mugdha kasmānna budhyase 
vismṛtaṃ kiṃ tadaṃśena daṃṣṭrotpātanapīḍitaḥ ।। 

vārāhavigrahaste adya sākrośaṃ tārakāriṇā 
dagdho asi yasya śūlāgre viṣvaksenacchalādbhavān ।। 

dakṣayajñe śiraśchinnaṃ mayā te yajñarūpiṇaḥ 
adyāpi tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ ।। 

chinnaṃ tamenābhisaṃdhaṃ tadaṃśaṃ tasya tadbalam 
nirjitastvaṃ dadhīcena saṃgrāme samarudgaṇaḥ ।। 

kaṇḍūyamāne śirasi kathaṃ tadvismṛtaṃ tvayā 
cakraṃ vikramato yasya cakrapāṇe tava priyam ।। 

kutaḥ prāptaṃ kṛtaṃ kena tvayā tadapi vismṛtam 
te mayā sakalā lokā gṛhītāstvaṃ payonidhau ।। 

nidrāparavaśaḥ śeṣe sa kathaṃ sāttviko bhavān 
tvadādistambaparyantaṃ rudraśaktivijṛmbhitam ।। 

śaktimānabhitastvaṃ ca hy analastvaṃ ca mohitaḥ 
tattejaso api māhātmyaṃ yuvāṃ draṣṭuṃ na hi kṣamau ।। 

sthūlā ye hi prapaśyanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam 
dyāvāpṛthivyā indrāgniyamasya varuṇasya ca ।। 

dhvāntodare śaśāṅkasya janitvā parameśvaraḥ 
kālo asi tvaṃ mahākālaḥ kālakālo maheśvaraḥ ।। 

atastvamugrakalayā mṛtyormṛtyurbhaviṣyasi 
sthiradhanvā kṣayo vīro vīro viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

upahastā jvaraṃ bhīmo mṛgapakṣihiraṇmayaḥ 
śāstāśeṣasya jagato na tvaṃ naivacaturmukhaḥ ।। 

itthaṃ sarvaṃ samālokya saṃharātmānam ātmanā 
no cedidānīṃ krodhasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ ।। 

vajrāśaniriva sthāṇos tv evaṃ mṛtyuḥ patiṣyati 
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ krodhavihvalaḥ ।। 

nanāda tanuvegena taṃ gṛhītuṃ pracakrame 
atrāntare mahāghoraṃ vipakṣabhayakāraṇam ।। 

gaganavyāpi durdharṣaśaivatejaḥsamudbhavam 
vīrabhadrasya tadrūpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva dṛśyate ।। 

na taddhiraṇmayaṃ saumyaṃ na sauraṃ nāgnisaṃbhavam 
na taḍiccandrasadṛśam anaupamyaṃ maheśvaram ।। 

tadā tejāṃsi sarvāṇi tasmin līnāni śāṅkare 
tato vyakto mahātejā vyakte saṃbhavatastataḥ ।। 

rudrasādhāraṇaṃ caiva cihnitaṃ vikṛtākṛti 
tataḥ saṃhārarūpeṇa suvyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। 

paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ 
sahasrabāhur jaṭilaś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ ।। 

sa mṛgārdhaśarīreṇa pakṣābhyāṃ cañcunā dvijāḥ 
atitīkṣṇamahādaṃṣṭro vajratulyanakhāyudhaḥ ।। 

kaṇṭhe kālo mahābāhuś catuṣpād vahnisaṃbhavaḥ 
yugāntodyatajīmūtabhīmagaṃbhīraniḥsvanaḥ ।। 

samaṃ kupitavṛttāgnivyāvṛttanayanatrayaḥ 
spaṣṭadaṃṣṭro adharoṣṭhaś ca huṅkāreṇa yuto haraḥ ।। 

haristaddarśanādeva vinaṣṭabalavikramaḥ 
bibhrad aurmyaṃ sahasrāṃśor adhaḥ khadyotavibhramam ।। 

atha vibhramya pakṣābhyāṃ nābhipāde abhyudārayan 
pādāvābadhya pucchena bāhubhyāṃ bāhumaṇḍalam ।। 

bhindannurasi bāhubhyāṃ nijagrāha haro harim 
tato jagāma gaganaṃ devaiḥ saha maharṣibhiḥ ।। 

sahasaiva bhayādviṣṇuṃ vihagaś ca yathoragam 
utkṣipyotkṣipya saṃgṛhya nipātya ca nipātya ca ।। 

uḍḍīyoḍḍīya bhagavān pakṣāghātavimohitam 
hariṃ harantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ viśveśānaṃ tamīśvaram ।। 

anuyānti surāḥ sarve namovākyena tuṣṭuvuḥ 
nīyamānaḥ paravaśo dīnavaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। 

tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ haristaṃ lalitākṣaraiḥ 
namo rudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave ।। 

nama ugrāya bhīmāya namaḥ krodhāya manyave 
namo bhavāya śarvāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te ।। 

kālakālāya kālāya mahākālāya mṛtyave 
vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline ।। 

mahādevāya mahate paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ 
ekāya nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine ।। 

namo anantāya sūkṣmāya namaste mṛtyumanyave 
parāya parameśāya parātparatarāya te ।। 

parātparāya viśvāya namaste viśvamūrttaye 
namo viṣṇukalatrāya viṣṇukṣetrāya bhānave ।। 

kaivartāya kirātāya mahāvyādhāya śāśvate 
bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābhairavarūpiṇe ।। 

namo nṛsiṃhasaṃhartre kāmakālapurāraye 
mahāpāśaughasaṃhartre viṣṇumāyāntakāriṇe ।। 

tryaṃbakāya tryakṣarāya śipiviṣṭāya mīḍhuṣe 
mṛtyuñjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makhāraye ।। 

makheśāya vareṇyāya namaste vahnirūpiṇe 
mahāghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇāpānapravartine ।। 

triguṇāya triśūlāya guṇātītāya yogine 
saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahāyantrapravartine ।। 

namaścandrāgnisūryāya muktivaicitryahetave 
varadāyāvatārāya sarvakāraṇahetave ।। 

kapāline karālāya pataye puṇyakīrttaye 
amoghāyāgninetrāya lakulīśāya śaṃbhave ।। 

bhiṣaktamāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine yogarūpiṇe 
meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ ।। 

avyaktāya viśokāya sthirāya sthiradhanvine 
sthāṇave kṛttivāsāya namaḥ pañcārthahetave ।। 

varadāyaikapādāya namaścandrārdhamauline 
namaste adhvararājāya vayasāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। 

yogīśvarāya nityāya satyāya parameṣṭhine 
sarvātmane namastubhyaṃ namaḥ sarveśvarāya te ।। 

ekadvitricatuḥpañcakṛtvas te astu namonamaḥ 
daśakṛtvastu sāhasrakṛtvaste ca namonamaḥ ।। 

namo aparimitaṃ kṛtvā-nantakṛtvo namonamaḥ 
namonamo namo bhūyaḥ punarbhūyo namonamaḥ ।। 

nāmnāmaṣṭaśatenaivaṃ stutvāmṛtamayena tu 
punastu prārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabheśvaram ।। 

yadā yadā mamājñānam atyahaṅkāradūṣitam 
tadā tadāpanetavyaṃ tvayaiva parameśvara ।। 

evaṃ vijñāpayanprītaḥ śaṅkaraṃ narakesarī 
nanvaśakto bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntaṃ parājitaḥ ।। 

tadvaktraśeṣamātrāntaṃ kṛtvā sarvasya vigraham 
śuktiśityaṃ tadā maṅgaṃ vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāttataḥ ।। 

atha brahmādayaḥ sarve vīrabhadra tvayā dṛśā 
jīvitāḥ smo vayaṃ devāḥ parjanyeneva pādapāḥ ।। 

yasya bhīṣā dahatyagnir udeti ca raviḥ svayam 
vāto vāti ca so asi tvaṃ mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ ।। 

yadavyaktaṃ paraṃ vyoma kalātītaṃ sadāśivam 
bhagavaṃstvāmeva bhavaṃ vadanti brahmavādinaḥ ।। 

ke vayameva dhātukye vedane parameśvaraḥ 
na viddhi paramaṃ dhāma rūpalāvaṇyavarṇane ।। 

upasargeṣu sarveṣu trāyasvāsmān gaṇādhipa 
ekādaśātman bhagavān vartate rūpavān haraḥ ।। 

īdṛśān te avatārāṇi dṛṣṭvā śiva bahūṃstamaḥ 
kadācit saṃdihen nāsmāṃs tvaccintāstamayā tathā ।। 

guñjāgirivarataṭā-mitarūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ 
abhyasaṃhara gamyaṃ te na nītavyaṃ parāparā ।। 

dve tanū tava rudrasya vedajñā brāhmaṇā viduḥ 
ghorāpyanyā śivāpyanyā te pratyekamanekadhā ।। 

ihāsmānpāhi bhagavan nityāhatamahābalaḥ 
bhavatā hi jagatsarvaṃ vyāptaṃ svenaiva tejasā ।। 

brahmaviṣṇvindracandrādi vayaṃ ca pramukhāḥ surāḥ 
surāsurāḥ samprasūtās tvattaḥ sarve maheśvara ।। 

brahmā ca indro viṣṇuś ca yamādyā na surāsurān 
tato nigṛhya ca hariṃ siṃha ity upacetasam ।। 

yato bibharṣi sakalaṃ vibhajya tanumaṣṭadhā 
ato asmān pāhi bhagavan surān dānair abhīpsitaiḥ ।। 

uvāca tān surāndevo maharṣīṃś ca purātanān 
yathā jale jalaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣīraṃ kṣīre ghṛtaṃ ghṛte ।। 

eka eva tadā viṣṇuḥ śivalīno na cānyathā 
eṣa eva nṛsiṃhātmā sadarpaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। 

jagatsaṃhārakāreṇa pravṛtto narakesarī 
yājanīyo namastasmai madbhaktisiddhikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। 

etāvaduktvā bhagavān vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ 
apaśyan sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 

nṛsiṃhakṛttivasanas tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaraḥ 
vaktraṃ tanmuṇḍamālāyāṃ nāyakatvena kalpitam ।। 

tato devā nirātaṅkāḥ kīrtayantaḥ kathāmimām 
vismayotphullanayanā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam ।। 

ya idaṃ paramākhyānaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiḥ samanvitam 
paṭhitvā śṛṇute caiva sarvaduḥkhavināśanam ।। 

dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṣṭivardhanam 
sarvavighnapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam ।। 

apamṛtyupraśamanaṃ mahāśāntikaraṃ śubham 
aricakrapraśamanaṃ sarvādhipravināśanam ।। 

tato duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ sarvabhūtanivāraṇam 
viṣagrahakṣayakaraṃ putrapautrādivardhanam ।। 

yogasiddhipradaṃ samyak śivajñānaprakāśakam 
śeṣalokasya sopānaṃ vāñchitārthaikasādhanam ।। 

viṣṇumāyānirasanaṃ devatāparamārthadam 
vāñchāsiddhipradaṃ caiva ṛddhiprajñādisādhanam ।। 

idaṃ tu śarabhākāraṃ paraṃ rūpaṃ pinākinaḥ 
prakāśitavyaṃ bhakteṣu cireṣūdyamiteṣu ca ।। 

taireva paṭhitavyaṃ ca śrotavyaṃ ca śivātmabhiḥ 
śivotsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca ।। 

paṭhetpratiṣṭhākāleṣu śivasannidhikāraṇam 
coravyāghrāhisiṃhāntakṛto rājabhayeṣu ca ।। 

atrānyotpātabhūkampadavāgnipāṃsuvṛṣṭiṣu 
ulkāpāte mahāvāte vinā vṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭiṣu ।। 

atastatra paṭhedvidvāñ chivabhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi stavaṃ sarvamanuttamam ।। 

sa rudratvaṃ samāsādya rudrasyānucaro bhavet ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śarabhaprādurbhāvo nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

jalandharaṃ jaṭāmauliḥ purā jambhārivikramam 
kathaṃ jaghāna bhagavān bhaganetraharo haraḥ ।। 

vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata 
jalandhara iti khyāto jalamaṇḍalasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

āsīdantakasaṃkāśas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ 
tena devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ ।। 

nirjitāḥ samare sarve brahmā ca bhagavānajaḥ 
jitvaiva devasaṃghātaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vai jalandharaḥ ।। 

jagāma devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvaharaṃ gurum 
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ divārātram aviśramam ।। 

jalandhareśayostena nirjito madhusūdanaḥ 
jalandharo api taṃ jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam ।। 

provācedaṃ diteḥ putrān nyāyadhīrjetumīśvaram 
sarve jitā mayā yuddhe śaṅkaro hyajito raṇe ।। 

taṃ jitvā sarvamīśānaṃ gaṇapair nandinā kṣaṇāt 
ahameva bhavatvaṃ ca brahmatvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।। 

vāsavatvaṃ ca yuṣmākaṃ dāsye dānavapuṅgavāḥ 
jalandharavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavādhamāḥ ।। 

jagarjuruccaiḥ pāpiṣṭhā mṛtyudarśanatatparāḥ 
daityairetaistathānyaiś ca rathanāgaturaṅgamaiḥ ।। 

saṃnaddhaiḥ saha saṃnahya śarvaṃ prati yayau balī 
bhavo api dṛṣṭvā daityendraṃ merukūṭamiva sthitam ।। 

avadhyatvam api śrutvā tathānyair bhaganetrahā 
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ rakṣan rakṣako jagatāṃ prabhuḥ ।। 

sāṃbaḥ sanandī sagaṇaḥ provāca prahasanniva 
kiṃ kṛtyamasureśāna yuddhenānena sāṃpratam ।। 

madbāṇairbhinnasarvāṅgo martumabhyudyate mudā 
jalandharo api tadvākyaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam ।। 

sureśvaramuvācedaṃ suretarabaleśvaraḥ 
vākyenālaṃ mahābāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja ।। 

candrāṃśusannibhaiḥ śastrair hara yoddhumihāgataḥ 
niśamyāsya vacaḥ śūlī pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā 
mahāṃbhasi cakārāśu rathāṅgaṃ raudramāyudham ।। 

kṛtvārṇavāṃbhasi sitaṃ bhagavān rathāṅgaṃ smṛtvā jagattrayamanena hatāḥ surāś ca 
dakṣāndhakāntakapuratrayayajñahartā lokatrayāntakakaraḥ prahasaṃtadāha ।। 

pādena nirmitaṃ daitya jalandhara mahārṇave 
balavān yadi coddhartuṃ tiṣṭha yoddhuṃ na cānyathā ।। 

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā krodhenādīptalocanaḥ 
pradahanniva netrābhyāṃ prāhālokya jagattrayam ।। 

gadāmuddhṛtya hatvā ca nandinaṃ tvāṃ ca śaṅkara 
hatvā lokānsuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍo yathā ।। 

hantuṃ carācaraṃ sarvaṃ samartho ahaṃ savāsavam 
ko maheśvara madbāṇair acchedyo bhuvanatraye ।। 

bālabhāve ca bhagavān tapasaiva vinirjitaḥ 
brahmā balī yauvane vai munayaḥ surapuṅgavaiḥ ।। 

dagdhaṃ kṣaṇena sakalaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
tapasā kiṃ tvayā rudra nirjito bhagavānapi ।। 

indrāgniyamavitteśavāyuvārīśvarādayaḥ 
na sehire yathā nāgā gandhaṃ pakṣipateriva ।। 

na labdhvā divi bhūmau ca bāhavo mama śaṅkara 
samastānparvatānprāpya gharṣitāś ca gaṇeśvara ।। 

girīndro mandaraḥ śrīmān nīlo meruḥ suśobhanaḥ 
gharṣito bāhudaṇḍena kaṇḍūnodārtham āpatat ।। 

gaṅgā niruddhā bāhubhyāṃ līlārthaṃ himavadgirau 
nārīṇāṃ mama bhṛtyaiś ca vajro baddho divaukasām ।। 

vaḍavāyā mukhaṃ bhagnaṃ gṛhītvā vai kareṇa tu 
tatkṣaṇādeva sakalaṃ caikārṇavamabhūdidam ।। 

airāvatādayo nāgāḥ kṣiptāḥ sindhujalopari 
saratho bhagavānindraḥ kṣiptaś ca śatayojanam ।। 

garuḍo api mayā baddho nāgapāśena viṣṇunā 
urvaśyādyā mayā nītā nāryaḥ kārāgṛhāntaram ।। 

kathaṃcillabdhavān śakraḥ śacīmekāṃ praṇamya mām 
māṃ na jānāsi daityendraṃ jalandharamumāpate ।। 

evamukto mahādevaḥ prādahadvai rathaṃ tadā 
tasya netrāgnibhāgaikakalārdhārdhena cākulam ।। 

daityānāmatulabalairhayaiś ca nāgair daityendrās tripuraripor nirīkṣaṇena 
nāgād vaiśasam anusaṃvṛtaś ca nāgair deveśaṃ vacanamuvāca cālpabuddhiḥ ।। 

kiṃ kāryaṃ mama yudhi devadaityasaṃghair hantuṃ yatsakalamidaṃ kṣaṇātsamarthaḥ 
yattasmādbhayamihanāsti yoddhum īśa vāñchaiṣā vipulatarā na saṃśayo atra ।। 

tasmāttvaṃ mama madanāridakṣaśatro yajñāre tripuraripo mamaiva vīraiḥ 
bhūtendrairharivadanena devasaṃghair yoddhuṃ te balamiha cāsti ceddhi tiṣṭha ।। 

ityuktvātha mahādevaṃ mahādevārinandanaḥ 
na cacāla na sasmāra nihatānbāndhavānyudhi ।। 

durmadenāvinītātmā dorbhyāmāsphoṭya dorbalāt 
sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ tena hantuṃ samudyataḥ ।। 

durdhareṇa rathāṅgena kṛcchreṇāpi dvijottamāḥ 
sthāpayāmāsa vai skandhe dvidhābhūtaś ca tena vai ।। 

kuliśena yathā chinno dvidhā girivaro dvijāḥ 
papāta daityo balavān añjanādririvāparaḥ ।। 

tasya raktena raudreṇa sampūrṇam abhavatkṣaṇāt 
tadraktamakhilaṃ rudraniyogānmāṃsameva ca ।। 

mahārauravamāsādya raktakuṇḍamabhūdaho 
jalandharaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvapārṣadāḥ ।। 

siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā sādhu deveti cābruvan 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi jalandharavimardanam ।। 

śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge jalandharavadho nāma saptanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

kathaṃ devena vai sūta devadevānmaheśvarāt 
sudarśanākhyaṃ vai labdhaṃ vaktumarhasi viṣṇunā ।। 

devānām asurendrāṇām abhavacca sudāruṇaḥ 
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vināśakaraṇo mahān ।। 

te devāḥ śaktimuśalaiḥ sāyakairnataparvabhiḥ 
prabhidyamānāḥ kuntaiś ca dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ ।। 

parājitāstadā devā devadeveśvaraṃ harim 
praṇemustaṃ sureśānaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasāḥ ।। 

tān samīkṣyātha bhagavān devadeveśvaro hariḥ 
praṇipatya sthitāndevān idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। 

vatsāḥ kimiti vai devāś cyutālaṅkāravikramāḥ 
samāgatāḥ sasaṃtāpā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ ।। 

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tathābhūtāḥ surottamāḥ 
praṇamyāhuryathāvṛttaṃ devadevāya viṣṇave ।। 

bhagavandevadeveśa viṣṇo jiṣṇo janārdana 
dānavaiḥ pīḍitāḥ sarve vayaṃ śaraṇamāgatāḥ ।। 

tvameva devadeveśa gatirnaḥ puruṣottama 
tvameva paramātmā hi tvaṃ pitā jagatāmapi ।। 

tvameva bhartā hartā ca bhoktā dātā janārdana 
hantumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ dānavāndānavārdana ।। 

daityāś ca vaiṣṇavairbrāhmai raudrairyāmyaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ 
kauberaiścaiva saumyaiś ca nairṛtyairvāruṇairdṛḍhaiḥ ।। 

vāyavyaiś ca tathāgneyair aiśānair vārṣikaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
saurai raudrais tathā bhīmaiḥ kampanair jṛmbhaṇair dṛḍhaiḥ ।। 

avadhyā varalābhātte sarve vārijalocana 
sūryamaṇḍalasambhūtaṃ tvadīyaṃ cakram udyatam ।। 

kuṇṭhitaṃ hi dadhīcena cyāvanena jagadguro 
daṇḍaṃ śārṅgaṃ tavāstraṃ ca labdhaṃ daityaiḥ prasādataḥ ।। 

purā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ tripurāriṇā 
rathāṅgaṃ suśitaṃ ghoraṃ tena tān hantum arhasi ।। 

tasmāttena nihantavyā nānyaiḥ śastraśatairapi 
tato niśamya teṣāṃ vai vacanaṃ vārijekṣaṇaḥ ।। 

vācaspatimukhānāha sa hariścakrabhṛt svayam 
bhobho devā mahādevaṃ sarvair devaiḥ sanātanaiḥ ।। 

samprāpya sāṃprataṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi divaukasām 
devā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ hi purāriṇā ।। 

labdhvā rathāṅgaṃ tenaiva nihatya ca mahāsurān 
sarvāndhundhumukhāndaityān aṣṭaṣaṣṭiśatān surān ।। 

sabāndhavānkṣaṇādeva yuṣmān saṃtārayāmyaham 
evam uktvā suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhamanusmaran ।। 

suraśreṣṭhastadā śreṣṭhaṃ pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram 
liṅgaṃ sthāpya yathānyāyaṃ himavacchikhare śubhe ।। 

meruparvatasaṃkāśaṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā 
tvaritākhyena rudreṇa raudreṇa ca janārdanaḥ ।। 

snāpya sampūjya gandhādyair jvālākāraṃ manoramam 
tuṣṭāva ca tadā rudraṃ sampūjyāgnau praṇamya ca ।। 

devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena yathākramam 
pūjayāmāsa ca śivaṃ praṇavādyaṃ namo antakam ।। 

devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena maheśvaram 
pratināma sa padmena pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram ।। 

agnau ca nāmabhir devaṃ bhavādyaiḥ samidādibhiḥ 
svāhāntairvidhivaddhutvā pratyekamayutaṃ prabhum ।। 

tuṣṭāva ca punaḥ śaṃbhuṃ bhavādyairbhavamīśvaram 
bhavaḥ śivo haro rudraḥ puruṣaḥ padmalocanaḥ ।। 

arthitavyaḥ sadācāraḥ sarvaśaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ 
īśvaraḥ sthāṇurīśānaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।। 

varīyān varado vandyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ 
gaṅgādharaḥ śūladharaḥ parārthaikaprayojanaḥ ।। 

sarvajñaḥ sarvadevādigiridhanvā jaṭādharaḥ 
candrāpīḍaścandramaulir vidvānviśvāmareśvaraḥ ।। 

vedāntasārasaṃdohaḥ kapālī nīlalohitaḥ 
dhyānādhāroparicchedyo gaurībhartā gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। 

aṣṭamūrtirviśvamūrtis trivargaḥ svargasādhanaḥ 
jñānagamyo dṛḍhaprajño devadevastrilocanaḥ ।। 

vāmadevo mahādevaḥ pāṇḍuḥ paridṛḍho dṛḍhaḥ 
viśvarūpo virūpākṣo vāgīśaḥ śucirantaraḥ ।। 

sarvapraṇayasaṃvādī vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavāhanaḥ 
īśaḥ pinākī khaṭvāṅgī citraveṣaścirantanaḥ ।। 

tamoharo mahāyogī goptā brahmāṅgahṛjjaṭī 
kālakālaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ subhagaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ ।। 

unmattaveṣaś cakṣuṣyo durvāsāḥ smaraśāsanaḥ 
dṛḍhāyudhaḥ skandaguruḥ parameṣṭhī parāyaṇaḥ ।। 

anādimadhyanidhano giriśo giribāndhavaḥ 
kuberabandhuḥ śrīkaṇṭho lokavarṇottamottamaḥ ।। 

sāmānyadevaḥ kodaṇḍī nīlakaṇṭhaḥ paraśvadhī 
viśālākṣo mṛgavyādhaḥ sureśaḥ sūryatāpanaḥ ।। 

dharmakarmākṣamaḥ kṣetraṃ bhagavān bhaganetrabhit 
ugraḥ paśupatis tārkṣyaḥ priyabhaktaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ ।। 

dātā dayākaro dakṣaḥ kapardī kāmaśāsanaḥ 
śmaśānanilayaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śmaśānastho maheśvaraḥ ।। 

lokakartā bhūtapatir mahākartā mahauṣadhī 
uttaro gopatirgoptā jñānagamyaḥ purātanaḥ ।। 

nītiḥ sunītiḥ śuddhātmā somaḥ somarataḥ sukhī 
somapo amṛtapaḥ somo mahānītirmahāmatiḥ ।। 

ajātaśatrurālokaḥ saṃbhāvyo havyavāhanaḥ 
lokakāro vedakāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ sanātanaḥ ।। 

maharṣiḥ kapilācāryo viśvadīptistrilocanaḥ 
pinākapāṇir bhūdevaḥ svastidaḥ svastikṛtsadā ।। 

tridhāmā saubhagaḥ śarvaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvagocaraḥ 
brahmadhṛg viśvasṛk svargaḥ karṇikāraḥ priyaḥ kaviḥ ।। 

śākho viśākho gośākhaḥ śivo naikaḥ kratuḥ samaḥ 
gaṅgāplavodako bhāvaḥ sakalaḥ sthapatiḥ sthiraḥ ।। 

vijitātmā vidheyātmā bhūtavāhanasārathiḥ 
sagaṇo gaṇakāryaś ca sukīrtiś chinnasaṃśayaḥ ।। 

kāmadevaḥ kāmapālo bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ 
bhasmapriyo bhasmaśāyī kāmī kāntaḥ kṛtāgamaḥ ।। 

samāyukto nivṛttātmā dharmayuktaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
caturmukhaścaturbāhur durāvāso durāsadaḥ ।। 

durgamo durlabho durgaḥ sarvāyudhaviśāradaḥ 
adhyātmayoganilayaḥ sutantustantuvardhanaḥ ।। 

śubhāṅgo lokasāraṅgo jagadīśo amṛtāśanaḥ 
bhasmaśuddhikaro merur ojasvī śuddhavigrahaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyaretās taraṇir marīcir mahimālayaḥ 
mahāhrado mahāgarbhaḥ siddhavṛndāravanditaḥ ।। 

vyāghracarmadharo vyālī mahābhūto mahānidhiḥ 
amṛtāṅgo amṛtavapuḥ pañcayajñaḥ prabhañjanaḥ ।। 

pañcaviṃśatitattvajñaḥ pārijātaḥ parāvaraḥ 
sulabhaḥ suvrataḥ śūro vāṅmayaikanidhirnidhiḥ ।। 

varṇāśramagururvarṇī śatrujicchatrutāpanaḥ 
āśramaḥ kṣapaṇaḥ kṣāmo jñānavānacalācalaḥ ।। 

pramāṇabhūto durjñeyaḥ suparṇo vāyuvāhanaḥ 
dhanurdharo dhanurvedo guṇarāśirguṇākaraḥ ।। 

anantadṛṣṭirānando daṇḍo damayitā damaḥ 
abhivādyo mahācāryo viśvakarmā viśāradaḥ ।। 

vītarāgo vinītātmā tapasvī bhūtabhāvanaḥ 
unmattaveṣaḥ pracchanno jitakāmo jitapriyaḥ ।। 

kalyāṇaprakṛtiḥ kalpaḥ sarvalokaprajāpatiḥ 
tapasvī tārako dhīmān pradhānaprabhur avyayaḥ ।। 

lokapālo antarhitātmā kalpādiḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ 
vedaśāstrārthatattvajño niyamo niyamāśrayaḥ ।। 

candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ ketur virāmo vidrumacchaviḥ 
bhaktigamyaḥ paraṃ brahma mṛgabāṇārpaṇo anaghaḥ ।। 

adrirājālayaḥ kāntaḥ paramātmā jagadguruḥ 
sarvakarmācalastvaṣṭā maṅgalyo maṅgalāvṛtaḥ ।। 

mahātapā dīrghatapāḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ sthaviro dhruvaḥ 
ahaḥ saṃvatsaro vyāptiḥ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। 

saṃvatsarakaro mantraḥ pratyayaḥ sarvadarśanaḥ 
ajaḥ sarveśvaraḥ snigdho mahāretā mahābalaḥ ।। 

yogī yogyo mahāretāḥ siddhaḥ sarvādir agnidaḥ 
vasurvasumanāḥ satyaḥ sarvapāpaharo haraḥ ।। 

amṛtaḥ śāśvataḥ śānto bāṇahastaḥ pratāpavān 
kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī vedāṅgo vedavinmuniḥ ।। 

bhrājiṣṇur bhojanaṃ bhoktā lokanetā durādharaḥ 
atīndriyo mahāmāyaḥ sarvāvāsaścatuṣpathaḥ ।। 

kālayogī mahānādo mahotsāho mahābalaḥ 
mahābuddhir mahāvīryo bhūtacārī purandaraḥ ।। 

niśācaraḥ pretacārī mahāśaktir mahādyutiḥ 
anirdeśyavapuḥ śrīmān sarvahāryamito gatiḥ ।। 

bahuśruto bahumayo niyatātmā bhavodbhavaḥ 
ojastejo dyutikaro nartakaḥ sarvakāmakaḥ ।। 

nṛtyapriyo nṛtyanṛtyaḥ prakāśātmā pratāpanaḥ 
buddhaspaṣṭākṣaro mantraḥ sanmānaḥ sārasaṃplavaḥ ।। 

yugādikṛd yugāvarto gaṃbhīro vṛṣavāhanaḥ 
iṣṭo viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭeṣṭaḥ śarabhaḥ śarabho dhanuḥ ।। 

apāṃ nidhiradhiṣṭhānaṃ vijayo jayakālavit 
pratiṣṭhitaḥ pramāṇajño hiraṇyakavaco hariḥ ।। 

virocanaḥ suragaṇo vidyeśo vibudhāśrayaḥ 
bālarūpo balonmāthī vivarto gahano guruḥ ।। 

karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ kartā sarvabandhavimocanaḥ 
vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvabhartā niśākaraḥ ।। 

vyavasāyo vyavasthānaḥ sthānado jagadādijaḥ 
dundubho lalito viśvo bhavātmātmani saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

vīreśvaro vīrabhadro vīrahā vīrabhṛd virāṭ 
vīracūḍāmaṇirvettā tīvranādo nadīdharaḥ ।। 

ājñādharastriśūlī ca śipiviṣṭaḥ śivālayaḥ 
vālakhilyo mahācāpas tigmāṃśur nidhir avyayaḥ ।। 

abhirāmaḥ suśaraṇaḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ sudhāpatiḥ 
maghavānkauśiko gomān viśrāmaḥ sarvaśāsanaḥ ।। 

lalāṭākṣo viśvadehaḥ sāraḥ saṃsāracakrabhṛt 
amoghadaṇḍī madhyastho hiraṇyo brahmavarcasī ।। 

paramārthaḥ paramayaḥ śambaro vyāghrako analaḥ 
rucir vararucir vandyo vācaspatiraharpatiḥ ।। 

ravirvirocanaḥ skandhaḥ śāstā vaivasvato janaḥ 
yuktirunnatakīrtiś ca śāntarāgaḥ parājayaḥ ।। 

kailāsapatikāmāriḥ savitā ravilocanaḥ 
vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvahartā nivāritaḥ ।। 

nityo niyatakalyāṇaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ 
dūraśravā viśvasaho dhyeyo duḥsvapnanāśanaḥ ।। 

uttārako duṣkṛtihā durdharṣo duḥsaho abhayaḥ 
anādirbhūrbhuvolakṣmīḥ kirīṭī tridaśādhipaḥ ।। 

viśvagoptā viśvabhartā sudhīro rucirāṅgadaḥ 
janano janajanmādiḥ prītimānnītimānnayaḥ ।। 

viśiṣṭaḥ kāśyapo bhānur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ 
praṇavaḥ saptadhācāro mahākāyo mahādhanuḥ ।। 

janmādhipo mahādevaḥ sakalāgamapāragaḥ 
tattvātattvavivekātmā vibhūṣṇur bhūtibhūṣaṇaḥ ।। 

ṛṣirbrāhmaṇavijjiṣṇur janmamṛtyujarātigaḥ 
yajño yajñapatiryajvā yajñānto amoghavikramaḥ ।। 

mahendro durbharaḥ senī yajñāṅgo yajñavāhanaḥ 
pañcabrahmasamutpattir viśveśo vimalodayaḥ ।। 

ātmayonir anādyantaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatsaptalokadhṛk 
gāyatrīvallabhaḥ prāṃśur viśvāvāsaḥ prabhākaraḥ ।। 

śiśurgirirataḥ samrāṭ suṣeṇaḥ suraśatruhā 
amogho ariṣṭamathano mukundo vigatajvaraḥ ।। 

svayaṃjyotir anujyotir ātmajyotir acañcalaḥ 
piṅgalaḥ kapilaśmaśruḥ śāstranetras trayītanuḥ ।। 

jñānaskandho mahājñānī nirutpattir upaplavaḥ 
bhago vivasvānādityo yogācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 

udārakīrtir udyogī sadyogī sadasanmayaḥ 
nakṣatramālī rākeśaḥ sādhiṣṭhānaḥ ṣaḍāśrayaḥ ।। 

pavitrapāṇiḥ pāpārir maṇipūro manogatiḥ 
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamāsīnaḥ śuklaḥ śānto vṛṣākapiḥ ।। 

viṣṇurgrahapatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ samartho anarthanāśanaḥ 
adharmaśatrurakṣayyaḥ puruhūtaḥ puruṣṭutaḥ ।। 

brahmagarbho bṛhadgarbho dharmadhenurdhanāgamaḥ 
jagaddhitaiṣī sugataḥ kumāraḥ kuśalāgamaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyavarṇo jyotiṣmān nānābhūtadharo dhvaniḥ 
arogo niyamādhyakṣo viśvāmitro dvijottamaḥ ।। 

bṛhajjyotiḥ sudhāmā ca mahājyotiranuttamaḥ 
mātāmaho mātariśvā nabhasvān nāgahāradhṛk ।। 

pulastyaḥ pulaho agastyo jātūkarṇyaḥ parāśaraḥ 
nirāvaraṇadharmajño viriñco viṣṭaraśravāḥ ।। 

ātmabhūr aniruddho atrijñānamūrtir mahāyaśāḥ 
lokacūḍāmaṇirvīraḥ caṇḍasatyaparākramaḥ ।। 

vyālakalpo mahākalpo mahāvṛkṣaḥ kalādharaḥ 
alaṃkariṣṇus tvacalo rociṣṇurvikramottamaḥ ।। 

āśuśabdapatirvegī plavanaḥ śikhisārathiḥ 
asaṃsṛṣṭo atithiḥ śakraḥ pramāthī pāpanāśanaḥ ।। 

vasuśravāḥ kavyavāhaḥ pratapto viśvabhojanaḥ 
jaryo jarādhiśamano lohitaś ca tanūnapāt ।। 

pṛṣadaśvo nabhoyoniḥ supratīkas tamisrahā 
nidāghastapano meghaḥ pakṣaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ ।। 

mukhānilaḥ suniṣpannaḥ surabhiḥ śiśirātmakaḥ 
vasaṃto mādhavo grīṣmo nabhasyo bījavāhanaḥ ।। 

aṅgirā munirātreyo vimalo viśvavāhanaḥ 
pāvanaḥ purujicchakras trividyo naravāhanaḥ ।। 

mano buddhirahaṅkāraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrapālakaḥ 
tejonidhir jñānanidhir vipāko vighnakārakaḥ ।। 

adharo anuttaro jñeyo jyeṣṭho niḥśreyasālayaḥ 
śailo nagastanurdeho dānavārirarindamaḥ ।। 

cārudhīr janakaścāruviśalyo lokaśalyakṛt 
caturvedaścaturbhāvaś caturaścaturapriyaḥ ।। 

āmnāyo atha samāmnāyas tīrthadevaśivālayaḥ 
bahurūpo mahārūpaḥ sarvarūpaś carācaraḥ ।। 

nyāyanirvāhako nyāyo nyāyagamyo nirañjanaḥ 
sahasramūrdhā devendraḥ sarvaśastraprabhañjanaḥ ।। 

muṇḍo virūpo vikṛto daṇḍī dānto guṇottamaḥ 
piṅgalākṣo atha haryakṣo nīlagrīvo nirāmayaḥ ।। 

sahasrabāhuḥ sarveśaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarvalokabhṛt 
padmāsanaḥ paraṃ jyotiḥ parāvaraṃ paraṃ phalam ।। 

padmagarbho mahāgarbho viśvagarbho vicakṣaṇaḥ 
parāvarajño bījeśaḥ sumukhaḥ sumahāsvanaḥ ।। 

devāsuragururdevo devāsuranamaskṛtaḥ 
devāsuramahāmātro devāsuramahāśrayaḥ ।। 

devādidevo devarṣidevāsuravarapradaḥ 
devāsureśvaro divyo devāsuramaheśvaraḥ ।। 

sarvadevamayo acintyo devatātmātmasaṃbhavaḥ 
īḍyo anīśaḥ suravyāghro devasiṃho divākaraḥ ।। 

vibudhāgravaraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvadevottamottamaḥ 
śivajñānarataḥ śrīmān śikhiśrīparvatapriyaḥ ।। 

jayastaṃbho viśiṣṭambho narasiṃhanipātanaḥ 
brahmacārī lokacārī dharmacārī dhanādhipaḥ ।। 

nandī nandīśvaro nagno nagnavratadharaḥ śuciḥ 
liṅgādhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣo yugādhyakṣo yugāvahaḥ ।। 

svavaśaḥ savaśaḥ svargaḥ svaraḥ svaramayasvanaḥ 
bījādhyakṣo bījakartā dhanakṛd dharmavardhanaḥ ।। 

daṃbho adambho mahādaṃbhaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ 
śmaśānanilayastiṣyaḥ seturapratimākṛtiḥ ।। 

lokottarasphuṭālokas tryaṃbako nāgabhūṣaṇaḥ 
andhakārirmakhadveṣī viṣṇukandharapātanaḥ ।। 

vītadoṣo akṣayaguṇo dakṣāriḥ pūṣadantahṛt 
dhūrjaṭiḥ khaṇḍaparaśuḥ sakalo niṣkalo anaghaḥ ।। 

ādhāraḥ sakalādhāraḥ pāṇḍurābho mṛḍo naṭaḥ 
pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ sukumāraḥ sulocanaḥ ।। 

sāmageyaḥ priyakaraḥ puṇyakīrtiranāmayaḥ 
manojavastīrthakaro jaṭilo jīviteśvaraḥ ।। 

jīvitāntakaro nityo vasuretā vasupriyaḥ 
sadgatiḥ satkṛtiḥ saktaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kalādharaḥ ।। 

mānī mānyo mahākālaḥ sadbhūtiḥ satparāyaṇaḥ 
candrasaṃjīvanaḥ śāstā lokagūḍho amarādhipaḥ ।। 

lokabandhurlokanāthaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtibhūṣaṇaḥ 
anapāyyakṣaraḥ kāntaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।। 

tejomayo dyutidharo lokamāyo agraṇīr aṇuḥ 
śucismitaḥ prasannātmā durjayo duratikramaḥ ।। 

jyotirmayo nirākāro jagannātho jaleśvaraḥ 
tumbavīṇī mahākāyo viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ ।। 

trilokātmā trilokeśaḥ śuddhaḥ śuddhī rathākṣajaḥ 
avyaktalakṣaṇo vyakto vyaktāvyakto viśāṃpatiḥ ।। 

varaśīlo varatulo māno mānadhano mayaḥ 
brahmā viṣṇuḥ prajāpālo haṃso haṃsagatiryamaḥ ।। 

vedhā dhātā vidhātā ca attā hartā caturmukhaḥ 
kailāsaśikharāvāsī sarvāvāsī satāṃ gatiḥ ।। 

hiraṇyagarbho hariṇaḥ puruṣaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitā 
bhūtālayo bhūtapatir bhūtido bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। 

saṃyogī yogavidbrahma brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇapriyaḥ 
devapriyo devanātho devajño devacintakaḥ ।। 

viṣamākṣaḥ kalādhyakṣo vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavardhanaḥ 
nirmado nirahaṅkāro nirmoho nirupadravaḥ ।। 

darpahā darpito dṛptaḥ sarvartuparivartakaḥ 
saptajihvaḥ sahasrārciḥ snigdhaḥ prakṛtidakṣiṇaḥ ।। 

bhūtabhavyabhavannāthaḥ prabhavo bhrāntināśanaḥ 
artho anartho mahākośaḥ parakāryaikapaṇḍitaḥ ।। 

niṣkaṇṭakaḥ kṛtānando nirvyājo vyājamardanaḥ 
sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyakīrtistambhakṛtāgamaḥ ।। 

akaṃpito guṇagrāhī naikātmā naikakarmakṛt 
suprītaḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukaro dakṣiṇo analaḥ ।। 

skandhaḥ skandhadharo dhuryaḥ prakaṭaḥ prītivardhanaḥ 
aparājitaḥ sarvasaho vidagdhaḥ sarvavāhanaḥ ।। 

adhṛtaḥ svadhṛtaḥ sādhyaḥ pūrvamūrtiryaśodharaḥ 
varāhaśṛṅgadhṛg vāyur balavān ekanāyakaḥ ।। 

śrutiprakāśaḥ śrutimān ekabandhur anekadhṛk 
śrīvallabhaśivārambhaḥ śāntabhadraḥ samañjasaḥ ।। 

bhūśayo bhūtikṛdbhūtir bhūṣaṇo bhūtavāhanaḥ 
akāyo bhaktakāyasthaḥ kālajñānī kalāvapuḥ ।। 

satyavratamahātyāgī niṣṭhāśāntiparāyaṇaḥ 
parārthavṛttir varado viviktaḥ śrutisāgaraḥ ।। 

anirviṇṇo guṇagrāhī kalaṅkāṅkaḥ kalaṅkahā 
svabhāvarudro madhyasthaḥ śatrughno madhyanāśakaḥ ।। 

śikhaṇḍī kavacī śūlī caṇḍī muṇḍī ca kuṇḍalī 
mekhalī kavacī khaḍgī māyī saṃsārasārathiḥ ।। 

amṛtyuḥ sarvadṛk siṃhas tejorāśir mahāmaṇiḥ 
asaṃkhyeyo aprameyātmā vīryavān kāryakovidaḥ ।। 

vedyo vedārthavidgoptā sarvācāro munīśvaraḥ 
anuttamo durādharṣo madhuraḥ priyadarśanaḥ ।। 

sureśaḥ śaraṇaṃ sarvaḥ śabdabrahma satāṃ gatiḥ 
kālabhakṣaḥ kalaṅkāriḥ kaṅkaṇīkṛtavāsukiḥ ।। 

maheṣvāso mahībhartā niṣkalaṅko viśṛṅkhalaḥ 
dyumaṇis taraṇir dhanyaḥ siddhidaḥ siddhisādhanaḥ ।। 

nivṛttaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ śilpo vyūḍhorasko mahābhujaḥ 
ekajyotir nirātaṅko naro nārāyaṇapriyaḥ ।। 

nirlepo niṣprapañcātmā nirvyagro vyagranāśanaḥ 
stavyastavapriyaḥ stotā vyāsamūrtiranākulaḥ ।। 

niravadyapadopāyo vidyārāśiravikramaḥ 
praśāntabuddhirakṣudraḥ kṣudrahā nityasundaraḥ ।। 

dhairyāgryadhuryo dhātrīśaḥ śākalyaḥ śarvarīpatiḥ 
paramārthagurur dṛṣṭir gurur āśritavatsalaḥ ।। 

raso rasajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasattvāvalaṃbanaḥ 
evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। 

snāpayāmāsa ca vibhuḥ pūjayāmāsa paṅkajaiḥ 
parīkṣārthaṃ hareḥ pūjākamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ ।। 

gopayāmāsa kamalaṃ tadaikaṃ bhuvaneśvaraḥ 
hṛtapuṣpo haristatra kimidaṃ tvabhyacintayat ।। 

jñātvā svanetramuddhṛtya sarvasattvāvalambanam 
pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum ।। 

tatastatra vibhurdṛṣṭvā tathābhūtaṃ haro harim 
tasmādavatatārāśu maṇḍalātpāvakasya ca ।। 

koṭibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam 
jvālāmālāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ bhayaṅkaram ।। 

śūlaṭaṅkagadācakrakuntapāśadharaṃ haram 
varādabhayahastaṃ ca dvīpicarmottarīyakam ।। 

itthaṃbhūtaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā bhavaṃ bhasmavibhūṣitam 
hṛṣṭo namaścakārāśu devadevaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। 

dudruvustaṃ parikramya sendrā devāstrilocanam 
cacāla brahmabhuvanaṃ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā ।। 

dadāha tejastacchaṃbhoḥ prāntaṃ vai śatayojanam 
adhastāccordhvataścaiva hāhetyakṛta bhūtale ।। 

tadā prāha mahādevaḥ prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ 
samprekṣya praṇayādviṣṇuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam ।। 

jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ janārdana 
sudarśanākhyaṃ cakraṃ ca dadāmi tava śobhanam ।। 

yadrūpaṃ bhavatā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaram 
hitāya tava yatnena tava bhāvāya suvrata ।। 

śāntaṃ raṇājire viṣṇo devānāṃ duḥkhasādhanam 
śāntasya cāstraṃ śāntaḥ syāc chāntenāstreṇa kiṃ phalam ।। 

śāntasya samare cāstraṃ śāntireva tapasvinām 
yoddhuḥ śāntyā balacchedaḥ parasya balavṛddhidaḥ ।। 

devairaśāntairyadrūpaṃ madīyaṃ bhāvayāvyayam 
kimāyudhena kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana ।। 

kṣamā yudhi na kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana 
anāgate vyatīte ca daurbalye svajanotkare ।। 

akālike tvadharme ca anarthe vārisūdana 
evamuktvā dadau cakraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham ।। 

netraṃ ca netā jagatāṃ prabhurvai padmasannibham 
tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhuḥ padmākṣamiti suvratam ।। 

dattvainaṃ nayanaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇave nīlalohitaḥ 
pasparśa ca karābhyāṃ vai suśubhābhyāmuvāca ha ।। 

varado ahaṃ varaśreṣṭha varānvaraya cepsitān 
bhaktyā vaśīkṛto nūnaṃ tvayāhaṃ puruṣottama ।। 

ityukto devadevena devadevaṃ praṇamya tam 
tvayi bhaktirmahādeva prasīda varamuttamam ।। 

nānyamicchāmi bhaktānām ārtayo nāsti yatprabho 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya dayāvān sutarāṃ bhavaḥ ।। 

pasparśa ca dadau tasmai śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ 
prāha caivaṃ mahādevaḥ paramātmānamacyutam ।। 

mayi bhaktaś ca vandyaś ca pūjyaścaiva surāsuraiḥ 
bhaviṣyasi na saṃdeho matprasādātsurottama ।। 

yadā satī dakṣaputrī vinindyaiva sulocanā 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ bhaviṣyati sureśvarī ।। 

divyā haimavatī viṣṇo tadā tvamapi suvrata 
bhaginīṃ tava kalyāṇīṃ devīṃ haimavatīmumām ।। 

niyogād brahmaṇaḥ sādhvīṃ pradāsyasi mamaiva tām 
matsaṃbandhī ca lokānāṃ madhye pūjyo bhaviṣyasi ।। 

māṃ divyena ca bhāvena tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaram 
drakṣyase ca prasannena mitrabhūtamivātmanā ।। 

ityuktvāntardadhe rudro bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ 
janārdano api bhagavān devānāmapi saṃnidhau ।। 

ayācata mahādevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ munibhiḥ samam 
mayā proktaṃ stavaṃ divyaṃ padmayone suśobhanam ।। 

yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān 
pratināmni hiraṇyasya tat tasya phalam āpnuyāt ।। 

aśvamedhasahasreṇa phalaṃ bhavati tasya vai 
ghṛtādyaiḥ snāpayedrudraṃ sthālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। 

nāmnāṃ sahasreṇānena śraddhayā śivamīśvaram 
so api yajñasahasrasya phalaṃ labdhvāsureśvaraiḥ ।। 

pūjyo bhavati rudrasya prītirbhavati tasya vai 
tathāstviti tathā prāha padmayonerjanārdanam ।। 

jagmatuḥ praṇipatyainaṃ devadevaṃ jagadgurum 
tasmānnāmnāṃ sahasreṇa pūjayed anagho dvijāḥ ।। 

japennāmnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sahasranāmabhiḥ pūjanād viṣṇucakralābho nāmāṣṭanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

saṃbhavaḥ sūcito devyās tvayā sūta mahāmate 
savistaraṃ vadasvādya satītve ca yathātatham ।। 

menājatvaṃ mahādevyā dakṣayajñavimardanam 
viṣṇunā ca kathaṃ dattā devadevāya śaṃbhave ।। 

kalyāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ tasya vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।। 

saṃbhavaṃ ca mahādevyāḥ prāha teṣāṃ mahātmanām 
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ daṇḍine tat suvistaram ।। 

yuṣmābhir vai kumārāya tena vyāsāya dhīmate 
tasmādahamupaśrutya pravadāmi suvistaram ।। 

vacanādvo mahābhāgāḥ praṇamyomāṃ tathā bhavam 
sā bhagākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅgamūrtestrivedikā ।। 

liṅgastu bhagavāndvābhyāṃ jagatsṛṣṭirdvijottamāḥ 
liṅgamūrtiḥ śivo jyotis tamasaścopari sthitaḥ ।। 

liṅgavedisamāyogād ardhanārīśvarobhavat 
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe devam agre putraṃ caturmukham ।। 

prāhiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānaṃ jñānamayo haraḥ 
viśvādhiko asau bhagavān ardhanārīśvaro vibhuḥ ।। 

hiraṇyagarbhaṃ taṃ devo jāyamānamapaśyata 
so api rudraṃ mahādevaṃ brahmāpaśyata śaṅkaram ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsthitaṃ devam ardhanārīśvaraṃ prabhum 
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ vārijodbhavaḥ ।। 

vibhajasveti viśveśaṃ viśvātmānamajo vibhuḥ 
sasarja devīṃ vāmāṅgāt patnīṃ caivātmanaḥ samām ।। 

śraddhā hyasya śubhā patnī tataḥ puṃsaḥ purātanī 
saivājñayā vibhordevī dakṣaputrī babhūva ha ।। 

satīsaṃjñā tadā sā vai rudramevāśritā patim 
dakṣaṃ vinindya kālena devī mainā hyabhūtpunaḥ ।। 

nāradasyaiva dakṣo api śāpādevaṃ vinindya ca 
avajñādurmado dakṣo devadevamumāpatim ।। 

anādṛtya kṛtiṃ jñātvā satī dakṣeṇa tatkṣaṇāt 
bhasmīkṛtvātmano dehaṃ yogamārgeṇa sā punaḥ ।। 

babhūva pārvatī devī tapasā ca gireḥ prabhoḥ 
jñātvaitadbhagavān bhargo dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

dakṣasya vipulaṃ yajñaṃ cyāvaner vacanādapi 
cyavanasya suto dhīmān dadhīca iti viśrutaḥ ।। 

vijitya viṣṇuṃ samare prasādāt tryaṃbakasya ca 
viṣṇunā lokapālāṃś ca śaśāpa ca munīśvaraḥ ।। 

rudrasya krodhajenaiva vahninā haviṣā surāḥ 
vināśo vai kṣaṇādeva māyayā śaṅkarasya vai ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devīsaṃbhavo nāma navanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ

vijitya viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ bhagavānparameśvaraḥ 
sarvāndadhīcavacanāt kathaṃ bheje maheśvaraḥ ।। 

dakṣayajñe suvipule devān viṣṇupurogamān 
dadāha bhagavān rudraḥ sarvān munigaṇān api ।। 

bhadro nāma gaṇastena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā 
viprayogena devyā vai duḥsahenaiva suvratāḥ ।। 

so asṛjad vīrabhadraś ca gaṇeśānromajāñchubhān 
gaṇeśvaraiḥ samāruhya rathaṃ bhadraḥ pratāpavān ।। 

gantuṃ cakre matiṃ yasya sārathirbhagavānajaḥ 
gaṇeśvarāś ca te sarve vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ ।। 

vimānairviśvato bhadrais tamanvayuratho surāḥ 
himavacchikhare ramye hemaśṛṅge suśobhane ।। 

yajñavāṭas tathā tasya gaṅgādvārasamīpataḥ 
taddeśe caiva vikhyātaṃ śubhaṃ kanakhalaṃ dvijāḥ ।। 

dagdhuṃ vai preṣitaścāsau bhagavān parameṣṭhinā 
tadotpāto babhūvātha lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsanaḥ ।। 

parvatāś ca vyaśīryanta pracakampe vasuṃdharā 
marutaś cāpy aghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ ।। 

agnayo naiva dīpyanti na ca dīpyati bhāskaraḥ 
grahāś ca na prakāśyante na devā na ca dānavāḥ ।। 

tataḥ kṣaṇāt praviśyaiva yajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ 
romajaiḥ sahito bhadraḥ kālāgnirivacāparaḥ ।। 

uvāca bhadro bhagavān dakṣaṃ cāmitatejasam 
saṃparkādeva dakṣādya munīndevān pinākinā ।। 

dagdhuṃ saṃpreṣitaś cāhaṃ bhavantaṃ samunīśvaraiḥ 
ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ ।। 

gaṇeśvarāś ca saṃkruddhā yūpānutpāṭya cikṣipuḥ 
prastotrā saha hotrā ca dagdhaṃ caiva gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।। 

gṛhītvā gaṇapāḥ sarvān gaṅgāsrotasi cikṣipuḥ 
vīrabhadro mahātejāḥ śakrasyodyacchataḥ karam ।। 

vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām 
bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā ।। 

nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaścaivaṃ nyapātayat 
tathā candramasaṃ devaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā ।। 

gharṣayāmāsa bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān 
cicheda ca śirastasya śakrasya bhagavānprabhoḥ ।। 

vahnerhastadvayaṃ chittvā jihvāmutpāṭya līlayā 
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ ।। 

yamasya daṇḍaṃ bhagavān pracicheda svayaṃ prabhuḥ 
jaghāna devamīśānaṃ triśūlena mahābalam ।। 

trayastriṃśatsurānevaṃ vinihatyāprayatnataḥ 
trayaś ca triśataṃ teṣāṃ trisāhasraṃ ca līlayā ।। 

trayaṃ caiva surendrāṇāṃ jaghāna ca munīśvarān 
anyāṃś ca devān devo asau sarvānyuddhāya saṃsthitān ।। 

jaghāna bhagavān rudraḥ khaḍgamuṣṭyādisāyakaiḥ 
atha viṣṇurmahātejāś cakram udyamya mūrchitaḥ ।। 

yuyodha bhagavāṃstena rudreṇa saha mādhavaḥ 
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam ।। 

viṣṇoryogabalāttasya divyadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।। 

śaṅkhacakragadāhastā asaṃkhyātāś ca jajñire 
tānsarvānapi devo asau nārāyaṇasamaprabhān ।। 

nihatya gadayā viṣṇuṃ tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani 
tataścorasi taṃ devaṃ līlayaiva raṇājire ।। 

papāta ca tadā bhūmau visaṃjñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
punarutthāya taṃ hantuṃ cakramudyamya sa prabhuḥ ।। 

krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān atiṣṭhat puruṣarṣabhaḥ 
tasya cakraṃ ca yadraudraṃ kālādityasamaprabham ।। 

vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā karasthaṃ na cacāla saḥ 
atiṣṭhat stambhitastena śṛṅgavāniva niścalaḥ ।। 

tribhiś ca dharṣitaṃ śārṅgaṃ tridhābhūtaṃ prabhostadā 
śārṅgakoṭiprasaṅgād vai cicheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ ।। 

chinnaṃ ca nipapātāsu śirastasya rasātale 
vāyunā preritaṃ caiva prāṇajena pinākinā ।। 

praviveśa tadā caiva tadīyāhavanīyakam 
tat pratidhvastakalaśaṃ bhagnayūpaṃ satoraṇam ।। 

pradīpitamahāśālaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajño api dudruve 
taṃ tadā mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ gaganaṃ prati ।। 

vīrabhadraḥ samādhāya viśiraskamathākarot 
tataḥ prajāpatiṃ dharmaṃ kaśyapaṃ ca jagadgurum ।। 

ariṣṭaneminaṃ vīro bahuputraṃ munīśvaram 
munim aṅgirasaṃ caiva kṛṣṇāśvaṃ ca mahābalaḥ ।। 

jaghāna mūrdhni pādena dakṣaṃ caiva yaśasvinam 
cicheda ca śirastasya dadāhāgnau dvijottamāḥ ।। 

sarasvatyāś ca nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca 
nikṛtya karajāgreṇa vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān ।। 

tasthau śriyā vṛto madhye pretasthāne yathā bhavaḥ 
etasminneva kāle tu bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

bhadramāha mahātejāḥ prārthayanpraṇataḥ prabhuḥ 
alaṃ krodhena vai bhadra naṣṭāścaiva divaukasaḥ ।। 

prasīda kṣamyatāṃ sarvaṃ romajaiḥ saha suvrata 
so api bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

śamaṃ jagāma śanakaiḥ śāntastasthau tadājñayā 
devo api tatra bhagavān antarikṣe vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। 

sagaṇaḥ sarvadaḥ śarvaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ 
prārthitaścaiva devena brahmaṇā bhagavān bhavaḥ ।। 

hatānāṃ ca tadā teṣāṃ pradadau pūrvavattanum 
indrasya ca śirastasya viṣṇoścaiva mahātmanaḥ ।। 

dakṣasya ca munīndrasya tathānyeṣāṃ maheśvaraḥ 
vāgīśyāścaiva nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca ।। 

naṣṭānāṃ jīvitaṃ caiva varāṇi vividhāni ca 
dakṣasya dhvastavaktrasya śirasā bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। 

kalpayāmāsa vai vaktraṃ līlayā ca mahān bhavaḥ 
dakṣo api labdhasaṃjñaś ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। 

tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam 
stutastena mahātejāḥ pradāya vividhānvarān ।। 

gāṇapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe 
devāś ca sarve deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram ।। 

nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ 
brahmā ca munayaḥ sarve pṛthakpṛthagajodbhavam ।। 

tuṣṭuvur devadeveśaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam 
tān devān anugṛhyaiva bhavo apyantaradhīyata ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivakṛddakṣayajñavidhvaṃsano nāma śatatamo adhyāyaḥ

kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī babhūvāṃbā satī śubhā 
kathaṃ vā devadeveśam avāpa patimīśvaram ।। 

sā menātanum āśritya svecchayaiva varāṅganā 
tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ ।। 

jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāś cakāra ca girīśvaraḥ 
dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā ।। 

tapastepe tayā sārdham anujā ca śubhānanā 
anyā ca devī hyanujā sarvaloke namaskṛtā ।। 

ṛṣayaś ca tadā sarve sarvalokamaheśvarīm 
tuṣṭuvus tapasā devīṃ samāvṛtya samantataḥ ।। 

jyeṣṭhā hyaparṇā hyanujā caikaparṇā śubhānanā 
tṛtīyā ca varārohā tathā caivaikapāṭalā ।। 

tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvaraḥ 
vaśīkṛto mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ ।। 

etasminneva kāle tu tārako nāma dānavaḥ 
tārātmajo mahātejā babhūva ditinandanaḥ ।। 

tasya putrāstrayaścāpi tārakākṣo mahāsuraḥ 
vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān ।। 

pitāmahas tathā caiṣāṃ tāro nāma mahābalaḥ 
tapasā labdhavīryaś ca prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ ।। 

so api tāro mahātejās trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
vijitya samare pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca jitavān asau ।। 

tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu divārātram aviśramam ।। 

sarathaṃ viṣṇumādāya cikṣepa śatayojanam 
tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। 

tāro varāñchataguṇaṃ labdhvā śataguṇaṃ balam 
pitāmahājjagatsarvam avāpa ditinandanaḥ ।। 

devendrapramukhāñjitvā devāndeveśvareśvaraḥ 
vārayāmāsa tair devān sarvalokeṣu māyayā ।। 

devatāś ca sahendreṇa tārakādbhayapīḍitāḥ 
na śāntiṃ lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇaṃ vā bhayārditāḥ ।। 

tadāmarapatiḥ śrīmān saṃnipatyāmaraprabhuḥ 
uvācāṅgirasaṃ devo devānāmapi saṃnidhau ।। 

bhagavaṃstārako nāma tārajo dānavottamaḥ 
tena saṃnihatā yuddhe vatsā gopatinā yathā ।। 

bhayāttasmānmahābhāga bṛhadyuddhe bṛhaspate 
aniketā bhramantyete śakuntā iva pañjare ।। 

asmākaṃ yāny amoghāni āyudhāny aṅgiro vara 
tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvādamaradviṣaḥ ।। 

daśavarṣasahasrāṇi dviguṇāni bṛhaspate 
viṣṇunā yodhito yuddhe tenāpi na ca sūditaḥ ।। 

yastenānirjito yuddhe viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā 
kathamasmadvidhastasya sthāsyate samare agrataḥ ।। 

evam uktas tu śakreṇa jīvaḥ sārdhaṃ surādhipaiḥ 
sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhuṃ samprāpyāha kuśadhvajam ।। 

so api tasya mukhācchrutvā praṇayātpraṇatārtihā 
devairaśeṣaiḥ sendraistu jīvamāha pitāmahaḥ ।। 

jāne vo artiṃ surendrāṇāṃ tathāpi śṛṇu sāṃpratam 
vinindya dakṣaṃ yā devī satī rudrāṅgasaṃbhavā ।। 

umā haimavatī jajñe sarvalokanamaskṛtā 
tasyāścaiveha rūpeṇa yūyaṃ devāḥ surottamāḥ ।। 

vibhoryatadhvamākraṣṭuṃ rudrasyāsya mano mahat 
tayoryogena sambhūtaḥ skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

ṣaḍāsyo dvādaśabhujaḥ senānīḥ pāvakiḥ prabhuḥ 
svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaś ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ ।। 

devaḥ śākho viśākhaś ca naigameśaś ca vīryavān 
senāpatiḥ kumārākhyaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ ।। 

līlayaiva mahāsenaḥ prabalaṃ tārakāsuram 
bālo api vinihatyaiko devān saṃtārayiṣyati ।। 

evam uktas tadā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā 
bṛhaspatis tathā sendrair devair devaṃ praṇamya tam ।। 

meroḥ śikharamāsādya smaraṃ sasmāra suvrataḥ 
smaraṇāddevadevasya smaro api saha bhāryayā ।। 

ratyā samaṃ samāgamya namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
saśakramāha taṃ jīvaṃ jagajjīvo dvijottamāḥ ।। 

smṛto yadbhavatā jīva samprāpto ahaṃ tavāntikam 
brūhi yanme vidhātavyaṃ tamāha surapūjitaḥ ।। 

tam āha bhagavāñchakraḥ saṃbhāvya makaradhvajam 
śaṅkareṇāṃbikāmadya saṃyojaya yathāsukham ।। 

tayā sa ramate yena bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ 
tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyānayā saha ।। 

so api tuṣṭo mahādevaḥ pradāsyati śubhāṃ gatim 
viprayuktastayā pūrvaṃ labdhvā tāṃ girijāmumām ।। 

evamukto namaskṛtya devadevaṃ śacīpatim 
devadevāśramaṃ gantuṃ matiṃ cakre tayā saha ।। 

gatvā tadāśraye śaṃbhoḥ saha ratyā mahābalaḥ 
vasaṃtena sahāyena devaṃ yoktumanā bhavat ।। 

tataḥ samprekṣya madanaṃ hasan devas triyaṃbakaḥ 
nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ tam avaikṣata ।। 

tato asya netrajo vahnir madanaṃ pārśvataḥ sthitam 
adahattatkṣaṇādeva lalāpa karuṇaṃ ratiḥ ।। 

ratyāḥ pralāpamākarṇya devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
kṛpayā parayā prāha kāmapatnīṃ nirīkṣya ca ।। 

amūrto api dhruvaṃ bhadre kāryaṃ sarvaṃ patistava 
ratikāle dhruve bhadre kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

yadā viṣṇuś ca bhavitā vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ 
śāpādbhṛgormahātejāḥ sarvalokahitāya vai ।। 

tadā tasya suto yaś ca sa patiste bhaviṣyati 
sā praṇamya tadā rudraṃ kāmapatnī śucismitā ।। 

jagāma madanaṃ labdhvā vasaṃtena samanvitā ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge madanadāho nāmaikādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyā vṛṣabhadhvaja 
prītiś ca bhagavāñcharvo vacanādbrahmaṇastadā ।। 

hitāya cāśramāṇāṃ ca krīḍārthaṃ bhagavānbhavaḥ 
tadā haimavatīṃ devīm upayeme yathāvidhi ।। 

jagāma sa svayaṃ brahmā marīcyādyairmaharṣibhiḥ 
tapovanaṃ mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tāṃ devīṃ sa jagato araṇīm 
kim arthaṃ tapasā lokān saṃtāpayasi śailaje ।। 

tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mātastvaṃ mā vināśaya 
tvaṃ hi saṃdhārayellokān imān sarvān svatejasā ।। 

sarvadeveśvaraḥ śrīmān sarvalokapatirbhavaḥ 
yasya vai devadevasya vayaṃ kiṅkaravādinaḥ ।। 

sa evaṃ parameśānaḥ svayaṃ ca varayiṣyati 
varade yena sṛṣṭāsi na vinā yastvayāṃbike ।। 

vartate nātra saṃdehas tava bharttā bhaviṣyati 
ityuktvā tāṃ namaskṛtya muhuḥ samprekṣya pārvatīm ।। 

gate pitāmahe devo bhagavān parameśvaraḥ 
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartuṃ dvijarūpeṇa cāśramam ।। 

sā ca dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ dvijarūpeṇa saṃsthitam 
pratibhādyaiḥ prabhuṃ jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। 

sampūjya varadaṃ devaṃ brāhmaṇacchadmanāgatam 
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ pārvatī parameśvaram ।। 

anugṛhya tadā devīm uvāca prahasanniva 
kuladharmāśrayaṃ rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 

krīḍārthaṃ ca satāṃ madhye sarvadevapatirbhavaḥ 
svayaṃvare mahādevī tava divyasuśobhane ।। 

āsthāya rūpaṃ yatsaumyaṃ sameṣye ahaṃ saha tvayā 
ityuktvā tāṃ samālokya devo divyena cakṣuṣā ।। 

jagāmeṣṭaṃ tadā divyaṃ svapuraṃ prayayau ca sā 
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastadā devīṃ menayā tuhinācalaḥ ।। 

āliṅgyāghrāya sampūjya putrīṃ sākṣāttapasvinīm 
duhiturdevadevena na jānannabhimantritam ।। 

svayaṃvaraṃ tadā devyāḥ sarvalokeṣvaghoṣayat 
atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ ।। 

śakraś ca bhagavān vahnir bhāskaro bhaga eva ca 
tvaṣṭāryamā vivasvāṃś ca yamo varuṇa eva ca ।। 

vāyuḥ somastatheśāno rudrāś ca munayas tathā 
aśvinau dvādaśādityā gandharvā garuḍas tathā ।। 

yakṣāḥ siddhāstathā sādhyā daityāḥ kiṃpuruṣoragāḥ 
samudrāś ca nadā vedā mantrāḥ stotrādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ ।। 

nāgāś ca parvatāḥ sarve yajñāḥ sūryādayo grahāḥ 
trayastriṃśacca devānāṃ trayaś ca triśataṃ tathā ।। 

trayaś ca trisahasraṃ ca tathānye bahavaḥ surā 
jagmur girīndraputryāstu svayaṃvaramanuttamam ।। 

atha śailasutā devī haimamāruhya śobhanam 
vimānaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtam ।। 

apsarobhiḥ pranṛttābhiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ 
gandharvasiddhairvividhaiḥ kinnaraiś ca suśobhanaiḥ ।। 

bandibhiḥ stūyamānā ca sthitā śailasutā tadā 
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśumiśritaṃ cāvahattathā ।। 

mālinī giriputryāstu saṃdhyā pūrṇendumaṇḍalam 
cāmarāsaktahastābhir divyastrībhiś ca saṃvṛtā ।। 

mālāṃ gṛhya jayā tasthau suradrumasamudbhavām 
vijayā vyajanaṃ gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpagā ।। 

mālāṃ pragṛhya devyāṃ tu sthitāyāṃ devasaṃsadi 
śiśurbhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। 

utsaṅgatalasaṃsupto babhūva bhagavānbhavaḥ 
atha dṛṣṭvā śiśuṃ devās tasyā utsaṃgavarttinam ।। 

ko ayam atreti saṃmantrya cukṣubhuś ca samāgatāḥ 
vajramāhārayattasya bāhum udyamya vṛtrahā ।। 

sa bāhurudyamastasya tathaiva samupasthitaḥ 
stambhitaḥ śiśurūpeṇa devadevena līlayā ।। 

vajraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhuṃ cālayituṃ tathā 
vahniḥ śaktiṃ tathā kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ ।। 

yamo api daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca nirṛtirmunipuṅgavāḥ 
varuṇo nāgapāśaṃ ca dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samīraṇaḥ ।। 

somo gadāṃ dhaneśaś ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍabhṛtāṃ varaḥ 
īśānaś ca tathā śūlaṃ tīvramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

rudrāś ca śūlamādityā muśalaṃ vasavas tathā 
mudgaraṃ stambhitāḥ sarve devenāśu divaukasaḥ ।। 

stambhitā devadevena tathānye ca divaukasaḥ 
śiraḥ prakampayan viṣṇuś cakram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ ।। 

tasyāpi śiraso bālaḥ sthiratvaṃ pracakāra ha 
cakraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhūṃścālayituṃ na ca ।। 

pūṣā dantān daśan dantair bālamaikṣata mohitaḥ
