tasyāpi daśanāḥ petur dṛṣṭamātrasya śaṃbhunā ।। 

balaṃ tejaś ca yogaṃ ca tathaivāstambhayad vibhuḥ 
atha teṣu sthiteṣveva manyumatsu sureṣvapi ।। 

brahmā paramasaṃvigno dhyānamāsthāya śaṅkaram 
bubudhe devamīśānam umotsaṃge tamāsthitam ।। 

sa buddhvā devamīśānaṃ śīghram utthāya vismitaḥ 
vavande caraṇau śaṃbhor astuvacca pitāmahaḥ ।। 

buddhistvaṃ sarvalokānām ahaṅkāras tvam īśvaraḥ 
bhūtānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca tvameveśa pravarttakaḥ ।। 

tavāhaṃ dakṣiṇāddhastāt sṛṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ purātanaḥ 
vāmahastān mahābāho devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

iyaṃ ca prakṛtirdevī sadā te sṛṣṭikāraṇa 
patnīrūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatkāraṇamāgatā ।। 

namastubhyaṃ mahādeva mahādevyai namonamaḥ 
prasādāttava deveśa niyogācca mayā prajāḥ ।। 

devādyāstu imāḥ sṛṣṭā mūḍhāstvadyogamohitāḥ 
kuru prasādameteṣāṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhavantvime ।। 

vijñāpyaivaṃ tadā brahmā devadevaṃ maheśvaram 
saṃstambhitāṃstadā tena bhagavān āha padmajaḥ ।। 

mūḍhāstha devatāḥ sarvā naiva budhyata śaṅkaram 
devadevam ihāyāntaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।। 

gacchadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ śīghraṃ devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ 
sanārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṅkaraṃ prabhum ।। 

sārdhaṃ mayaiva deveśaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram 
anayā haimavatyā ca prakṛtyā saha sattamam ।। 

tatra te stambhitāstena tathaiva surasattamāḥ 
praṇemur manasā sarve sanārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum ।। 

atha teṣāṃ prasanno bhūd devadevastriyaṃbakaḥ 
yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu vacanādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

tata evaṃ prasanne tu sarvadevanivāraṇam 
vapuścakāra deveśo divyaṃ paramamadbhutam ।। 

tejasā tasya devāste sendracandradivākarāḥ 
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sanārāyaṇakās tathā ।। 

sayamāś ca sarudrāś ca cakṣuraprārthayan vibhum 
tebhyaś ca paramaṃ cakṣuḥ sarvadṛṣṭau ca śaktimat ।। 

dadāvaṃbāpatiḥ śarvo bhavānyāś ca calasya ca 
labdhvā cakṣustadā devā indraviṣṇupurogamāḥ ।। 

sabrahmakaḥ saśakrāś ca tamapaśyanmaheśvaram 
brahmādyā nemire tūrṇaṃ bhavānī ca girīśvaraḥ ।। 

munayaś ca mahādevaṃ gaṇeśāḥ śivasaṃmatāḥ 
sasarjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।। 

devadundubhayo nedus tuṣṭuvurmunayaḥ prabhum 
jagurgandharvamukhyāś ca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। 

mumuhurgaṇapāḥ sarve mumodāṃbā ca pārvatī 
tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām ।। 

pādayoḥ sthāpayāmāsa mālāṃ divyāṃ sugandhinīm 
sādhu sādhviti samprocya tayā tatraiva cārcitam ।। 

saha devyā namaścakruḥ śirobhir bhūtalāśritaiḥ 
sarve sabrahmakā devāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāsvayaṃvaro nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

atha brahmā mahādevam abhivandya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ityuvāca maheśvaram ।। 

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
yatheṣṭamiti lokeśaṃ prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। 

udvāhārthaṃ maheśasya tatkṣaṇādeva suvratāḥ 
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ divyaṃ puraṃ ratnamayaṃ śubham ।। 

athāditirditiḥ sākṣād danuḥ kadruḥ sukālikā 
pulomā surasā caiva siṃhikā vinatā tathā ।। 

siddhirmāyā kriyā durgā devī sākṣātsudhā svadhā 
sāvitrī vedamātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ ।। 

svāhā svāhāmatir buddhir ṛddhir vṛddhiḥ sarasvatī 
rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumatī tathā ।। 

dharaṇī dhāraṇī celā śacī nārāyaṇī tathā 
etāścānyāś ca devānāṃ mātaraḥ patnayas tathā ।। 

udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti jagmuḥ sarvā mudānvitāḥ 
uragā garuḍā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kinnarā gaṇāḥ ।। 

sāgarā girayo meghā māsāḥ saṃvatsarās tathā 
vedā mantrās tathā yajñāḥ stomā dharmāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। 

huṅkāraḥ praṇavaścaiva pratihārāḥ sahasraśaḥ 
koṭirapsaraso divyās tāsāṃ ca paricārikāḥ ।। 

yāś ca sarveṣu dvīpeṣu devalokeṣu nimnagāḥ 
tāś ca strīvigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। 

gaṇapāś ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ 
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti tatrājagmurmudānvitāḥ ।। 

abhyayuḥ śaṅkhavarṇāś ca gaṇakoṭyo gaṇeśvarāḥ 
daśabhiḥ kekarākṣaś ca vidyuto aṣṭābhir eva ca ।। 

catuḥṣaṣṭyā viśākhāś ca navabhiḥ pārayātrikaḥ 
ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvāntakaḥ śrīmān tathaiva vikṛtānanaḥ ।। 

jvālākeśo dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhir gaṇapuṅgavaḥ 
saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubho aṣṭābhir eva ca ।। 

pañcabhiś ca kapālīśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ śubhaḥ 
koṭikoṭibhir eveha gaṇḍakaḥ kuṃbhakas tathā ।। 

viṣṭambho aṣṭābhir eveha gaṇapaḥ sarvasattamaḥ 
pippalaś ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaś ca tathā dvijāḥ ।। 

āveṣṭanas tathāṣṭābhiḥ saptabhiścandratāpanaḥ 
mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnāṃ gaṇapo vṛtaḥ ।। 

kuṇḍī dvādaśabhir vīras tathā parvatakaḥ śubhaḥ 
kālaś ca kālakaścaiva mahākālaḥ śatena vai ।। 

āgnikaḥ śatakoṭyā vai koṭyāgnimukha eva ca 
ādityamūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā caiva dhanāvahaḥ ।। 

saṃnāmaś ca śatenaiva kumudaḥ koṭibhis tathā 
amoghaḥ kokilaścaiva koṭikoṭyā sumantrakaḥ ।। 

kākapāṭo aparaḥ ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ prabhuḥ 
mahābalaś ca navabhir madhupiṅgaś ca piṅgalaḥ ।। 

nīlo navatyā deveśaḥ pūrṇabhadrastathaiva ca 
koṭīnāṃ caiva saptatyā caturvaktro mahābalaḥ ।। 

koṭikoṭisahasrāṇāṃ śatair viṃśatibhir vṛtāḥ 
tatrājagmus tathā devās te sarve śaṅkaraṃ bhavam ।। 

bhūtakoṭisahasreṇa pramathaḥ koṭibhistribhiḥ 
vīrabhadraścatuḥṣaṣṭyā romajāścaiva koṭibhiḥ ।। 

karaṇaścaiva viṃśatyā navatyā kevalaḥ śubhaḥ 
pañcākṣaḥ śatamanyuś ca meghamanyus tathaiva ca ।। 

kāṣṭhakūṭaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sukeśo vṛṣabhas tathā 
virūpākṣaś ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ ।। 

tāluketuḥ ṣaḍāsyaś ca pañcāsyaś ca sanātanaḥ 
saṃvartakas tathā caitro lakulīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। 

lokāntakaś ca dīptāsyas tathā daityāntakaḥ prabhuḥ 
mṛtyuhṛt kālahā kālo mṛtyuñjayakaras tathā ।। 

viṣādo viṣadaścaiva vidyutaḥ kāntakaḥ prabhuḥ 
devo bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadevapriyas tathā ।। 

aśanir bhāsakaś caiva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasrapāt 
ete cānye ca gaṇapā asaṃkhyātā mahābalāḥ ।। 

sarve sahasrahastāś ca jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ 
candrarekhāvataṃsāś ca nīlakaṇṭhās trilocanāḥ ।। 

hārakuṇḍalakeyūramukuṭādyair alaṃkṛtāḥ 
brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśā aṇimādiguṇairvṛtāḥ ।। 

sūryakoṭipratīkāśās tatrājagmurgaṇeśvarāḥ 
pātālacāriṇaścaiva sarvalokanivāsinaḥ ।। 

tuṃbarurnārado hāhā hūhūścaiva tu sāmagāḥ 
ratnānyādāya vādyāṃś ca tatrājagmustadā puram ।। 

ṛṣayaḥ kṛtsnaśastatra devagītāstapodhanāḥ 
puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān ajapur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। 

tata evaṃ pravṛtte tu sarvataś ca samāgame 
girijāṃ tām alaṃkṛtya svayameva śucismitām ।। 

puraṃ praveśayāmāsa svayam ādāya keśavaḥ 
sadasyāha ca deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamajo harim ।। 

bhavānagre samutpanno bhavānyā saha daivataiḥ 
vāmāṅgādasya rudrasya dakṣiṇāṅgādahaṃ prabho ।। 

manmūrtistuhinādrīśo yajñārthaṃ sṛṣṭa eva hi 
eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। 

śrautasmārtapravṛttyartham udvāhārtham ihāgataḥ 
ato asau jagatāṃ dhātrī dhātā tava mamāpi ca ।। 

asya devasya rudrasya mūrtibhir vihitaṃ jagat 
kṣmābagnikhendusūryātmapavanātmā yato bhavaḥ ।। 

tathāpi tasmai dātavyā vacanācca girermama 
eṣā hy ajā śuklakṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtirbhavān ।। 

śreyo api śailarājena saṃbandho ayaṃ tavāpi ca 
tava pādme samudbhūtaḥ kalpe nābhyaṃbujādaham ।। 

madaṃśasyāsya śailasya mamāpi ca gururbhavān 
bāḍham ityajam āhāsau devadevo janārdanaḥ ।। 

devāś ca munayaḥ sarve devadevaś ca śaṅkaraḥ 
tataścotthāya vidvānsaḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām ।। 

pādau prakṣālya devasya karābhyāṃ kamalekṣaṇaḥ 
abhyukṣad ātmano mūrdhni brahmaṇaś ca gires tathā ।। 

tvadīyaiṣā vivāhārthaṃ menajā hyanujā mama 
ityuktvā sodakaṃ dattvā devīṃ deveśvarāya tām ।। 

svātmānamapi devāya sodakaṃ pradadau hariḥ 
atha sarve muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavedārthapāragāḥ ।। 

ūcurdātā gṛhītā ca phalaṃ dravyaṃ vicārataḥ 
eṣa devo haro nūnaṃ māyayā hi tato jagat ।। 

ityuktvā taṃ praṇemuś ca prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ 
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।। 

devadundubhayo nedur nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ 
vedāś ca mūrtimantaste praṇemustaṃ maheśvaram ।। 

brahmaṇā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ devadevamumāpatim 
devo api devīmālokya salajjāṃ himaśailajām ।। 

na tṛpyatyanavadyāṅgī sā ca devaṃ vṛṣadhvajam 
varado asmīti taṃ prāha hariṃ so apyāha śaṅkaram ।। 

tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeti brahmākhyāṃ ca dadau tu saḥ 
tatastu punarevāha brahmā vijñāpayanprabhum ।। 

havirjuhomi vahnau tu upādhyāyapade sthitaḥ 
dadāsi mama yadyājñāṃ kartavyo hyakṛto vidhiḥ ।। 

tamāha śaṅkaro devaṃ devadevo jagatpatiḥ 
yadyadiṣṭaṃ suraśreṣṭha tatkuruṣva yathepsitam ।। 

kartāsmi vacanaṃ sarvaṃ devadeva pitāmaha 
tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭātmā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। 

hastaṃ devasya devyāś ca yuyoja paramaṃ prabhuḥ 
jvalanaś ca svayaṃ tatra kṛtāñjalirupasthitaḥ ।। 

śrautairetairmahāmantrair mūrtimadbhir upasthitaiḥ 
yathoktavidhinā hutvā lājānapi yathākramam ।। 

ānītānviṣṇunā viprān sampūjya vividhairvaraiḥ 
triś ca taṃ jvalanaṃ devaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam ।। 

muktvā hastasamāyogaṃ sahitaiḥ sarvadaivataiḥ 
suraiś ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। 

nanāma bhagavānbrahmā devadevamumāpatim 
tataḥ pādyaṃ tayor dattvā śaṃbhorācamanaṃ tathā ।। 

madhuparkaṃ tathā gāṃ ca praṇamya ca punaḥ śivam 
atiṣṭhadbhagavānbrahmā devairindrapurogamaiḥ ।। 

bhṛgvādyamunayaḥ sarve cākṣataistilataṇḍulaiḥ 
sūryādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvurvṛṣabhadhvajam ।। 

śivaḥ samāpya devoktaṃ vahnimāropya cātmani 
tayā samāgato rudraḥ sarvalokahitāya vai ।। 

yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi bhavodvāhaṃ śucismitaḥ 
śrāvayedvā dvijāñchuddhān vedavedāṅgapāragān ।। 

sa labdhvā gāṇapatyaṃ ca bhavena saha modate 
yatrāyaṃ kīrtyate viprais tāvadāste tadā bhavaḥ ।। 

tasmāt sampūjya vidhivat kīrtayennānyathā dvijāḥ 
udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

kīrtanīyamidaṃ sarvaṃ bhavodvāhamanuttamam 
kṛtodvāhastadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। 

sagaṇo nandinā sārdhaṃ sarvadevagaṇairvṛtaḥ 
purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ divyām ājagāma mahādyutiḥ ।। 

avimukte sukhāsīnaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam 
apṛcchatkṣetramāhātmyaṃ bhavānī harṣitānanā ।। 

athāhārdhendutilakaḥ kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam 
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ vistarācchakyate nahi ।। 

vaktuṃ mayā sureśāni ṛṣisaṃghābhipūjitam 
kiṃ mayā varṇyate devī hy avimuktaphalodayaḥ ।। 

pāpināṃ yatra muktiḥ syān mṛtānām ekajanmanā 
anyatra tu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vyapohati ।। 

vārāṇasyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paiśācyanarakāvaham 
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām ।। 

na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā 
yatra triviṣṭapo devo yatra viśveśvaro vibhuḥ ।। 

oṃkāreśaḥ kṛttivāsā mṛtānāṃ na punarbhavaḥ 
uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepācchaśiśekharaḥ ।। 

darśayāmāsa codyānaṃ parityajya gaṇeśvarān 
tatraiva bhagavān jāto gajavaktro vināyakaḥ ।। 

daityānāṃ vighnarūpārtham avighnāya divaukasām 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamuttamam ।। 

yathāśrutaṃ mayā sarvaṃ prasādādvaḥ suśobhanam ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pārvatīvivāhavarṇanaṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

kathaṃ vināyako jāto gajavaktro gaṇeśvaraḥ 
kathaṃ prabhāvastasyaivaṃ sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। 

etasminnantare devāḥ sendropendrāḥ sametya te 
dharmavighnaṃ tadā kartuṃ daityānāmabhavandvijāḥ ।। 

asurā yātudhānāś ca rākṣasāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ 
tāmasāś ca tathā cānye rājasāś ca tathā bhuvi ।। 

avighnaṃ yajñadānādyaiḥ samabhyarcya maheśvaram 
brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ viprā labdhepsitavarā yataḥ ।। 

tato asmākaṃ suraśreṣṭhāḥ sadā vijayasaṃbhavaḥ 
teṣāṃ tatastu vighnārtham avighnāya divaukasām ।। 

putrārthaṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasiddhaye 
vighneśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sraṣṭuṃ gaṇapaṃ stotumarhatha ।। 

ityuktvānyonyamanaghaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ śivamīśvaram 
namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ sarvajñāya pinākine ।। 

anaghāya viriñcāya devyāḥ kāryārthadāyine 
akāyāyārthakāyāya hareḥ kāyāpahāriṇe ।। 

kāyāntasthāmṛtādhāramaṇḍalāvasthitāya te 
kṛtādibhedakālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ ।। 

kālāgnirudrarūpāya dharmādyaṣṭapadāya ca 
kālīviśuddhadehāya kālikākāraṇāya te ।। 

kālakaṇṭhāya mukhyāya vāhanāya varāya te 
aṃbikāpataye tubhyaṃ hiraṇyapataye namaḥ ।। 

hiraṇyaretase caiva namaḥ śarvāya śūline 
kapāladaṇḍapāśāsicarmāṅkuśadharāya ca ।। 

pataye haimavatyāś ca hemaśuklāya te namaḥ 
pītaśuklāya rakṣārthaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavartmane ।। 

pañcamāya mahāpañcayajñināṃ phaladāya ca 
pañcāsyaphaṇihārāya pañcākṣaramayāya te ।। 

pañcadhā pañcakaivalyadevairarcitamūrtaye 
pañcākṣaradṛśe tubhyaṃ parātparatarāya te ।। 

ṣoḍaśasvaravajrāṅgavaktrāyākṣayarūpiṇe 
kādipañcakahastāya cādihastāya te namaḥ ।। 

ṭādipādāya rudrāya tādipādāya te namaḥ 
pādimeṇḍhrāya yadyaṅgadhātusaptakadhāriṇe ।। 

śāntātmarūpiṇe sākṣāt kṣadantakrodhine namaḥ 
lavarephahalāṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ ।। 

sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe 
bhruvor ante sadā sadbhir dṛṣṭāyātyantabhānave ।। 

bhānusomāgninetrāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe 
guṇatrayoparisthāya tīrthapādāya te namaḥ ।। 

tīrthatattvāya sārāya tasmādapi parāya te 
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedāya oṃkārāya namo namaḥ ।। 

oṅkāre trividhaṃ rūpam āsthāyoparivāsine 
pītāya kṛṣṇavarṇāya raktāyātyantatejase ।। 

sthānapañcakasaṃsthāya pañcadhāṇḍabahiḥ kramāt 
brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyaṃ kumārāya namonamaḥ ।। 

aṃbāyāḥ parameśāya sarvoparicarāya te 
mūlasūkṣmasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmāya te namaḥ ।। 

sarvasaṃkalpaśūnyāya sarvasmādrakṣitāya te 
ādimadhyāntaśūnyāya citsaṃsthāya namonamaḥ ।। 

yamāgnivāyurudrāṃbusomaśakraniśācaraiḥ 
diṅmukhe diṅmukhe nityaṃ sagaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te ।। 

sarveṣu sarvadā sarvamārge sampūjitāya te 
rudrāya rudranīlāya kadrudrāya pracetase 
maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te ।। 
atha śṛṇu bhagavan stavacchalena kathitamajendramukhaiḥ surāsureśaiḥ । 
makhamadanayamāgnidakṣayajñakṣapaṇavicitraviceṣṭitaṃ kṣamasva ।। 

yaḥ paṭhettu stavaṃ bhaktyā śakrāgnipramukhaiḥ suraiḥ 
kīrtitaṃ śrāvayedvidvān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devastutirnāma caturadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

yadā sthitāḥ sureśvarāḥ praṇamya caivamīśvaram 
tadāṃbikāpatir bhavaḥ pinākadhṛṅ maheśvaraḥ ।। 

dadau nirīkṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇād bhavaḥ sa tānsurottamān 
praṇemurādarāddharaṃ surā mudārdralocanāḥ ।। 

bhavaḥ sudhāmṛtopamair nirīkṣaṇairnirīkṣaṇāt 
tadāha bhadramastu vaḥ sureśvarān maheśvaraḥ ।। 

varārthamīśa vīkṣyate surā gṛhaṃ gatāstvime 
praṇamya cāha vākpatiḥ patiṃ nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ ।। 

suretarādibhiḥ sadā hy avighnamarthito bhavān 
samastakarmasiddhaye surāpakārakāribhiḥ ।। 

tataḥ prasīdatād bhavān suvighnakarmakāraṇam 
surāpakārakāriṇām ihaiṣa eva no varaḥ ।। 

tatastadā niśamya vai pinākadhṛk sureśvaraḥ 
gaṇeśvaraṃ sureśvaraṃ vapurdadhāra saḥ śivaḥ ।। 

gaṇeśvarāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sureśvarā maheśvaram 
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ bhavārttihāriṇaṃ śubham ।। 

ibhānanāśritaṃ varaṃ triśūlapāśadhāriṇam 
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ gajānanaṃ tadāṃbikā ।। 

daduḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ hi siddhā munīndrās tathā khecarā devasaṃghāstadānīm 
tadā tuṣṭuvuścaikadantaṃ sureśāḥ praṇemurgaṇeśaṃ maheśaṃ vitandrāḥ ।। 

tadā tayorvinirgataḥ subhairavaḥ sa mūrtimān 
sthito nanarta bālakaḥ samastamaṅgalālayaḥ ।। 

vicitravastrabhūṣaṇair alaṃkṛto gajānanaḥ 
maheśvarasya putrako abhivandya tātam ambikām ।। 

jātamātraṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakāra bhagavānbhavaḥ 
gajānanāya kṛtyāṃstu sarvānsarveśvaraḥ svayam ।। 

ādāya ca karābhyāṃ ca susukhābhyāṃ bhavaḥ svayam 
āliṅgyāghrāya mūrdhānaṃ mahādevo jagadguruḥ ।। 

tavāvatāro daityānāṃ vināśāya mamātmaja 
devānāmupakārārthaṃ dvijānāṃ brahmavādinām ।। 

yajñaś ca dakṣiṇāhīnaḥ kṛto yena mahītale 
tasya dharmasya vighnaṃ ca kuru svargapathe sthitaḥ ।। 

adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ vyākhyānaṃ karma eva ca 
yo anyāyataḥ karotyasmin tasya prāṇānsadā hara ।। 

varṇāccyutānāṃ nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ narapuṅgava 
svadharmarahitānāṃ ca prāṇānapahara prabho ।। 

yāḥ striyastvāṃ sadā kālaṃ puruṣāś ca vināyaka 
yajanti tāsāṃ teṣāṃ ca tvatsāmyaṃ dātumarhasi ।। 

tvaṃ bhaktān sarvayatnena rakṣa bālagaṇeśvara 
yauvanasthāṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca ihāmutra ca pūjitaḥ ।। 

jagattraye atra sarvatra tvaṃ hi vighnagaṇeśvaraḥ 
saṃpūjyo vandanīyaś ca bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

māṃ ca nārāyaṇaṃ vāpi brahmāṇam api putraka 
yajanti yajñairvā viprair agre pūjyo bhaviṣyasi ।। 

tvām anabhyarcya kalyāṇaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca laukikam 
kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। 

brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūdraiścaiva gajānana 
sampūjya sarvasiddhyarthaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। 

tvāṃ gandhapuṣpadhūpādyair anabhyarcya jagattraye 
devairapi tathānyaiś ca labdhavyaṃ nāsti kutracit ।। 

abhyarcayanti ye lokā mānavāstu vināyakam 
te cārcanīyāḥ śakrādyair bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

ajaṃ hariṃ ca māṃ vāpi śakramanyānsurānapi 
vighnair bādhayasi tvāṃ cen nārcayanti phalārthinaḥ ।। 

sasarja ca tadā vighnagaṇaṃ gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ 
gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ namaskṛtvāpy atiṣṭhattasya cāgrataḥ ।। 

tadā prabhṛti loke asmin pūjayanti gaṇeśvaram 
daityānāṃ dharmavighnaṃ ca cakārāsau gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। 

etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ skandāgrajasamudbhavam 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā sukhībhavet ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vināyakotpattirnāma pañcādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

nṛtyārambhaḥ kathaṃ śaṃbhoḥ kimarthaṃ vā yathātatham 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ śrutaḥ skandāgrajodbhavaḥ ।। 

dāruko asurasambhūtas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ 
sūdayāmāsa kālāgnir iva devāndvijottamān ।। 

dārukeṇa tadā devās tāḍitāḥ pīḍitā bhṛśam 
brahmāṇaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ kumāraṃ viṣṇumeva ca ।। 

yamamindramanuprāpya strīvadhya iti cāsuraḥ 
strīrūpadhāribhiḥ stutyair brahmādyairyudhi saṃsthitaiḥ ।। 

bādhitāstena te sarve brahmāṇaṃ prāpya vai dvijāḥ 
vijñāpya tasmai tatsarvaṃ tena sārdhamumāpatim ।। 

samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve pitāmahapurogamāḥ 
brahmā prāpya ca deveśaṃ praṇamya bahudhā nataḥ ।। 

dāruṇo bhagavāndāruḥ pūrvaṃ tena vinirjitāḥ 
nihatya dārukaṃ daityaṃ strīvadhyaṃ trātumarhasi ।। 

vijñaptiṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhaganetrahā 
devīmuvāca deveśo girijāṃ prahasanniva ।। 

bhavatīṃ prārthayāmyadya hitāya jagatāṃ śubhe 
vadhārthaṃ dārukasyāsya strīvadhyasya varānane ।। 

atha sā tasya vacanaṃ niśamya jagato araṇiḥ 
viveśa dehe devasya deveśī janmatatparā ।। 

ekenāṃśena deveśaṃ praviṣṭā devasattamam 
na viveda tadā brahmā devāścendrapurogamāḥ ।। 

girijāṃ pūrvavacchaṃbhor dṛṣṭvā pārśvasthitāṃ śubhām 
māyayā mohitastasyāḥ sarvajño api caturmukhaḥ ।। 

sā praviṣṭā tanuṃ tasya devadevasya pārvatī 
kaṇṭhasthena viṣeṇāsya tanuṃ cakre tadātmanaḥ ।। 

tāṃ ca jñātvā tathābhūtāṃ tṛtīyenekṣaṇena vai 
sasarja kālīṃ kāmāriḥ kālakaṇṭhīṃ kapardinīm ।। 

jātā yadā kālimakālakaṇṭhī jātā tadānīṃ vipulā jayaśrīḥ 
devetarāṇāmajayastvasiddhyā tuṣṭirbhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya ।। 

jātāṃ tadānīṃ surasiddhasaṃghā dṛṣṭvā bhayād dudruvur agnikalpām 
kālīṃ garālaṃkṛtakālakaṇṭhīm upendrapadmodbhavaśakramukhyāḥ ।। 

tathaiva jātaṃ nayanaṃ lalāṭe sitāṃśulekhā ca śirasyudagrā 
kaṇṭhe karālaṃ niśitaṃ triśūlaṃ kare karālaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇāni ।। 

sārdhaṃ divyāṃbarā devyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
siddhendrasiddhāś ca tathā piśācā jajñire punaḥ ।। 

ājñayā dārukaṃ tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvarī 
dānavaṃ sūdayāmāsa sūdayantaṃ surādhipān ।। 

saṃraṃbhātiprasaṃgād vai tasyāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat 
krodhāgninā ca viprendrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadāturam ।। 

bhavo api bālarūpeṇa śmaśāne pretasaṃkule 
ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodhāgniṃ pātum īśvaraḥ ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā bālamīśānaṃ māyayā tasya mohitā 
utthāpyāghrāya vakṣojaṃ stanaṃ sā pradadau dvijāḥ ।। 

stanajena tadā sārdhaṃ kopamasyāḥ papau punaḥ 
krodhenānena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ rakṣako abhavat ।। 

mūrtayo aṣṭau ca tasyāpi kṣetrapālasya dhīmataḥ 
evaṃ vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodhamūrchitā ।। 

kṛtamasyāḥ prasādārthaṃ devadevena tāṇḍavam 
saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvabhūtendraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā ।। 

pītvā nṛtyāmṛtaṃ śaṃbhor ākaṇṭhaṃ parameśvarī 
nanarta sā ca yoginyaḥ pretasthāne yathāsukham ।। 

tatra sabrahmakā devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samantataḥ 
praṇemustuṣṭuvuḥ kālīṃ punardevīṃ ca pārvatīm ।। 

evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ śūlinaḥ prabhoḥ 
yogānandena ca vibhos tāṇḍavaṃ ceti cāpare ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivatāṇḍavakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

puropamanyunā sūta gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt 
kṣīrārṇavaḥ kathaṃ labdho vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।। 

evaṃ kālīm upālabhya gate deve triyaṃbake 
upamanyuḥ samabhyarcya tapasā labdhavānphalam ।। 

upamanyuriti khyāto muniś ca dvijasattamāḥ 
kumāra iva tejasvī krīḍamāno yadṛcchayā ।। 

kadācit kṣīram alpaṃ ca pītavān mātulāśrame 
īrṣyayā mātulasuto hy apibat kṣīram uttamam ।। 

pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā provāca mātaram 
mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini ।। 

gavyaṃ kṣīram atisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ namāmyaham 
upalālitaivaṃ putreṇa putram āliṅgya sādaram ।। 

duḥkhitā vilalāpārtā smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ 
smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ kṣīram upamanyurapi dvijāḥ 
dehi dehīti tāmāha rodamāno mahādyutiḥ ।। 

uñchavṛttyārjitān bījān svayaṃ piṣṭvā ca sā tadā 
bījapiṣṭaṃ tadāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī ।। 

aihyehi mama putreti sāmapūrvaṃ tataḥ sutam 
āliṅgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ ।। 

pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrā dattaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ ।। 

duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha samprekṣyāghrāya mūrdhani 
saṃmārjya netre putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate ।। 

taṭinī ratnapūrṇāste svargapātālagocarāḥ 
bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāś ca ye śive ।। 

rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam 
na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ ।। 

bhavaprasādajaṃ sarvaṃ nānyadevaprasādajam 
anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca ।। 

kṣīraṃ tatra kuto asmākaṃ mahādevo na pūjitaḥ 
pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamudyamya vai suta ।। 

tadeva labhyaṃ nānyattu viṣṇumudyamya vā prabhum 
niśamya vacanaṃ mātur upamanyurmahādyutiḥ ।। 

bālo api mātaraṃ prāha praṇipatya tapasvinīm 
tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge mahādevo asti cetkvacit ।। 

cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham 
tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā sa tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame ।। 

tamāha mātā suśubhaṃ kurviti sutarāṃ sutam 
anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sudustaram ।। 

himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ 
tapasā tasya viprasya vidhūpitamabhūjjagat ।। 

praṇamyāhustu tatsarve haraye devasattamāḥ 
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ ।। 

kimidaṃ tviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ 
jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā ।। 

dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ 
bhagavan brāhmaṇaḥ kaścid upamanyuritiśrutaḥ ।। 

kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā taṃ nivāraya 
etasminnantare devaḥ pinākī parameśvaraḥ 
śakrarūpaṃ samāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tadā ।। 

atha jagāma munestu tapovanaṃ gajavareṇa sitena sadāśivaḥ 
saha surāsurasiddhamahoragair amararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ ।। 
sahaiva cāruhya tadā dvipaṃ taṃ pragṛhya vālavyajanaṃ vivasvān । 
vāmena śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa cānyena sitātapatram ।। 

rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ 
sitātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ ।। 

āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ 
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartum upamanyos tadāśramam ।। 

taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam 
praṇamya śirasā prāha munirmunivarāḥ svayam ।। 

pāvitaścāśramaścāyaṃ mama deveśvaraḥ svayam 
prāptaḥ śakro jagannātho bhagavānbhānunā prabhuḥ ।। 

evamuktvā sthitaṃ vīkṣya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ dvijam 
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ ।। 

tuṣṭo asmi te varaṃ brūhi tapasānena suvrata 
dadāmi cepsitān sarvān dhaumyāgraja mahāmate ।। 

evamuktastadā tena śakreṇa munisattamaḥ 
varayāmi śive bhaktim ityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। 

tato niśamya vacanaṃ muneḥ kupitavatprabhuḥ 
prāha savyagramīśānaḥ śakrarūpadharaḥ svayam ।। 

māṃ na jānāsi devarṣe devarājānamīśvaram 
trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।। 

madbhakto bhava viprarṣe māmevārcaya sarvadā 
dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam ।। 

tataḥ śakrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam 
upamanyuridaṃ prāha japan pañcākṣaraṃ śubham ।। 

manye śakrasya rūpeṇa nūnam atrāgataḥ svayam 
kartuṃ daityādhamaḥ kaścid dharmavighnaṃ ca nānyathā ।। 

tvayaiva kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavanindāratena vai 
prasaṃgāddevadevasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। 

bahunātra kimuktena mayādyānumitaṃ mahat 
bhavāntarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya tu ।। 

śrutvā nindāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva saṃtyajet 
svadehaṃ taṃ nihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

yo vācotpāṭayejjihvāṃ śivanindāratasya tu 
triḥ saptakulamuddhṛtya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

āstāṃ tāvanmamecchāyāḥ kṣīraṃ prati surādhamam 
nihatya tvāṃ śivāstreṇa tyajāmyetatkalevaram ।। 

purā mātrā tu kathitaṃ tathyameva na saṃśayaḥ 
pūrvajanmani cāsmābhir apūjita iti prabhuḥ ।। 

evamuktvā tu taṃ devam upamanyurabhītavat 
śakraṃ cakre matiṃ hantum atharvāstreṇa mantravit ।। 

bhasmādhārānmahātejā bhasmamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca 
atharvāstraṃ tatastasmai sasarja ca nanāda ca ।। 

dagdhuṃ svadeham āgneyīṃ dhyātvā vai dhāraṇāṃ tadā 
atiṣṭhacca mahātejāḥ śuṣkendhanamivāvyayaḥ ।। 

evaṃ vyavasite vipre bhagavānbhaganetrahā 
vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ ।। 

atharvāstraṃ tadā tasya saṃhṛtaṃ candrakeṇa tu 
kālāgnisadṛśaṃ cedaṃ niyogānnandinas tathā ।। 

svarūpameva bhagavān āsthāya parameśvaraḥ 
darśayāmāsa viprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam ।। 

kṣīradhārāsahasraṃ ca kṣīrodārṇavameva ca 
dadhyāderarṇavaṃ caiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca ।। 

phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaṃ tathā 
apūpagirayaścaiva tathātiṣṭhan samantataḥ ।। 

upamanyumuvāca sasmito bhagavānbandhujanaiḥ samāvṛtam 
girijām avalokya sasmitāṃ saghṛṇaṃ prekṣyatu taṃ tadā ghṛṇī ।। 

bhuṅkṣva bhogānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me ।
upamanyo mahābhāga tavāṃbaiṣā hi pārvatī ।। 

mayā putrīkṛto asyadya dattaḥ kṣīrodadhis tathā 
madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhnaścārṇava eva ca ।। 

ājyodanārṇavaścaiva phalalehyārṇavas tathā 
apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaḥ punaḥ ।। 

pitā tava mahādevaḥ pitā vai jagatāṃ mune 
mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātā na saṃśayaḥ ।। 

amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam 
varānvaraya dāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhya tam 
āghrāya mūrdhani vibhur dadau devyāstadā bhavaḥ ।। 

devī tanayamālokya dadau tasmai girīndrajā 
yogaiśvaryaṃ tadā tuṣṭā brahmavidyāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 

so api labdhvā varaṃ tasyāḥ kumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā 
tuṣṭāva ca mahādevaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā ।। 

varayāmāsa ca tadā vareṇyaṃ virajekṣaṇam 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

prasīda devadeveśa tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī 
śraddhā caiva mahādeva sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā ।। 

evamuktastadā tena prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ 
dattvepsitaṃ hi viprāya tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upamanyucaritaṃ nāma saptādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ

dṛṣṭo asau vāsudevena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā 
dhaumyāgrajastato labdhaṃ divyaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam ।। 

kathaṃ labdhaṃ tadā jñānaṃ tasmātkṛṣṇena dhīmatā 
vaktumarhasi tāṃ sūta kathāṃ pātakanāśinīm ।। 

svecchayā hyavatīrṇo api vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ 
nindayanneva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ ।। 

putrārthaṃ bhagavāṃstatra tapastaptuṃ jagāma ca 
āśramaṃ copamanyorvai dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taṃ munim ।। 

namaścakāra taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhaumyāgrajamaho dvijāḥ 
bahumānena vai kṛṣṇas triḥ kṛtvā vai pradakṣiṇam ।। 

tasyāvalokanādeva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ 
naṣṭameva malaṃ sarvaṃ kāyajaṃ karmmajaṃ tathā ।। 

bhasmanoddhūlanaṃ kṛtvā upamanyurmahādyutiḥ 
tamagniriti viprendrā vāyurityādibhiḥ kramāt ।। 

divyaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ pradadau prītamānasaḥ 
muneḥ prasādānmānyo asau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ ।। 

tapasā tvekavarṣānte dṛṣṭvā devaṃ maheśvaram 
sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyagraṃ labdhavānputramātmanaḥ ।। 

tadāprabhṛti taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ 
divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā ।। 

anyaṃ ca kathayiṣyāmi muktyarthaṃ prāṇināṃ sadā 
sauvarṇīṃ mekhalāṃ kṛtvā ādhāraṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam ।। 

sauvarṇaṃ piṇḍikaṃ cāpi vyajanaṃ daṇḍameva ca 
naraiḥ striyātha vā kāryaṃ maṣībhājanalekhanīm ।। 

kṣurāḥ kartarikā cāpi atha pātramathāpi vā 
pāśupatāya dātavyaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaiḥ ।। 

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vātha nivedayet 
ātmavittānusāreṇa yoginaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ ।। 

te sarve pāpanirmuktāḥ samastakulasaṃyutāḥ 
yānti rudrapadaṃ divyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। 

tasmādanena dānena gṛhastho mucyate bhavāt 
yogināṃ saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipraṃ prasīdati ।। 

rājyaṃ putraṃ dhanaṃ bhavyam aśvaṃ yānamathāpi vā 
sarvasvaṃ vāpi dātavyaṃ yadīcchenmokṣamuttamam ।। 

adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvaṃ sādhyaṃ prayatnataḥ 
bhavyaṃ pāśupataṃ nityaṃ saṃsārārṇavatārakam ।। 

etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepānna ca saṃśayaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। 

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge aṣṭottaraśatatamo adhyāyaḥ
